      *Place the scaffolding on the outside of the goalpost rows. Scaffolding to be built-up from ground level to the top of the bottom girder.*
    - 提供鍋爐左側與右側之進入途徑(上下設備)。
      *Provide access from both the left and right side of the boiler.*
- 在底部外殼板上鋪排膠合板。
  *Use and apply plywood on the bottom casing panels.*

    - 在鍋爐主鋼構門型架預組裝期間，準備膠合板用於保護底部外殼板。
      *Prepare the plywood panels (for protection of the bottom panels) during the pre-assembly of the goalpost rows for the boiler main steel.*
    - 為避免損壞鍋爐外殼板之襯板，請使用膠合板外殼板。在安裝底部外殼板時，同步安裝膠合板外殼板。
      *To avoid damaging of the boiler casing panels liner sheeting use plywood panels. Erect the plywood panels during erection of the bottom panels.*
    - 在對準與銲接工項期間，打開膠合板外殼板，但需儘可能使其彼此保持閉合。
      *Open the plywood panels during the fit-up and weld activities, but keep the panels as closed to each other as far as possible.*
    - 底部外殼板襯板上之膠合板需維持原位，直至施工階段結束。
      *Plywood on the bottom casing panels liner sheeting needs to be in place until the end of the construction phase.*
    - 在完成底部內部外殼後，修改膠合板，以便在後續安裝期間「保護地面」。
      *After finalizing the inside bottom casing, modify the plywood in such a way that the “floor is protected” during further erection.*
    - 為管路工項在膠合板上切割孔洞，並在相關管路安裝前保持孔洞閉合。
      *Cut holes in the plywood for piping activities and close the holes until the relevant piping is erected.*
    - 需檢查所安裝之膠合板是否符合安裝要求，並經製造商認可。
      *Plywood erected shall be checked for correct erection, acceptance by the manufacturer.*
- 施工架平台(外架) (底部外殼安裝後與側壁外殼安裝期間或之後)。
  *Elevated platform (after erection of the bottom casing and during or after the erection of the sidewall casing).*

    - 對於鍋爐內部，施工架工作平台 (人員吊籃) 對於安裝側邊外殼與銜接處之內部保溫非常有用。
      *An elevated working platform (man basket) on the inside of the boiler is useful for erection of internal insulation at the casing sidewall insulation field splices.*
    - 高架平台之安裝可在側壁外殼板安裝期間開始。
      *Erection of the elevated platforms can commence during sidewall casing panel erection.*
    - 高架平台應安裝在鍋爐兩側 (右側/左側)，以便沿著鍋爐側壁之完整長度與高度提供適當的入口。
      *Elevated platforms to be erected on both sides (right / left side) of the boiler in such a way that proper access along the complete length and height of the boiler sidewalls can be provided.*

##### 釋出後續工項 *Release subsequent activities*
- 順利完成本段落之工項後，即可釋出下列工項。
  *With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given:*

    - 底部銜接接縫之保溫與襯板。
      *Insulation and liner sheeting bottom field splices.*
    - 角鋼連接 (若適用)。
      *Angle bar connections (where applicable).*
    - 側壁外殼板之安裝
      *Erection casing sidewall panels*

##### 安裝 *Erection*
- 安裝、調整底部外殼板並進行定位銲。
  *Erect, fit and tack-weld the bottom casing panels.*

    - 安裝前，清除外殼穿透處之塑膠與保溫棉。使用小刀正確切割塑膠與保溫棉，切勿強行拉出。
      *Before erection, remove the plastic and insulation wool from the casing penetrations. Properly cut the plastic and wool using a knife. Do not pull it out using force.*
    - 首先在 HRSG 前部或後部側面安裝單一底部外殼板。
      *First erect a single bottom panel on the HRSG front or rear side.*
    - 將外殼板對準正確位置，並將 U 型鋼槽用螺栓鎖定至主樑。
      *Align the panel to the correct position and bolt the U-channels to the girders.*
    - 切勿從已對準之位置移動外殼板。
      *DO NOT MOVE THE PANEL from the aligned position.*
    - 安裝後續外殼板並對準至首個已安裝之外殼板，僅將 U 型鋼槽彼此用螺栓鎖定。
      *Erect and align the consecutive panels to the first erected panel bolting the U-channels to each other only.*
    - 切除底部外殼板上之內部保溫保護塑膠。
      *Cut away the internal insulation protection plastic from the bottom panels.*
    - 進行定位銲時，無需留間隙。視需求依據圖面使用墊片。
      *Fit and tack-weld the panels without gap. Use filler plates where required as per drawing.*
    - 進行定位銲期間，使用銲接毯覆蓋保溫棉以進行火花防護。
      *During tack-welding, cover the insulation wool using weld blankets for spark protection.*
    - 安裝其餘之螺栓與螺帽。偵測到螺栓孔錯位時，調整僅可在諮詢製造商後進行。
      *Erect the remaining bolts and nuts. When a misalignment of bolt holes is detected, adjustment can be made only after consultation with the manufacturer.*
    - 對於與 U 型鋼槽之連接，請使用錐形墊圈。
      *Use taper washers for the connection to the U-channels.*

##### 底部外殼板銲接 *Welding bottom panels*
- 銲接底部外殼板。
  *Weld the bottom casing panels*

    - 請依照圖面與 WPS 上之銲接細節或型式作業進行。
      *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.*
    - 外部銲縫均應為連續銲，外側不允許進行點銲。
      *All external welds shall be continuous, no stitch welds on the outside allowed.*
    - 僅允許在內部接縫上進行點銲，尺寸請參見圖面上之細節。
      *Stitch welds are only allowed on the inside joints, for dimensions see the details on drawings.*
    - 對於所有鋼槽末端，銲縫應為連續銲。
      *For all channel ends the welds shall be continuous.*
    - 銲接期間，使用銲接毯覆蓋保溫棉以進行火花防護。
      *During welding, cover the insulation wool using weld blankets for spark protection.*

#### 8.3.4. 側面壁板 *Side wall panels*

側面壁板之安裝描述為一般性，適用於所有側面壁板之安裝工作。
*The described erection for Side wall panels is set-up generally and applies for all Side wall panel erection works.*
在側面壁板安裝期間，可同時進行其他工項。
*Parallel to the erection of Side wall panels, other activities can be carried out.*
在外殼板安裝之前與期間，需提前準備一些工項。
*Before and during erection of the Side wall panels, some activities need to be prepared in advance.*


![[Pasted image 20260611092549.png]]![[Pasted image 20260611092558.png]]
安裝 Box 1 至 6 的下部側面壁板。
*Erect the lower side wall casing panels for box 1 ~ 6*

##### 準備工作與先決條件 *Preparations and preconditions*
- 前一段落提及之文件與程序需備妥並由權責單位進行審查。
  *The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).*
- 下列準備工作/工項需已完成，若適用則需在 FQP 中簽署同意。
  *The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.*
    - 主鋼構之安裝與對準。
      *Installation and alignment of main steel structure.*
    - 材料已接收並檢測其數量與品質 (OSD 報告)。
      *Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report).*
- 鍋爐「內部」之施工架。可改用吊籃或高空作業車。
  *Scaffolding for access to the boiler “inside”.*
    - 將施工架放置在主鋼構之「內部」。施工架需從地面高度搭建至頂部橫樑。
      *Place the scaffolding on the inside of the main steel structure. Scaffolding to be built-up from ground level to the top girder.*
    - 若無可用施工架，鍋爐內部之高架工作平台 (人員吊籃) 對於內部外殼銲接與安裝外殼側壁保溫現場銜接處之內部保溫非常有用。
      *When there is no scaffolding available, an elevated working platform (man basket) on the inside of the boiler can be useful for inside casing welding and erection of internal insulation at the casing sidewall insulation field splices.*
    - 高架平台之安裝可在側壁外殼板安裝期間開始。
      *Erection of the elevated platforms can commence during sidewall casing panel erection.*

##### 釋出後續工項 *Release subsequent activities*
- 順利完成本段落之工項後，即可釋出下列工項。
  *With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given:*
    - 銜接處之保溫與襯板。
      *Insulation and liner sheeting field splices.*
    - 角鋼連接 (若適用)。
      *Angle bar connections (where applicable).*

##### 安裝 *Erection*
- 安裝、調整側面壁板並進行定位銲。
  *Erect, fit and tack-weld the Side wall panels.*
    - 確認圖面上指示之安裝高程與公差。
      *Verify fit-up elevations and tolerances as indicated on the drawings.*
    - 銲接前，清除需要之塑膠與保溫棉。使用小刀正確切割塑膠與保溫棉，切勿強行拉出。
      *Before welding, remove the plastic and insulation wool where required. Properly cut the plastic and wool using a knife. Do not pull it out using force.*
    - 將外殼板對準正確位置。切勿從已對準之位置移動外殼板。
      *Align the panel to the correct position. Do not move the panel from the aligned position.*
    - 若兩個相鄰外殼板之間有銲接連接，則將後續外殼板對準至第一個已對準之外殼板。
      *In case of a welded connection between two adjacent panels erect and align the consecutive panels to the first aligned panel.*
    - 若兩個相鄰外殼板之間有 U 型鋼槽連接，在銲接前將兩個溝槽螺栓鎖定在一起。
      *In case of a UNP to UNP connection between two adjacent panels, bolt the two channels together prior to welding.*
    - 進行定位銲時，無需留間隙。視需求依據圖面使用墊片。
      *Fit and tack-weld the panels without gap. Use filler plates where required as per drawing.*
    - 進行定位銲期間，使用銲接毯覆蓋保溫棉以進行火花防護。
      *During tack-welding, cover the insulation wool using weld blankets for spark protection.*

##### 側面壁板銲接 *Welding Side wall panels*
- 當側面壁板已對準並確認最終位置正確後，銲接側面壁板現場銜接處。
  *When alignment and final position of the Side wall panels is achieved and verified for correctness, weld the Side wall panel field splices.*
    - 所有外部與內部銲縫均應為連續銲，不允許進行點銲。
      *All external and internal welds shall be continuous, no stitch welds are allowed.*
    - 對於所有鋼槽末端，銲縫應為連續銲。
      *For all channel ends the welds shall be continuous.*
    - 請依照圖面與 WPS 上之銲接細節或型式作業密切執行，因為這可能因位置而異 (例如：內部銲接、外部銲接或外殼板之密封銲)。
      *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS closely, as these may differ per location. (E.g. inside welding, outside welding or seal welding of panels).*
    - 進行銲接期間，使用銲接毯覆蓋保溫棉以進行火花防護。
      *During welding, cover the insulation wool using weld blankets for spark protection.*

##### 現場部件 *Field parts*
- 裝配並定位銲 tack-weld 所有必要之現場部件。
  *Fit up and tack-weld all necessary field parts.*
    - 外殼板現場部件可為填隙板filler plates、導板guide plates與加強板stiffener plates。識別圖面上指定之所有必要現場部件。
      *Field parts for the casing panels can be filler, guide and stiffener plates. Identify all required field parts as indicated on the drawings.*
    - 導板/加強板/U 型鋼槽之交叉與連接點，需使用正確的銲接準備進行安裝。
      *Cross- and connection points of guide plates / stiffeners / U-channels, need to be installed using the correct weld preparation.*
    - 依照現場部件圖面上之銲接地圖要求執行。
      *Follow the requirements of the weld typical on the field part drawings.*
    - 角落與現場銜接處之所有間隙必須使用填隙板 (6 毫米厚) 進行封閉 (密封銲)。
      *All gaps at corners and field splices have to be closed (seal welded), using filler plates (6 mm thick).*

##### 銲接外殼板現場部件 *Welding field parts casing panels*
- 銲接所有已組裝之現場部件。
  *Weld all fitted-up field parts.*
    - 遵循圖面上之銲接細節或型式。
      *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings.*
    - 所有外部銲縫均應為連續銲，外側不允許進行點銲。
      *All external welds shall be continuous, no stitch welds on the outside allowed.*
    - 千斤頂穿透處之蓋板除外(先不焊接)。這些蓋板只能在移除鏈條千斤頂後安裝。
      *Except for the cover plates for the penetrations of the header strand jacks. These can only be installed after removal of strand jacks.*

##### 品質管制 *Quality control*
- 依據適用之 FQP 與/或程序執行品質管制工項。
  *Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).*
    - 在銲接前檢查外殼板之對準、高程、尺寸與公差。
      *Check alignment, elevation and dimensions and tolerances of the casing panels before welding.*
    - 釋出並列出未完成項目清單 (若有)。
      *Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).*

#### 8.3.5. 上半部外殼板 (包含在鍋爐管束模組中) *Top wall casing panels (included in the boiler harp module)*

上半部外殼板與鍋爐管束模組一起實施並吊裝。
*The Top wall casing panels are implemented and lifted with the boiler harp modules.*
上半部外殼板應銲接氣密至頂部大樑之底部法蘭，側面壁板則通過角鋼與條鋼連接銲接，而各上半部外殼板之間之現場銜接處則使用 T 型鋼或條鋼封閉。
*The top wall casing panels are to be welded gastight to the bottom flanges of the top girders, the side wall panels by means of angle bar and strip connections and the field splice between each top casing panel is closed by means of a T-bar or strip.*
上述側面壁板之安裝工作描述一般適用於所有上半部外殼板之安裝工作。
*The described erection for Top wall casing panels is set-up generally and applies for all Top wall casing panel erection works.*
在上半部外殼板安裝期間，可同時進行其他工項。
*Parallel to the erection of Top wall casing panels, other activities can be carried out.*
在上半部外殼板安裝之前與期間，需提前準備一些工項。
*Before and during erection of the Top wall casing panels, some activities need to be prepared in advance.*


![[Pasted image 20260611092849.png]]
安裝 Box 1 至 6 的上部側壁外殼板。
*Erect the upper side wall casing panels for box 1 ~ 6.*

![[Pasted image 20260611093041.png]]
在鍋爐側壁區域安裝防屈曲加勁板與斜撐。
*Erect the buckling stiffeners and bracings at the boiler side wall area.*
##### 準備工作與先決條件 *Preparations and preconditions*
- 前一段落提及之文件與程序需備妥並由權責單位進行審查。
  *The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).*
- 下列準備工作/工項需已完成，若適用則需在 FQP 中簽署同意。
  *The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.*
    - 鍋爐管束模組之安裝與對準。
      *Installation and alignment of boiler harp modules.*
    - 材料已接收並檢測其數量與品質 (OSD 報告)。
      *Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report).*

##### 釋出後續工項 *Release subsequent activities*
- 順利完成本段落之工項後，即可釋出下列工項。
  *With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given:*
    - 門型架列填隙板。
      *Filler plates goal post rows*
    - 角鋼連接 (若適用)。
      *Angle bar connections (where applicable).*
    - 各上半部外殼板間之 T 型鋼或條鋼連接。
      *T-bar or strip connection between separate top casing panels*
    - 保溫與襯板現場銜接處。
      *Insulation and liner sheeting field splices.*

##### 安裝 *Erection*
- 安裝、調整上半部外殼板並進行定位銲。
  *Erect, fit and tack-weld the Top wall casing panels.*
    - 確認圖面上指示之安裝高程與公差。
      *Verify fit-up elevations and tolerances as indicated on the drawings.*
    - 銲接前，清除需要之塑膠與保溫棉。使用小刀正確切割塑膠與保溫棉，切勿強行拉出。
      *Before welding, remove the plastic and insulation wool where required. Properly cut the plastic and wool using a knife. Do not pull it out using force.*
    - 進行定位銲時，無需留間隙。視需求依據圖面使用墊片。
      *Fit and tack-weld the panels without gap. Use filler plates where required as per drawing.*
    - 進行定位銲期間，使用銲接毯覆蓋保溫棉以進行火花防護。
      *During tack-welding, cover the insulation wool using weld blankets for spark protection.*

##### 銲接上半部外殼板 *Welding Top wall casing panels*
- 當上半部外殼板已對準並確認最終位置正確後，銲接上半部外殼板現場銜接處。
  *When alignment and final position of the Top wall casing panels is achieved and verified for correctness, weld the Top wall casing panel field splices.*
    - 所有外部與內部銲縫均應為連續銲，不允許進行點銲。
      *All external and internal welds shall be continuous, no stitch welds are allowed.*
    - 對於所有鋼槽末端，銲縫應為連續銲。
      *For all channel ends the welds shall be continuous.*
    - 請依照圖面與 WPS 上之銲接細節或型式作業密切執行，因為這可能因位置而異 (例如：內部銲接、外部銲接或外殼板之密封銲)。
      *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS closely, as these may differ per location. (E.g. inside welding, outside welding or seal welding of panels).*
    - 進行銲接期間，使用銲接毯覆蓋保溫棉以進行火花防護。
      *During welding, cover the insulation wool using weld blankets for spark protection.*

##### 現場部件 *Field parts*
- 裝配並定位銲所有必要之現場部件。
  *Fit up and tack-weld all necessary field parts.*
    - 外殼板現場部件可為填隙板、導板與加強板。識別圖面上指定之所有必要現場部件。
      *Field parts for the casing panels can be filler, guide and stiffener plates. Identify all required field parts as indicated on the drawings.*
    - 導板/加強板/U 型鋼槽之交叉與連接點，需使用正確的銲接準備進行安裝。
      *Cross- and connection points of guide plates / stiffeners / U-channels, need to be installed using the correct weld preparation.*
    - 依照現場部件圖面上之銲接地圖要求執行。
      *Follow the requirements of the weld typical on the field part drawings.*
    - 角落與現場銜接處之所有間隙必須使用填隙板 (6 毫米厚) 進行封閉 (密封銲)。
      *All gaps at corners and field splices have to be closed (seal welded), using filler plates (6 mm thick).*

##### 銲接外殼板現場部件 *Welding field parts casing panels*
- 銲接所有已組裝之現場部件。
  *Weld all fitted-up field parts.*
    - 遵循圖面上之銲接細節或型式。
      *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings.*
    - 所有外部銲縫均應為連續銲，外側不允許進行點銲。
      *All external welds shall be continuous, no stitch welds on the outside allowed.*
    - 標頭鏈條千斤頂穿透處之蓋板除外。這些蓋板只能在移除鏈條千斤頂後安裝。
      *Except for the cover plates for the penetrations of the header strand jacks. These can only be installed after removal of strand jacks.*

##### 品質管制 *Quality control*
- 依據適用之 FQP 與/或程序執行品質管制工項。
  *Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).*
    - 在銲接前檢查外殼板之對準、高程、尺寸與公差。
      *Check alignment, elevation and dimensions and tolerances of the casing panels before welding.*
    - 釋出並列出未完成項目清單 (若有)。
      *Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).*

#### 8.3.6. 門型架列填隙板 *Filler plates goal post rows*

填隙板連接是用於填補熱回收鍋爐主鋼構各門型架列底部側，兩個相鄰側面外殼板之間所存在之間隙。
*Filler plate connections are the plates placed to fill the gap located at each goalpost row bottom side for the main steel structure boiler, between two adjacent sidewall panels.*

密封板連接用作填隙板，並在角鋼連接安裝完成後，於這些位置提供鍋爐煙道之氣密性。
*Sealing plate connections are used as filler plates and provide gas tightness in boiler duct at these locations, once the angle bar connections are erected.*

![[Pasted image 20260611093456.png]]
![[Pasted image 20260611093459.png]]![[Pasted image 20260611093537.png]]
在門型架立柱列上安裝填縫板，以確保外殼在這些位置的氣密性。
*Erect the filler plates on goal post rows in order to make the casing gas tight at this locations.*
##### 準備工作與預置條件 *Preparations and preconditions*
- 前一段落提及之文件與程序需備妥並由權責單位進行審查。
  *The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).*
- 下列準備工作/工項需已完成，若適用則需在 FQP 中簽署同意。
  *The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.*
    - 底部與側面壁外殼板之安裝。
      *Erection of bottom and side wall casing panels.*

##### 釋出後續工項 *Release subsequent activities*
- 順利完成本段落之工項後，即可釋出下列工項。
  *With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given:*
    - 角鋼連接。
      *Angle bar connections.*

##### 安裝 *Erection*
- 安裝、調整左側與右側各門型架列底部側、相鄰兩個側面外殼板之間之填隙板並進行定位銲。
  *Erect, fit and tack-weld the filler plates for each goalpost row bottom side, between two adjacent sidewall panels on the left and right side.*
    - 調整填隙板以在各門型架列之要求位置完全填補現有之間隙。
      *Fit the filler plates to fill the complete existing gap at the required locations for each goalpost row.*

##### 銲接填隙板連接 *Welding filler plate connections*
- 銲接填隙板連接。
  *Weld the filler plate connections.*
    - 依照圖面與 WPS 上之銲接細節或型式進行。
      *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.*
    - 銲接期間，使用銲接毯覆蓋保溫棉以進行火花防護。
      *During welding, cover the insulation wool using weld blankets for spark protection.*

##### 品質管制 *Quality control*
- 依據適用之 FQP 與/或程序執行品質管制工項。
  *Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).*

#### 8.3.7. 角鋼 / 扁鋼連接與 T 型鋼連接 (一般) *Angle/flat bar connections and T-bar connections (general)*

角鋼 / 扁鋼與 T 型鋼連接是用於轉角與直形外殼現場銜接處之連接。
*Angle / flat bar and T bar connections are the connections used at corner and straight casing field splices.*

角鋼 / 扁鋼連接在這些位置提供鍋爐煙道之氣密性與剛性。
*Angle / flat bar connections provide in boiler duct gas tightness and rigidness at these locations.*
![[Pasted image 20260611093858.png]]![[Pasted image 20260611093905.png]]
![[Pasted image 20260611093901.png]]![[Pasted image 20260611093907.png]]
![[Pasted image 20260611093920.png]]
安裝側壁板與底部板之間的角鋼 / 條板連接件。
*Erect the angle bar / strip connections between side wall panels and bottom panels.*
##### 準備工作與預置條件 *Preparations and preconditions*
- 前一段落提及之文件與程序需備妥並由權責單位進行審查。
  *The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).*
- 下列準備工作/工項需已完成，若適用則需在 FQP 中簽署同意。
  *The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.*
    - 後續外殼板之安裝。
      *Installation of subsequent casing panels.*
    - 材料已接收並檢測其數量與品質 (OSD 報告)。
      *Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report).*

##### 釋出後續工項 *Release subsequent activities*
- 順利完成本段落之工項後，即可釋出下列工項。
  *With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given:*
    - 外殼板之保溫與內襯板。
      *Insulation and liner sheeting casing panels.*

##### 安裝 *Erection*
- 在相關的現場銜接位置安裝、調整相關角鋼 / 扁鋼與 T 型鋼連接並進行定位銲。
  *Erect, fit and tack-weld the angle / flat bar and T-bar connections at the relevant field splice location.*
    - 將角鋼 / 扁鋼與 T 型鋼連接對齊外殼板，且不留間隙。
      *Align the angle / flat bar and T-bar connection to the casing panel without gap.*
    - 角鋼 / 扁鋼與 T 型鋼連接之橫斷面與連接點，需使用正確的銲接準備進行安裝。細節請參見圖面。
      *Angle / flat bar and T-bar connection cross sections and connection points need to be erected using the correct weld preparation. For details see the drawings.*

##### 銲接角鋼 / 扁鋼與 T 型鋼連接 *Welding angle/flat bar and T-bar connections*
- 銲接所有角鋼 / 扁鋼與 T 型鋼連接。
  *Weld all angle / flat bar and T-bar connections.*
    - 所有外部與內部銲縫均應為連續銲，不允許在外部進行點銲。
      *All external and internal welds shall be continuous, no stitch welds on the outside allowed.*
    - 依照圖面與 WPS 上之銲接細節或型式進行。
      *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.*
    - 銲接期間，使用銲接毯覆蓋保溫棉以進行火花防護。
      *During welding, cover the insulation wool using weld blankets for spark protection.*
 ![[Pasted image 20260624143351.png]]
##### 品質管制 *Quality control*
- 依據適用之 FQP 與/或程序執行品質管制工項。
  *Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).*
    - 銲接前檢查角鋼 / 扁鋼與 T 型鋼連接之組合。
      *Check fit-up of the angle / flat bar and T-bar connections before welding.*
    - 釋出，並列出內部保溫之未決項目清單 (若有)。
      *Release for internal insulation with a list of outstanding items (if any).*

#### 8.3.8. 鍋爐外殼內部保溫與內襯板 (一般) *Internal insulation and liner sheeting boiler casing (general)*

現場銜接處之內部保溫與內襯板安裝，可在各自之外殼板已安裝且轉角連接已完成後執行。安裝工作係基於「內部保溫與內襯板」章節。
*Installation of internal insulation and liner sheeting for field splices, can be performed after respective casing panels are installed and corner connections have been finished. The installation is based on chapter “Internal insulation and liner sheeting”.*

##### 安裝 *Erection*
- 關於外殼內部保溫與內襯板之安裝，請遵循「內部保溫與內襯板」章節中所規定的步驟與要求。
  *For casing internal insulation and liner sheeting erection, follow the steps and requirements stipulated in chapter “Internal insulation and liner sheeting”.*

##### 品質管制 *Quality control*
- 依據適用之 FQP 與/或程序執行品質管制工項。
  *Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).*
    - 釋出，並列出未決項目清單 (若有)。
      *Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).*
    - 內部保溫與內襯板之品質管制係基於第 7.3 節：「內部保溫與內襯板」。
      *Quality control for the internal insulation and liner sheeting is based on chapter 7.3:“Internal insulation and liner sheeting”.*

### 8.4. 次鋼構組件 *Secondary steel components*

本段落描述次鋼構組件之吊裝。
*This paragraph describes the erection of the secondary steel components.*

#### 8.4.1. 一般 *General*

次鋼構組件之安裝係基於第 13 章「次鋼構」之說明。
*Erection of the secondary steel components is based on the description in chapter 13 “Secondary steel”*

施工方法說明書 / 風險評估以及次鋼構組件安裝之吊裝計畫應由安裝承包商準備。
*Work method statements / risk assessments with lifting plans for the erection of the secondary steel components shall be prepared by the erection contractor.*

次鋼構組件之吊裝順序示於文件 60031-730-05-001。
*The erection sequence for the secondary steel components is shown in document 60031-730-05-001.*

#### 8.4.2. 鍋爐頂部平台安裝 (部分) *Erection of Boiler top platforms (partly)*

在開始頂部平台之安裝之前，需提前準備一些工項。
*Before erection of the top platforms can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance.*
![[Pasted image 20260611100438.png]]![[Pasted image 20260611100448.png]]
為了能夠順利進入鍋爐頂部，請確認安裝樓梯與（部分）頂部平台的可能性。
請確保已安裝的平台部分不會妨礙後期模組的安裝。
*In order to get good accessebility to the top of the boiler verify the possibility to erec the staircase and the top platforms (partly). Make sure that the erected platforms parts will not hinder the erection of modules in the later stage.*

##### 準備工作與預置條件 *Preparations and preconditions*
- 參考平台部件之位置，評估在吊裝模組之前可以安裝那些頂部平台部分。
  *Verify the possibility of which parts of the top platform can be erected before loading modules with reference to the locations of the platform parts.*
- 前一段落提及之文件與程序需備妥並由權責單位進行審查。
  *The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).*
- 下列準備工作/工項需已完成，若適用則需在 FQP 中簽署同意。
  *The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.*
    - 次鋼構組件之預製。
      *Pre-fabrication secondary steel components.*
    - 主鋼構安裝完成。
      *Main steel erected.*

##### 安裝 *Erection*
- 僅在門型架列之右側與左側吊裝預先組裝之平台。鍋爐前部與後部側之頂部平台將於入口與出口煙道吊裝後進行安裝。
  *Erect the pre-assembled platforms only at the right and left side of the goalpost rows. The top platforms at the front and rear side of the boiler will be erected, after erection of the inlet and outlet duct.*
    - 與所有涉及 / 受影響之各方密切協調在此階段吊裝之頂部平台的確切位置與安裝。
      *With all involved / affected parties properly coordinate the exact location and erection of the top platforms erected at this stage.*

#### 8.4.3. 鍋爐樓梯 *Boiler staircase*

![[Pasted image 20260611100438.png]]![[Pasted image 20260611100443.png]]

為了能夠順利進入鍋爐頂部，請確認安裝樓梯與（部分）頂部平台的可能性。
請確保已安裝的平台部分不會妨礙後期模組的安裝。
*In order to get good accessebility to the top of the boiler verify the possibility to erec the staircase and the top platforms (partly). Make sure that the erected platforms parts will not hinder the erection of modules in the later stage.*

在開始頂部平台之安裝之前，需提前準備一些工項。
*Before erection of the top platforms can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance.*

##### 準備工作與預置條件 *Preparations and preconditions*
- 前一段落提及之文件與程序需備妥並由權責單位進行審查。
  *The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).*
- 下列準備工作/工項需已完成，若適用則需在 FQP 中簽署同意。
  *The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.*
    - 次鋼構組件之預製。
      *Pre-fabrication secondary steel components.*

##### 安裝 *Erection*
- 將已預先組裝之樓梯部分吊裝至最終位置。
  *Lift the already pre-assembled staircase parts into final position.*
- 安裝時請遵循第 13 章「次鋼構」中規定的安裝步驟與要求。
  *For erection follow the erection steps and requirements stipulated in the chapter 13“Secondary steel”.*
    - 根據適用之施工方法說明書 (WMS) 指示執行吊裝作業。
      *Execute the lifting works according the applicable WMS instructions.*

##### 品質管制 *Quality control*
- 依據適用之 FQP 與/或程序執行品質管制工項。
  *Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).*
    - 釋出，且無任何未決項目。
      *Release without any outstanding items.*

### 8.5. 橫向緩衝器 *Transverse bumpers*

本段落描述橫向緩衝器之安裝。
*This paragraph describes the erection of the transverse bumpers.*
![[Pasted image 20260611094427.png]]
![[Pasted image 20260611094443.png]]

![[Pasted image 20260611100107.png]]![[Pasted image 20260611100110.png]]
![[Pasted image 20260611100117.png]]

吊裝所有軸線的橫向緩衝器（F 軸除外）。
*Erect the transverse bumpers for all axes, except axis f.*
安裝 (D 軸)緩衝器之間的連接件。此階段尚不需要緩衝器墊片。
*Install the connections between the bumpers (axis d). Bumper shim plates will not be required in this stage.*

#### 8.5.1. 一般 *General*

施工方法說明書 / 風險評估以及橫向緩衝器安裝之吊裝計畫應由安裝承包商準備。
*Work method statements / risk assessments with lifting plans for the erection of the transverse bumpers shall be prepared by the erection contractor.*

橫向緩衝器之吊裝順序示於文件 60031-730-05-001。
*The erection sequence for the transverse bumpers is shown in document 60031-730-05-001.*

#### 8.5.2. 文件與程序 *Documents and procedures*

- 橫向緩衝器安裝所需之文件與程序：
  *Documents and procedures required for erection of the transverse bumpers.*

    - 施工方法說明書：安裝橫向緩衝器。
      *Work method statement : Erection transverse bumpers.*
    - 施工品質計畫書：熱回收鍋爐模組。
      *FQP : HRSG boiler modules.*
    - 銲接作業程序書 / 銲接程序資格檢定紀錄 / 銲工資格檢定：非受壓組件。
      *WPS / PQR / WPQ : Non-pressure parts.*
    - 銲接地圖 / 紀錄：非受壓組件。
      *Weld typical / record : Non-pressure parts.*
    - 銲接耗材處理程序書：非受壓組件。
      *Welding consumable handling procedure : Non-pressure parts.*
    - 非破壞檢測程序書 / 人員資格認證：非受壓組件。
      *NDE procedures / personnel qualifications : Non-pressure parts.*

#### 8.5.3. 橫向緩衝器每列安裝 *Transverse bumper erection per row*

在開始橫向緩衝器之安裝之前，需提前準備一些工項。
*Before erection of the transverse bumpers can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance.*

##### 準備工作與先決條件 *Preparations and preconditions*
- 前一段落提及之文件與程序需備妥並由權責單位進行審查。
  *The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).*
- 下列準備工作/工項需已完成，若適用則需在 FQP 中簽署同意。
  *The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.*
    - 材料已接收並檢測其數量與品質 (OSD 報告)。
      *Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report)*
	- 緩衝器與支撐 (Bumpers and supports)
	    - 橫向緩衝器配置在每列上，如圖面所示。
	      *Transverse bumpers are positioned on each row as indicated on the drawings.*
	    - 每列之橫向緩衝器與相應之導板皆有編號及材料組別標記指示。
	      *Transverse bumpers and the corresponding guide plates are indicated by numbering and material group marking, for each row.*
	    - 檢查緩衝器支撐之位置與水平度是否正確。
	      *Check the bumper supports for correct position and level*
	    - 確認每個位置之緩衝器編號與材料標記組別是否正確。
	      *Verify having the correct bumper number and material marking group for each position.*
	    - 將每列之緩衝器（包括導板）一同存放。
	      *Store the bumpers, including the guide plates together for each row.*
	    - 若緩衝器準備工作有任何偏差，請聯繫製造商。
	      *In case of any deviation regarding the bumper preparation, contact the manufacturer.*

##### 釋出後續工項 *Release subsequent activities*
- 順利完成本段落之工項後，即可釋出下列工項。
  *With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given:*
    - 模組安裝。
      *Module erection.*
    - 導流板與密封板之臨時存放。
      *Temporary storage of baffles and sealing plates*

##### 安裝每一列的橫向緩衝器 *Erection transverse bumpers per row*
- 安裝橫向緩衝器。
  *Erect the transverse bumpers.*
    - 從每列最低的橫向緩衝器開始安裝，並在該列由下至上持續安裝。安裝該列之所有緩衝器。
      *Start with the erection of the lowest transverse bumper for each row and continue the erection from top to bottom for that row. Erect all bumpers per row.*
    - 安裝緩衝器後，調整相應之緩衝器至正確位置。
      *After erection of a bumper adjust respective bumper for correct position.*
    - 在開始安裝下一個緩衝器之前，先完成前一個緩衝器，以避免在安裝過程中發生意外。
      *Finalize each bumper as described before starting with the next bumper, this to avoid accidents during the erection.*
    - 在緩衝器支撐與緩衝器之間保持自由間隙。橫向緩衝器應調整至緩衝器支撐之間的正確位置。每列所需之自由間隙（以 "A" 表示）如圖面所示。
      *Maintain a free gap between the bumper support and the bumper. Transverse bumpers are to be adjusted to the correct location between the bumper supports. For each row, the free gap (indicated with “A”) required is indicated on the drawing.*
    - 一旦定位，緩衝器應在整個表面上與緩衝器支撐接觸。
      *Once positioned, the bumper shall touch the bumper support over the complete surface.*
    - 若有任何偏差，請聯繫製造商。
      *In case of any deviation contact the manufacturer.*
- 安裝緩衝器兩端之導板。
  *Erect the guide plate at both bumper ends.*
    - 導板僅能銲接至緩衝器。
      *Weld the bumper guide to the bumper only.*

##### 銲接導板 *Welding guide plate*
- 銲接導板。
  *Weld the guide plate.*
    - 依照圖面與 WPS 之銲接細節或型式進行。
      *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS..*

##### 品質管制 *Quality control*
- 依據適用之 FQP 與/或程序執行品質管制工項。
  *Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).*
    - 應確認圖面上提及之自由間隙 "A"。確認導板未銲接至緩衝器支撐。
      *The free gap “A” mentioned on the drawings shall be verified. Verify that the guide plate is not welded to the bumper support*
    - 無任何未決項目即可釋出。
      *Release without a list of outstanding items.*
    - 製造商應依據適用之公差圖面 60031-730-06-系列，審查緩衝器端部與內襯板之間間隙之實際量測報告。
      *Manufacturer shall review the actual survey report of the gap between the bumper ends and inner liner sheeting according the applicable tolerance drawings.*

#### 8.5.4. 橫向緩衝器之最終檢查 *Final inspection of the transverse bumpers*

當特定系統或一組特定組件之機械安裝完成後，應進行檢查。未完成項目應彙整於未完成項目清單中，並附於最終檢查合格證上。
*When the mechanical erection of a certain system, or group of specific components is finalized these shall be inspected. Outstanding items shall be collected in an outstanding items list and attached to the Final inspection Certificate.*

橫向緩衝器之最終檢查合格書描述了所檢查之系統或組件。
*The Final inspection Certificate of the transverse bumpers describes the systems or components inspected.*

##### 檢查 *Inspection*
- 最終檢查合格書上提及之所有系統或特定組件組應進行正確安裝、完整性與損壞之最終檢查。
  *All systems or group of specific components referred to on the Final inspection Certificate shall have a final inspection for correct erection, completeness and damages.*
- 在步行檢視後應立即建立未完成項目紀錄（如有）。
  *A record of outstanding items (if any) shall be set-up directly after the walk-down.*
- 若有未完成項目清單適用，其應分類為：
  *In case a list of outstanding items is applicable it shall be categorized in :*
    - 於水壓試驗前需解決之項目（A 級項目）
      *Items to be solved before hydro testing (A-items)*
    - 於熱試運轉前需解決之項目（B 級項目）
      *Items to be solved before hot-commissioning (B-items)*
    - 於初期驗收前需解決之項目（C 級項目）
      *Items to be solved before provisional acceptance (PAC) (C-items)*
- 確認所涉及系統之適用現場 FQP 已由所有涉入方簽署同意。未完成項目應納入未決點清單。
  *Verify that the applicable site FQPs for the systems involved are signed off by all parties involved. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list*
- 確認所有不符合事項報告已關閉。未完成項目應納入未決點清單。
  *Verify that all Non-Conformity Reports are closed. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list*

### 8.6. 鍋爐主鋼構門型架列無收縮水泥灌漿 *Grouting goalpost rows main steel structure boiler*

灌漿之安裝係基於第 7.2 節之說明。
*Grouting erection is based on paragraph 7.2.*

![[Pasted image 20260611100822.png]]
![[Pasted image 20260611100749.png]]![[Pasted image 20260611100752.png]]
在所有門型架對位完成後，進行主鋼結構底板的灌漿作業。
*After alignment of all portals, perform grouting of the base plates main steel structure.*

#### 8.6.1. 無收縮水泥灌漿 *Grouting*

在開始澆置無收縮水泥灌漿之前，需提前準備一些工項。
*Before pouring of the grouting can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance.*

##### 準備工作與先決條件 *Preparations and preconditions*
- 模板及混凝土之鑿毛需提前準備。
  *Formwork and chipping of the concrete is to be prepared in advance.*
- 下列準備工作/工項需已完成，若適用則需在 FQP 中簽署同意。
  *The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.*
    - 底部與側面外殼板已吊裝。
      *Bottom and sidewall casing panels erected.*
    - 橫向緩衝器已安裝。
      *Transvers bumpers erected*

##### 釋出後續工項 *Release subsequent activities*
- 順利完成本段落之工項後，即可釋出下列工項。
  *With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given:*
    - 模組安裝。
      *Erection of Modules.*

##### 安裝 *Erection*
- 依據無收縮水泥灌漿程序書第 7.2 節澆置無收縮水泥灌漿。
  *Pour the grouting according the grouting procedure, paragraph 7.2*

### 8.7. 模組吊裝 *Module erection*

本段落描述模組之安裝。
*This paragraph describes the erection of the Modules.*

#### 8.7.1. 一般 *General*

模組安裝是一個包含數個相互連結之準備與安裝工項的安裝順序，需針對各箱體依序執行。
*Module erection is an erection sequence with several preparation and erection activities linked to each other, which need to be executed for each box consecutively.*

模組安裝之順序描述於下列段落及安裝順序圖面（文件 60031-730-05-001）。
*The sequence for the erection of the module is described in the following paragraphs and the erection sequence drawings (document 60031-730-05-001).*

本章中提及之工項為一般性工項，不一定適用於所有箱體。各箱體之安裝細節與要求可在適用之圖面中找到。
*Activities mentioned in this chapter are general and do not have to be applicable for all boxes. Erection details and requirements for each box can be found in the applicable drawings.*

安裝之特定要求於相關段落中提及。
*Specific requirements for the erection are mentioned in the relevant paragraph.*

所有模組將以運輸框架運送至現場。
*All the modules will be transported in a shipping frame to site.*

預計配置一組用於水平搬運模組之吊梁。
*One hoisting beams for horizontal handling of modules is foreseen.*

預計配置一組帶有頂部吊裝框架之強化背架，以將模組從水平位置調整至垂直位置。
*One strong back with top hoisting frame to get the modules from horizontal to vertical position is foreseen.*

預計配置一組用於主吊車之頂部平衡梁，以及一組用於尾吊車之尾部平衡梁。
*One top spreader beam for the main crane and one tail spreader beam for the tail crane are foreseen.*

為防止整組運輸框架與強化背架組合傾覆，提供了一處至主鋼構之臨時連接。
*To avoid the bundle shipping frame – strong back combination from tumbling, a temporary connection to the main steel is provided.*

模組應自頂部進行安裝（頂部鎖定式）。
*The modules shall be erected from the top (top loaders).*

施工方法說明書 / 風險評估以及模組安裝之吊裝計畫應由安裝承包商準備。
*Work method statements / risk assessments with lifting plans for erection of the modules shall be prepared by the erection contractor.*



#### 8.7.2. 文件與程序 *Documents and procedures*

- 模組安裝所需之文件與程序：
  *Documents and procedures required for erection of the modules.*

    - 施工方法說明書：安裝模組。
      *Work method statement : Erection modules.*
    - 施工方法說明書：安裝模組施工架。
      *Work method statement : Erection scaffolding modules.*
    - 施工品質計畫書：熱回收鍋爐模組。
      *FQP : HRSG boiler modules.*
    - 螺栓鎖緊扭力程序書：非受壓組件。
      *Bolt torque procedure : Non pressure parts.*
    - 銲接作業程序書 / 銲接程序資格檢定紀錄 / 銲工資格檢定：非受壓組件。
      *WPS / PQR / WPQ : Non-pressure parts*
    - 銲接地圖 / 紀錄：非受壓組件。
      *Weld typical / record : Non-pressure parts.*
    - 銲接耗材處理程序書：非受壓組件。
      *Welding consumable handling procedure : Non-pressure parts.*
    - 非破壞檢測程序書 / 人員資格認證：非受壓組件。
      *NDE procedures / personnel qualifications : Non-pressure parts.*

#### 8.7.3. 準備工作與先決條件 *Preparations and preconditions*

在模組安裝之前與期間進行適當之準備，對於安全、順暢且高品質之模組安裝至關重要。在開始模組安裝之前，需提前準備一些工項。
*Proper preparation before and during the module erection is essential for a safe, smooth and high quality erection of the modules. Before erection of the modules can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance.*

![[Pasted image 20260611101017.png]]
暫時存放互連管線 *Temporary storage of interconnecting piping*
在模組安裝之前，請確認將大型內部互連管軸存放在 K 與 L 軸的橫向緩衝器（頂部 Box）上方的可能性。這將有助於後續這些部件的安裝步驟，因為模組安裝後內部進出空間會受限。
*Verify the possibility of storing large internal interconnecting pipe spools on top of the transverse bumpers (top boxes) at axis k and l, prior to module erection. This will facilitate the later erection steps for these parts, as accessibility is limited when modules are installed.*

##### 準備工作與先決條件 *Preparations and preconditions*
- 前一段落提及之文件與程序需備妥並由權責單位進行審查。
  *The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).*
- 下列準備工作/工項需已完成，若適用則需在 FQP 中簽署同意。
  *The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.*
    - 材料已接收並檢測其數量與品質 (OSD 報告)。
      *Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report)*
    - 主鋼構之灌漿已完成。
      *grouting of main steel*

##### • 底部板管道（臨時存放） *• Piping bottom panels (temporary storage)*
將現場已有的管道臨時存放在底部外殼板上。
*Temporarily store the piping (spools) which are available on site temporarily on the bottom casing panels.*

後續階段交付之管道應經由鍋爐地下室開放之前端與後端運送至適當位置。
*Piping (spools) delivered in a later stage, are brought into position via the boiler basement open front and rear sides.*
- 確保存放僅在夾板上進行，且夾板保持在正確位置。
  *Ensure storage is performed on plywood only and that the plywood panels remain properly positioned.*
- 存放底部管道時，應確保仍提供通往地下室箱體之適當通道。
  *Store the bottom piping in such a way that proper access to the basement boxes is still provided.*
- 在可能的情況下，利用爐殼穿透件將底部管道儘量存放在較低位置。
  *Where possible store the bottom piping as low as possible, using the casing penetrations.*

##### • 懸吊裝置碟形彈簧下方的臨時墊塊 *• Temporary spacers under disc springs of suspensions*
在將模組吊升至垂直位置之前，檢查碟形彈簧下方的臨時墊塊是否已拆除。
*Check if the temporary spacers under the disc springs are removed before lifting the module in vertical position.*
![[Pasted image 20260624142041.png]]
##### • 強化背架與頂部吊裝框架 *• Strong back and top hoisting frame*
對於強化背架與頂部吊裝之吊裝，請遵循章節「次鋼構」與適用圖面中規定之步驟與要求。
*For erection of the strong back and top hoisting follow the steps and requirements stipulated in the chapter “Secondary steel” and the applicable drawings.*
- 整地：強化背架與頂部吊升框架之區域。
  *Level the area for the strong back and top hoisting frame.*
- 強化背架與頂部吊裝框架組件交付時已完全預製，僅需在現場進行組裝。強化背架與頂部吊裝框架組件由框架件、梁、鋼索與卸扣組成。
  *The strong back and top hoisting frame parts are delivered completely fabricated and only require assembly on site. The strong back and top hoisting frame parts consist of a frame parts, beams, cables and shackles.*
- 依據圖面上規定之要求預先組裝強化背架與頂部吊裝框架。
  *Pre-assemble the strong back and top hoisting frame according the requirements stipulated on the drawings.*
- 確認強化背架框架上是否有正確之識別牌。
  *Verify the correct identification plate is present on the strong back frame.*
- 確認強化背架與頂部吊裝框架之起重設備標記與有效性（例如：CE 標記，若適用）。
  *Validate marking and validity of the marking for lifting equipment (e.g. CE marking) for the strong back and top hoisting frame (if applicable).*
- 檢查所有強化背架與頂部吊裝框架材料之完整性且無損壞。
  *Check all strong back and top hoisting frame material for integrity and absence of damages.*
- 若有任何偏差，請聯繫製造商。
  *In case of any deviation contact the manufacturer.*

##### • 吊升模組用之模組吊梁 *• Module hoisting beam for lifting modules*
執行將模組吊升至強化背架框架內之吊梁的預先組裝。
*Execute the pre-assembly of the hoisting beam for lifting of the modules into the strong back frame.*
- 吊梁組件交付時已完全預製，僅需在現場進行組裝。吊梁組件由框架、梁、鋼索、卸扣與鏈條組成。
  *The hoisting beam parts are delivered completely fabricated and only require assembly on site. The hoisting beam parts consist of a frame, beams, cables, shackles and chains.*
- 依據圖面上規定之要求預先組裝吊梁。
  *Pre-assemble the hosting beam according the requirements stipulated on the drawings.*
- 確認吊梁上是否有正確之識別牌。
  *Verify the correct identification plate is present on the hoisting beam.*
- 確認吊梁之起重設備標記與有效性（例如：CE 標記，若適用）。
  *Validate marking and validity of the marking for lifting equipment (e.g. CE marking) for the hoisting beam (if applicable).*
- 確認所有鏈條長度是否相同。
  *Verify all chains are of the same length.*
- 檢查所有模組吊梁材料之完整性且無損壞。
  *Check all module hoisting beam material for integrity and absence of damages.*
- 若有任何偏差，請聯繫製造商。
  *In case of any deviation contact the manufacturer.*

#### 8.7.4. 模組之卸載 / 裝載 *Unloading / loading of modules*

在開始模組之卸載 / 裝載之前，需提前準備一些工項。
*Before unloading / loading of the modules can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance.*

##### 準備工作與先決條件 *Preparations and preconditions*
- 前一段落提及之文件與程序需備妥並由權責單位進行審查。
  *The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).*
- 下列準備工作/工項需已完成，若適用則需在 FQP 中簽署同意。
  *The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.*
    - 模組安裝之準備工作已就緒。
      *Preparations for erection of modules ready*

##### 釋出後續工項 *Release subsequent activities*
- 順利完成本段落之工項後，即可釋出下列工項。
  *With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given:*
    - 各箱體之模組安裝。
      *Module erection per box*

##### 連接吊梁 *Connecting the hoisting beam*
- 將模組吊梁連接至自走式模組運輸車 (SPMT) 上的模組運輸框架。
  *Connect the module hoisting beam to the shipping frame of the module on the SPMT.*
    - 在連接前，確認模組狀況無損壞或其他異常。
      *Before connecting, verify the module condition to be without damages, or other abnormalities.*
    - 確認模組編號與位置是否正確。模組在強化背架中的位置取決於將從哪一側裝載哪一個箱體。
      *Verify the module to have the correct numbering and position.The module position in the strong back is depending on which box will be loaded from which side.*

##### 將模組裝載至強化背架與頂部吊裝框架上 *Loading of the modules onto the strong back and top hoisting frame*
- 將模組（包括運輸框架）吊升至強化背架上，並將運輸框架連接至強化背架與頂部吊裝框架。
  *Lift the module including shipping frame onto the strong back and connect the shipping frame  to the strong back and top hoisting frame.*
    - 僅在強化背架區域先抓水平之後，方可開始將模組裝載至強化背架上。
      *Loading of the modules onto the strong back can commence only when the strong back area is levelled.*
    - 使用正確之螺栓材料與扭力值鎖緊頂部之連接。
      *Use the correct bolt material and torque values for bolting the connections on the top part.*
    - 裝載時再次檢查模組編號與位置是否正確。
      *When loaded once more check the module to have the correct numbering and position.*
    - 確認模組是否依據圖面指示進行裝載。
      *Verify the module to be loaded as per the drawing instructions.*
![[Pasted image 20260624123154.png]]
##### 品質管制 *Quality control*
- 依據適用之 FQP 與/或程序執行品質管制工項。
  *Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).*
    - 若有任何偏差或失效，請聯繫製造商。
      *In case of any deviation or failure, contact the manufacturer.*
    - 在卸載 / 裝載過程中，應經常檢查設備之狀態是否良好。
      *During unloading / loading frequently check the status of the equipment to be in good shape.*
    - 在卸載 / 裝載過程中，請勿匆忙進行連接，以避免損壞模組。
      *During unloading / loading do not rush the connection process to avoid damaging of the modules.*

#### 8.7.5. 各箱體之模組安裝 *Module erection per box*

模組吊裝可自熱回收鍋爐之前端或後端開始，具體取決於熱回收鍋爐之配置、交付順序與吊車計畫。各箱體之模組吊裝順序應與所有相關涉入方進行妥善溝通。
*Module erection can be started from the front and rear side of the HRSG, depending on the HRSG lay-out, delivery sequence and crane plan. The sequence for module erection per box shall be properly communicated to all parties involved.*

在開始模組之吊裝之前，需提前準備一些工項。
*Before erection of the modules can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance.*

##### 準備工作與先決條件 *Preparations and preconditions*
- 前一段落提及之文件與程序需備妥並由權責單位進行審查。
  *The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).*
- 下列準備工作/工項需已完成，若適用則需在 FQP 中簽署同意。
  *The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.*
    - 模組安裝之準備工作已完成。
      *Preparation for module erection.*
    - 模組之卸載 / 裝載已完成。
      *Unloading / loading of modules*

##### 釋出後續工項 *Release subsequent activities*
- 順利完成本段落之工項後，即可釋出下列工項。
  *With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given:*
    - 各箱體之模組對齊調整。
      *Module alignment per box*

##### 模組之卸載 / 裝載 *Unloading / loading of the modules*
- 將模組自卡車上卸載並裝載至強化背架框架上，係基於第 8.7.4 節「模組之卸載 / 裝載」。
  *Unloading of the modules from the truck and loading onto the strong back frame, based on paragraph 8.8.5:“unloading/loading of modules”*
    - 若有任何偏差或失效，請聯繫製造商。
      *In case of any deviation or failure, contact the manufacturer.*
    - 在卸載 / 裝載過程中，應經常檢查設備之狀態是否良好。
      *During unloading / loading frequently check the status of the equipment to be in good shape.*
    - 在卸載 / 裝載過程中，請勿匆忙進行連接，以避免損壞模組。
      *During unloading / loading do not rush the connection process to avoid damaging of the modules.*

##### 模組之吊裝 *Erection of modules*
- 安裝各箱體之模組。
  *Erect the modules per box.*
    - 遵循圖面上提及之安裝順序進行模組之裝載。
      *Follow the erection sequence as mentioned on the drawing for loading of the modules.*
    - 使用主起重機與尾起重機（雙起重機工法）將強化背架模組組合自水平位置調整至垂直位置。主吊車連接至頂部吊裝框架，尾吊車連接至強化背架之底部。
      *Transfer the strong back module combination from horizontal to vertical position using a main and tail crane. Main crane is connected to the top hoisting frame and tail crane is connected to the bottom of the strong back.*
- ![[Pasted image 20260624123334.png]]
    - 一旦處於垂直位置，將強化背架連接至主鋼構上之臨時連接。
      *Once in vertical position connect the strong back to the temporary connections on the main steel.*
- ![[Pasted image 20260624123358.png]]
    - 自強化背架拆開頂部吊裝框架，並自運輸框架拆開模組。
      *Disconnect the top hoisting frame from the strong back and disconnect the module from the shipping frame.*
   ![[Pasted image 20260624123416.png]]
    - 使用頂部吊裝框架將模組吊升至鍋爐中，並將模組懸吊梁連接至主鋼構。
      *Lift the module with use of the top hoisting frame into the boiler and connect the module suspension beams to the main steel.*
    ![[Pasted image 20260624123554.png]]
    - 確保在吊升各個模組期間，所有的 shim 均已安裝，且在起重機斷開連接之前，模組懸吊梁與主鋼構之間的螺栓連接已完全緊固。
      *Be sure that during the erection of each module all the shims are erected and the bolted connections between the module suspension beams and the main steel structure are completely tightened before the crane is disconnected.*
    - 模組之對齊調整將在後續階段進行。
      *Alignment of the modules will be performed in a later stage.*
    - 請勿匆忙進行模組之吊裝，並避免對模組造成不必要之損壞。
      *Do not rush the erection of the modules and avoid unnecessary damaging of the modules.*
    - 若有任何偏差或失效，請聯繫製造商。
      *In case of any deviation or failure, contact the manufacturer.*

##### 品質管制 *Quality control*
- 依據適用之 FQP 與/或程序執行品質管制工項。
  *Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).*

#### 8.7.6. 每列之消音導流板、側壁導流板與頂棚導流板（若適用） *Sound baffles, sidewall gas baffles and attic baffles per row (if applicable)*

==在每列橫向緩衝器安裝驗收後，將（預先組裝之）每列導流板臨時安裝/存放於最終位置或其附近。==每列導流板之安裝應基於「消音導流板」與/或「模組側壁煙氣導流板」段落。
*Temporarily erect/store the (pre-assembled) baffles per row at or near their final location, after acceptance of the transverse bumper erection per row. Erection of the baffles per row shall be based on paragraph “Sound baffles” and/or “Module sidewall gas baffles”.*

每列導流板安裝之型式順序示於文件 60031-730-05-001。
*The typical sequence for the erection of the baffles per row per row is shown in document 60031-730-05-001.*
![[Pasted image 20260611101317.png]]
![[Pasted image 20260611101145.png]]
暫時存放導流板 *Temporary storage of field installed baffles*
在模組安裝之前，請確認將現場安裝的導流板與密封板存放在橫向緩衝器上方及底部 Box 內的可能性。這將有助於後續這些部件的安裝步驟，因為模組安裝後內部進出空間會受限。
*Verify the possibility of storing the field installed baffles and sealing plates on top of the transverse bumpers and in the bottom boxes, prior to module erection. This will facilitate the later erection steps for these parts, as accessibility is limited when modules are installed.*
#### 8.7.7. 每列施工施工架 *Scaffolding per row*

在每列橫向緩衝器安裝驗收以及消音導流板 / 頂棚導流板與側壁煙氣導流板（若適用）驗收後，搭建每列之施工施工架。
*Erect the scaffolding per row after acceptance of the transverse bumper erection per row and acceptance of the sound baffles / attic baffles and side wall gas baffles, where applicable.*

搭建每列施工架之型式順序示於文件 60031-730-05-001。
*The typical sequence for erection of the scaffolding per row is shown in document 60031-730-05-001.*
- 確保搭建之施工架安全，並提供通往模組表面、爐殼側壁、消音導流板與降流管之通道。
  *Ensure the scaffold built is safe and provides access to the module surface, casing sidewalls, the sound baffles and the down comer piping.*
- 妥善協調施工施工架之搭建，以確保搭建之施工架不會干擾附近材料之最終吊裝或組裝。
  *Properly coordinate building of the scaffolding to ensure the scaffold built will not interfere with final erection or assembly of materials in the vicinity.*

#### 8.7.8. 各模組對齊調整 *Alignment of the modules per box*

在開始模組之對齊調整之前，需提前準備一些工項。
*Before alignment of the modules can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance.*

##### 準備工作與先決條件 *Preparations and preconditions*
- 前一段落提及之文件與程序需備妥並由權責單位進行審查。
  *The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).*
- 下列準備工作/工項需已完成，若適用則需在 FQP 中簽署同意。
  *The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.*
    - 各箱體之模組已安裝。
      *Modules per box erected.*

##### 釋出後續工項 *Release subsequent activities*
- 順利完成本段落之工項後，即可釋出下列工項。
  *With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given:*
    - 頂部與底部模組集管連接板。
      *Connection plates top and bottom module headers.*
    - 模組懸吊密封。
      *Module suspension sealing.*
    - 環繞扣件連接。
      *Wrap around connections*

##### 對齊調整 *Alignment*
- 執行各箱體之模組對齊調整。
  *Perform alignment of the modules per box.*
- 各箱體之模組對齊調整可與其餘模組安裝工作平行執行。
  *Alignment of modules per box can be performed in parallel with the remaining module erection works.*
- 將模組對齊調整至正確位置與高程。
  *Align the modules to the correct position and elevation.*
- ![[Pasted image 20260624143835.png]]
    - 量測第一列之頂部與底部集管之高程，並確認實際情況是否符合圖面要求。
      *Measure the elevations of the top and bottom header of the first row and verify the actual situation with the requirements as per drawing.*
    - ==模組之對齊調整係經由旋轉模組懸吊桿頂部之螺帽來達成。==為了達到模組集管之正確高程與位置，順時針或逆時針旋轉懸吊桿上之螺帽。量測頂部集管位置之數據非常重要，以確定應向上或向下調整哪些懸吊桿，從而達到正確高程。
      *Alignment of the modules is achieved by turning the nuts on the top of the module suspension rods. In order to achieve the correct elevation and position of the module headers, turn the nuts on the suspension rods clock or counter clockwise. It is important to have the measurements of the top header locations in order to determine which rods should be adjusted up or down in order to achieve the correct elevation.*
    - 當旋轉懸吊桿頂部之螺帽時，確認懸吊桿是否靜止，且未在叉形鉸鏈連接處旋入或旋出。所需距離請參見圖面。
      *When turning the nut on top of the suspension rods verify that the rod is static and not turning in, or out of the clevis at the clevis connection. For the required distances, see the drawings.*
    - 由於大部分之膨脹發生在底部集管，因此將底部集管找平至正確高程非常重要。在調整螺帽期間，持續確認底部集管高程。
      *As most of the expansion is taking place at the bottom headers it is important to have the bottom headers levelled to the correct elevation. During adjustment of the nuts continuously verify the bottom header elevation.*
    - 確認懸吊桿是否垂直懸掛。
      *Verify the suspension rods are hanging straight.*
    - 當模組對齊調整完成後，點銲頂部之模組懸吊的墊圈板(washer plate)，然後即可安裝懸吊桿頂部之第二個螺帽。
      *When a module is aligned, tack-weld the washer plate of the module suspension on the top, after which the second nut on top of suspension rod can be erected.*
    - 與製造商討論對齊調整之順序，以達到各箱體之正確對齊調整。
      *Discuss the alignment sequence with the manufacturer to achieve the right alignment per box.*

##### 品質管制 *Quality control*
- 依據適用之 FQP 與/或程序執行品質管制工項。
  *Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).*
    - 執行各箱體之模組對齊調整。
      *Perform alignment of the modules per box.*
    - 釋出並隨帶未完成事項清單。
      *Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).*
    - 製造商應目視檢查並審查由管束夾最終對齊所量測收集之實際量測報告，以符合適用之公差圖面。
      *Manufacturer shall visually check the actual report of the measurements collected from the final alignment of the bundles to be in accordance with the applicable drawings.*

#### 8.7.9. 後續箱體之模組安裝 *Erection of modules consecutive boxes*

對於各箱體之模組、降流管、消音導流板與施工施工架之吊裝，重複本章第 8.7.1 節「一般」至第 8.7.8 節「各箱體之模組對齊調整」提及之前述步驟。
*For erection of the, modules, down comer piping, sound baffles and scaffolding per box, repeat the previous steps as mentioned in this chapter under paragraph 8.7.1: “General” till paragraph 8.7.8: “Alignment of the modules per box”*

#### 8.7.10. 頂部與底部模組集管連接板 *Connection plates top and bottom module headers*

在開始安裝頂部與底部集管上之連接板之前，需提前準備一些工項。
*Before erection of the connection plates on top and bottom headers can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance.*

##### 準備工作與先決條件 *Preparations and preconditions*
- 前一段落提及之文件與程序需備妥並由權責單位進行審查。
  *The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).*
- 下列準備工作/工項需已完成，若適用則需在 FQP 中簽署同意。
  *The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.*
    - 模組對齊調整。
      *Module alignment.*

##### 釋出後續工項 *Release subsequent activities*
- 順利完成本段落之工項後，即可釋出下列工項。
  *With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given:*
    - 橫向緩衝器之間的填隙片。
      *Shims between transverse bumpers.*

##### 安裝 *Erection*
- 安裝適用模組之頂部與底部集管連接板。
  *Erect the connection plates on the top and bottom headers for the applicable modules.*
    - 檢查板上之標記編號以正確安裝。
      *Check the mark numbers on the plates for correct erection.*
    - 若有任何偏差，請聯繫製造商。
      *In case of any deviation, contact the manufacturer.*

##### 品質管制 *Quality control*
- 依據適用之 FQP 與/或程序執行品質管制工項。
  *Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).*
    - 檢查各箱體之模組集管連接板(header connection plates)。
      *Check the module header connection plates per box.*
    - 釋出並隨帶未完成事項清單。
      *Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).*

#### 8.7.11. 橫向緩衝器與模組集管 / 環繞扣件之間的填隙片 *Shims between transverse bumpers and module headers / wrap arounds*

在開始安裝橫向緩衝器與模組集管及環繞扣件之間的填隙片之前，需提前準備一些工項。
*Before erection of the shims between transverse bumpers and the module headers and wrap arounds can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance.*

##### 準備工作與先決條件 *Preparations and preconditions*
- 前一段落提及之文件與程序需備妥並由權責單位進行審查。
  *The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).*
- 下列準備工作/工項需已完成，若適用則需在 FQP 中簽署同意。
  *The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.*
    - 模組對齊調整。
      *Module alignment.*
    - 連接板已安裝。
      *Erection connection plates.*
    - 材料已接收並檢測其數量與品質 (OSD 報告)。
      *Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report)*

##### 釋出後續工項 *Release subsequent activities*
- 順利完成本段落之工項後，即可釋出下列工項。
  *With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given:*
    - 環繞扣件固定件安裝。
      *Erection of wrap around fixations.*

##### 安裝 *Erection*
- 橫向緩衝器與模組集管 / 環繞扣件之間填隙片之安裝順序示於文件 60031-730-05-001。
  *The erection sequence for shims between the transverse bumpers and module headers / wrap arounds is shown in document 60031-730-05-001.*
- 裝配並點銲帶有臨時填充板(木板)之填隙片。
  *Fit and tack-weld the shims with temporary filler plates.*
    - 為確定填隙片之正確位置，確認填隙片上之組別標記編號。
      *To determine the correct position of the shims, verify the group marking number on the shims.*
    - 在進行填隙片安裝量測之前，先確保各箱體之模組已經垂直懸掛且已「收縮鎖緊 hanging plump and compressed」。
      *Make sure modules per box are hanging plump before and “compressed” before taking measurements for shim erection.*
    - 依據適用之圖面與公差圖面安裝填隙片。
      *Erect the shim plates as per the applicable drawings and tolerance drawings.*
    - 考量集管與環繞扣件所需之自由間隙（用於熱膨脹可能性）非常重要。仔細閱讀公差圖面上關於填隙片安裝之附註。
      *It is very important to take into account the required free gap (for expansion possibilities) of headers and wrap-arounds. Carefully read the notes for shimming on the tolerances drawings.*
    - 必要時，調整填隙片至正確長度。在此情況下，請先聯繫製造商。
      *When necessary adjust the shim plates to the correct length. In this case, first contact the manufacturer.*
    - 在安裝填隙片之前，在填隙片上放置一片具有所需自由間隙厚度之臨時填充板(木板)。這將確保提供填隙片與集管或環繞扣件之間的正確自由間隙。
      *Before erection of the shim, place a temporary filler plate with the required free gap thickness to the shim. This will ensure the correct free gap between the shim and the header or wrap-around is provided.*
    - 在填隙片安裝期間，檢查公差圖面所給之公差。
      *Check the tolerance as given on the tolerance drawings, during erection of the shims.*

##### 銲接 *Welding*
- 銲接所有填隙片。
  *Weld all shims.*
    - 依照圖面與 WPS 之銲接細節或型式進行。
      *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.*

##### 品質管制 *Quality control*
- 依據適用之 FQP 與/或程序執行品質管制工項。
  *Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).*
    - 在填隙片最終銲接之前檢查填隙片公差。
      *Check the shim plate tolerances before final welding of the plate.*
    - 釋出並隨帶未完成事項清單。
      *Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).*
    - 製造商應目視檢查並審查集管與橫向緩衝器之間、以及集管與填隙片（位於橫向緩衝器上）之間的量測實際報告，以符合適用之公差圖面 60031-730-06-系列。
      *Manufacturer shall visually check and review the actual survey report of the measurements between the headers -transverse bumpers and the headers - shims (located on the transverse bumpers) to be in accordance with the applicable tolerance drawings 60031-730-06-series.*

#### 8.7.12. 環繞扣件固定件 *Warp around fixations*

在開始安裝環繞扣件固定件之前，需提前準備一些工項。
*Before erection of the wrap around fixations can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance.*
![[Pasted image 20260624123858.png]]
##### 準備工作與先決條件 *Preparations and preconditions*
- 前一段落提及之文件與程序需備妥並由權責單位進行審查。
  *The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).*
- 下列準備工作/工項需已完成，若適用則需在 FQP 中簽署同意。
  *The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.*
    - 填隙片已安裝。
      *Erection shim plates.*
    - 材料已接收並檢測其數量與品質 (OSD 報告)。
      *Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report)*

##### 釋出後續工項 *Release subsequent activities*
- 順利完成本段落之工項後，即可釋出下列工項。
  *With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given:*
    - 內部護肩安裝。
      *Erection internal shoulders.*
##### 安裝 *Erection*
- 安裝、裝配並點銲固定件。
  *Erect, fit and tack-weld the fixations.*
    - 使用組別標記編號檢查環繞固定件之位置是否正確。
      *Check for correct location of the wrap-around fixations, using the group marking number.*
    - 在銲接前，檢查固定件之兩 (2) 孔之間的尺寸。
      *Check the dimensions between the two (2) holes of the fixations, before welding.*
    - 檢查圖面以確定固定件之確切位置。
      *Check the drawings for exact location of the fixations.*
    - 若有任何偏差，請聯繫製造商。
      *In case of any deviation, contact manufacturer.*

##### 銲接 *Welding*
- 銲接所有環繞扣件固定件。
  *Weld all wrap around fixations.*
    - 依照圖面與 WPS 之銲接細節或型式進行。
      *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.*

##### 品質管制 *Quality control*
- 依據適用之 FQP 與/或程序執行品質管制工項。
  *Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).*
    - 銲接前檢查公差。
      *Check the tolerances before welding.*
    - 釋出並隨帶未完成事項清單。
      *Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).*

#### 8.7.13. 內部護肩 *Internal shoulders*

在開始安裝內部護肩之前，需提前準備一些工項。
*Before erection of the internal shoulders can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance.*

![[Pasted image 20260611094443.png]]
預組內部護肩支撐 (滑動管設計)時，盡可能將其推向外殼壁，以便為模組安裝騰出空間。
*(pre) erect the internal shoulders (sliding pipe design). At this stage of erection slide them as much as possible towards the casing walls in order to create room for module erection.*
##### 準備工作與先決條件 *Preparations and preconditions*
- 前一段落提及之文件與程序需備妥並由權責單位進行審查。
  *The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).*
- 下列準備工作/工項需已完成，若適用則需在 FQP 中簽署同意。
  *The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.*
    - 側壁外殼板（包括保溫材與內襯板）。
      *Side wall casing panels including insulation and liner sheeting*
    - 材料已接收並檢測其數量與品質 (OSD 報告)。
      *Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report)*

##### 釋出後續工項 *Release subsequent activities*
- 順利完成本段落之工項後，即可釋出下列工項。
  *With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given:*
    - 管束（模組）鎖定。
      *Locking of bundles (modules)*

##### 安裝與對齊調整 *Erection and alignment*
- 依據相關護肩圖面上的理論尺寸安裝各箱體之頂部與底部內部護肩。
  *Erect the top and bottom internal shoulders per box according theoretical dimensions on relevant shoulder drawings.*
- 對齊內部頂部與底部護肩。
  *Align the top and bottom internal shoulders.*
    - 圖面上提及之自由間隙 "a" 必須存在於護肩與模組集管蓋頂部與底部之間。
      *The free gap “a”, as mentioned on the drawings, needs to present between the shoulder and the module header covers top and bottom.*
    - 在護肩安裝期間，此自由間隙 "a" 可經由安裝或拆除填隙片來達成。
      *During erection of the shoulders, the free gap “a” can be achieved by erecting or removing shim plates.*
    - 最終自由間隙 "a" 應在護肩安裝後以及內部頂部與底部管道安裝後進行檢查。
      *The final free gap “a” shall be checked after erection of the shoulders and after erection of the internal top and bottom piping.*
    - 內部管道安裝完成且自由間隙 "a" 正確後，依據型式圖安裝長圓孔與固定孔之護肩螺栓連接。
      *After the internal piping erection is completed and the free gap “a” is correct, erect the shoulder bolt connections for the slotted and fixed holes as per the typical.*
    - 若有任何偏差，請聯繫製造商。
      *In case of any deviation, contact the manufacturer.*

##### 品質管制 *Quality control*
- 依據適用之 FQP 與/或程序執行品質管制工項。
  *Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).*
    - 確認公差。
      *Verify the tolerances.*
    - 釋出並隨帶未完成事項清單。
      *Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).*
    - 製造商應目視檢查並審查集管蓋與內部護肩之間量測的實際報告，以符合適用之公差圖面 60031-730-06-系列。
      *Manufacturer shall visually check and review the actual survey report for the measurements between header caps and the internal shoulders, according the applicable tolerance drawings 60031-730-06-series.*

#### 8.7.14. 管束模組鎖定 *Locking of bundles (modules)*

在開始鎖定管束（模組）之前，需提前準備一些工項。
*Before locking of the bundles (modules) can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance.*
![[Pasted image 20260624130525.png]]
##### 準備工作與先決條件 *Preparations and preconditions*
- 前一段落提及之文件與程序需備妥並由權責單位進行審查。
  *The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).*
- 下列準備工作/工項需已完成，若適用則需在 FQP 中簽署同意。
  *The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.*
    - 內部護肩安裝已完成。
      *Erection of internal shoulders*
    - 環繞扣件固定件安裝已完成。
      *Erection of wrap around fixations*
    - 橫向緩衝器、模組集管與環繞扣件之間的填隙片安裝已完成。
      *Erection of shim plates between transverse bumpers, module headers and wrap arounds*

##### 釋出後續工項 *Release subsequent activities*
- 順利完成本段落之工項後，即可釋出下列工項。
  *With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given:*
    - 內部管道安裝。
      *Erection of internal piping*

##### 安裝 *Erection*
- 在護肩與頂部和底部集管之集管蓋之間安裝臨時型鋼（角鋼）。
  *Erect a temporary profile (angle) between the shoulders and the header covers of the top and bottom headers.*
- 將型鋼點銲至護肩，以在鍋爐寬度方向鎖定管束，並保持所需之自由間隙。切勿銲接至集管！
  *Tack weld the profile to the shoulders in order to lock the bundles in the boiler widthwise direction, maintaining the free gap required. Do not weld to the header!*
    - 模組已使用填隙片上之臨時填隙片在鍋爐長度方向鎖定。透過此臨時型鋼（角鋼）之吊裝，整個模組管束可在鍋爐寬度方向與長度方向進行鎖定，以確保內部管道安裝期間隨時符合兩側之自由間隙要求。
      *The modules were already locked in the boiler longitudinal direction using the temporary filling plates on the shims. Through the erection of these temporary profile (angle) the complete module bundle is locked in both the boiler width wise and the longitudinal direction, ensuring the free gap requirements to either side at all times during internal piping erection.*
    - 臨時型鋼至護肩之點銲應以容易在後續階段拆除之方式進行。
      *Tack welding of the temporary profile to the shoulder to be performed in such a way that the weld can be easily removed in a later stage.*

##### 品質管制 *Quality control*
- 依據適用之 FQP 與/或程序執行品質管制工項。
  *Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).*
    - 檢查臨時型鋼安裝是否正確。
      *Check correct erection temporary profile.*
    - 釋出並隨帶未完成事項清單。
      *Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).*

#### 8.7.15. 內部管道安裝 *Erection internal piping*

鍋爐內部管道（連接管道）之安裝可在管束鎖定完成驗收後開始。鍋爐內部（連接）管道之安裝應基於「管道」章節之說明。內部管道安裝之型式順序示於文件 60031-730-05-001。
*Boiler internal piping (interconnecting piping) erection can start after acceptance of the locking of the modules. Erection of the boiler internal (interconnecting) piping shall be based on chapter “Piping”. The typical sequence for the erection of the internal piping is shown in document 60031-730-05-001.*

#### 8.7.16. 吊桿懸吊密封 *Harp suspension sealing*

一旦確認模組之懸吊與安裝正確，即可將位於鍋爐外部之懸吊桿關閉至氣密狀態。這係透過在鍋爐頂部外部安裝懸吊密封來完成。
*Once the modules have been verified to be suspended and installed correctly the harp suspension rods located on the outside of the boiler can be closed of gastight. This is done by installing the harp suspension sealing on the outside on top of the boiler.*

##### 準備工作與先決條件 *Preparations and preconditions*
- 前一段落提及之文件與程序需備妥並由權責單位進行審查。
  *The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).*
- 下列準備工作/工項需已完成，若適用則需在 FQP 中簽署同意。
  *The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.*
    - 具備臨時運輸框架之模組懸吊管束對齊調整確認已完成。
      *Verification of the harp bundle alignment for modules with temporary transport frames.*

##### 安裝 *Installation*
- 為所有具備臨時運輸框架之模組安裝懸吊密封。
  *Install the harp suspension sealing for all modules with temporary transport frames.*
    - 仔細檢查圖面，以確定哪些密封箱需要填充保溫材。在配有碟形彈簧之箱體中，不得安裝任何內部保溫材。
      *Carefully check the drawing to identify which box needs to filled with insulation. In case of boxes with disc springs no internal insulation shall be installed.*
    - 在安裝「懸吊密封箱」之前，於槽鋼之間一直放置保溫材到底部。對所有需要保溫材之位置執行此操作。
      *Before installation of the “harp suspension sealing box” place insulation between the channels all the way to the bottom. Do this is for all locations requiring insulation.*
  ![[Pasted image 20260624130112.png]]
##### 銲接 *Welding*
- 銲接懸吊密封。
  *Weld the harp suspension sealing.*
    - 遵循圖面上的銲接細節或型式進行。
      *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings.*

##### 品質管制 *Quality control*
- 依據適用之 FQP 與/或程序執行品質管制工項。
  *Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).*
- 釋出並隨帶未完成事項清單。
  *Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).*

#### 8.7.17. 模組安裝之最終檢查 *Final inspection of the module erection*

當特定系統或一組特定組件之機械安裝完成後，應進行檢查。未完成項目應彙整於未完成項目清單中，並附於最終檢查合格證上。
*When the mechanical erection of a certain system, or group of specific components is finalized these shall be inspected. Outstanding items shall be collected in an outstanding items list and attached to the Final inspection Certificate.*

具備臨時運輸框架之模組最終檢查合格書描述了所檢查之系統或組件。
*The Final inspection Certificate of the modules with temporary transport frames describes the systems or components inspected.*

##### 檢查 *Inspection*
- 最終檢查合格書上提及之所有系統或特定組件組應進行正確安裝、完整性與損壞之最終檢查。
  *All systems or group of specific components referred to on the Final inspection Certificate shall have a final inspection for correct erection, completeness and damages.*
- 在步行檢視後應立即建立未完成項目紀錄（如有）。
  *A record of outstanding items (if any) shall be set-up directly after the walk-down.*
- 若有未完成項目清單適用，其應分類為：
  *In case a list of outstanding items is applicable it shall be categorized in :*
    - 於水壓試驗前需解決之項目（A 級項目）
      *Items to be solved before hydro testing (A-items)*
    - 於熱試運轉前需解決之項目（B 級項目）
      *Items to be solved before hot-commissioning (B-items)*
    - 於初期驗收前需解決之項目（C 級項目）
      *Items to be solved before provisional acceptance (PAC) (C-items)*
- 確認所涉及系統之適用現場 FQP 已由所有涉入方簽署同意。未完成項目應納入未決點清單。
  *Verify that the applicable site FQPs for the systems involved are signed off by all parties involved. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list*
- 確認所有不符合事項報告已關閉。未完成項目應納入未決點清單。
  *Verify that all Non-Conformity Reports are closed. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list*

### 8.8. 爐殼（剩餘組件） *Casing (remaining components)*

本段落描述爐殼剩餘組件之安裝。
*This paragraph describes the erection of the remaining components for the casing.*

#### 8.8.1. 一般 *General*

施工方法說明書 / 風險評估以及剩餘爐殼組件安裝之吊裝計畫應由安裝承包商準備。
*Work method statements / risk assessments with lifting plans for the erection of the remaining casing components shall be prepared by the erection contractor.*

剩餘爐殼組件之吊裝順序示于文件 60031-730-05-001。
*The erection sequence for the remaining casing components is shown in document 60031-730-05-001.*

#### 8.8.2. 文件與程序 *Documents and procedures*

- 剩餘爐殼組件安裝所需之文件與程序：
  *Documents and procedures required for erection of the remaining casing components.*

    - 施工方法說明書：安裝鍋爐外殼板。
      *Work method statement : Erection boiler casing panels*
    - 施工方法說明書：安裝高空作業平台（鍋爐內部）。
      *Work method statement : Erection elevated work platform (inside boiler)*
    - 施工品質計畫書：熱回收鍋爐爐殼。
      *FQP : HRSG boiler casing*
    - 螺栓鎖緊扭力程序書：非受壓組件。
      *Bolt torque procedure : Non pressure parts.*
    - 施工方法說明書：施工施工架。
      *Work method statement : Scaffolding*
    - 銲接作業程序書 / 銲接程序資格檢定紀錄 / 銲工資格檢定：非受壓組件。
      *WPS / PQR / WPQ : Non-pressure parts*
    - 銲接地圖 / 紀錄：非受壓組件。
      *Weld typical / record : Non-pressure parts*
    - 銲接耗材處理程序書：非受壓組件。
      *Welding consumable handling procedure : Non-pressure parts*
    - 非破壞檢測程序書 / 人員資格認證：非受壓組件。
      *NDE procedures / personnel qualifications : Non-pressure parts*

#### 8.8.3. 前後側(D & F 與 H & M )垂直外殼板之安裝 *Erection of vertical top and bottom casing panels rows D & F and H & M*

這些垂直頂部與底部皮組件位於鍋爐進口側與出口側，以及 SCR 區域。
*These vertical top and bottom panels are located on boiler inlet side and outlet side, as well as in the SCR area.*

在開始安裝垂直頂部與底部板之前，需提前準備一些工項。
*Before erection of the vertical top and bottom panels can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance.*
![[Pasted image 20260624130452.png]]
![[Pasted image 20260624142217.png]]
![[Pasted image 20260624142230.png]]
##### 準備工作與先決條件 *Preparations and preconditions*
- 前一段落提及之文件與程序需備妥並由權責單位進行審查。
  *The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).*
- 下列準備工作/工項需已完成，若適用則需在 FQP 中簽署同意。
  *The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.*
    - 其對應的模組已鎖定。
      *Locking of modules for the applicable box*
    - 材料已接收並檢測其數量與品質 (OSD 報告)。
      *Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report)*

##### 釋出後續工項 *Release subsequent activities*
- 順利完成本段落之工項後，即可釋出下列工項。
  *With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given:*
    - 內部保溫與內襯板。
      *Internal insulation and liner sheeting.*
    - 管式緩衝器之最終安裝。
      *Final erection pipe bumpers.*

##### 安裝 *Erection*
- 安裝帶有角鋼連接之垂直頂部與底部皮組件（若適用）。
  *Erect the vertical top and bottom panels with angle bar connections (where applicable).*
- 裝配並點銲外殼板。
  *Fit and tack-weld the panels.*
    - 對齊外殼板，且在此階段僅進行點銲。外殼板需成一直線並彼此平行。
      *Align the casing panels and in this stage only tack-weld. The panels need to be in line and parallel to each other.*
    - 安裝前，拆除爐殼穿透孔處之塑料與保溫棉。使用刀具妥善切割塑料與保溫棉。切勿用力拉扯。
      *Before erection, remove the plastic and insulation wool from the casing penetrations. Properly cut the plastic and wool using a knife. Do not pull it out using force.*
    - 將皮組件對齊至正確位置。
      *Align the panels to the correct position.*
    - 切除頂部皮組件上之內部保溫防護塑料。
      *Cut away the internal insulation protection plastic from the top panels.*
    - 在點銲期間，使用銲接毯覆蓋保溫棉以進行火花防護。
      *During tack welding, cover the insulation wool using weld blankets for spark protection.*
    - 在安裝垂直頂部與底部外殼板期間，切勿忘記臨時安裝管式緩衝器。在安裝前，以保溫棉填充管式緩衝器。
      *During erection of the vertical top and bottom casing panels do not forget to temporarily erect the pipe bumpers. Prior to erection, fill the pipe bumpers with insulation wool.*
    - 關於管式緩衝器之安裝說明，請參見第 8.9.5 節。
      *For erection instructions for pipe bumpers, see paragraph 8.9.5.*
  ![[Pasted image 20260624143011.png]]
##### 皮組件之銲接 *Welding of the panels*
- 將外殼板銲接至角鋼連接處。
  *Weld the casing panels to the angle bar connections.*
    - 依照圖面與 WPS 之銲接細節或型式進行。
      *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.*
    - 所有外部銲接應為連續銲，外部不允許進行間斷銲。
      *All external welds shall be continuous, no stich welds on the outside allowed.*
    - 僅在內部接頭上允許進行間斷銲，尺寸請參見細節圖。
      *Stitch welds are only allowed on the inside joints, for dimensions see details.*

##### 頂部 / 底部皮組件現場組件之安裝 *Field parts erection top / bottom panels*
- 將導板 / 加強板安裝至外部右側 / 左側外殼板上。
  *Erect the guide / stiffeners to the outside right / left side casing panels.*
- 裝配並點銲導板 / 加強板。
  *Fit and tack-weld the guide plates / stiffeners.*
    - 導板與加強板之交叉點及連接點需以正確之銲接坡口準備進行安裝。
      *Guide and stiffener plate cross and connection points need to be erected with the correct weld preparation.*
    - 角隅處與現場接頭處之所有間隙應使用填隙片（厚度 6 mm）進行密合（密封銲接）。
      *All gaps at corners and field splices shall be closed (seal welded) using filler plates.(6 mm thickness).*

##### 銲接 *Welding*
- 銲接所有現場零件。
  *Weld all field parts.*
    - 依照圖面與 WPS 之銲接細節或型式進行。
      *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.*

##### 品質管制 *Quality control*
- 依據適用之 FQP 與/或程序執行品質管制工項。
  *Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).*
    - 銲接前檢查外殼板之裝配與對齊情況。
      *Check the fit-up and alignment of the panels before welding.*

### 8.9. 熱回收鍋爐導流板與密封板 *HRSG baffles and sealing plates*

本段落描述熱回收鍋爐導流板與密封板之安裝。

施工方法說明書 / 風險評估以及熱回收鍋爐導流板與密封板安裝之吊裝計畫應由安裝承包商準備。
*Work method statements / risk assessments with lifting plans for installation of the HRSG baffle and sealing plates shall be prepared by the erection contractor.*

熱回收鍋爐導流板與密封板之安裝順序示于文件 60031-730-05-001。
*The erection sequence for the HRSG baffle and sealing plate is shown in document 60031-730-05-001.*

#### 8.9.2. 文件與程序 *Documents and procedures*

- 熱回收鍋爐導流板與密封板安裝所需之文件與程序：
  *Documents and procedures required for installation of the HRSG baffles and sealing plates.*

    - 施工方法說明書：安裝熱回收鍋爐導流板與密封板。
      *Work method statement : Installation HRSG baffles and sealing plates*
