      *Work method statement : Installation scaffolding boiler casing*
    - 施工品質計畫書：熱回收鍋爐導流板與密封板。
      *FQP : HRSG baffles and sealing plates*
    - 銲接作業程序書 / 銲接程序資格檢定紀錄 / 銲工資格檢定：非受壓組件。
      *WPS / PQR / WPQ : Non-pressure parts*
    - 銲接地圖 / 紀錄：非受壓組件。
      *Weld typical / record : Non-pressure parts*
    - 銲接耗材處理程序書：非受壓組件。
      *Welding consumable handling procedure : Non-pressure parts*
    - 非破壞檢測程序書 / 人員資格認證：非受壓組件。
      *NDE procedures / personnel qualifications : Non-pressure parts*

#### 8.9.3. 緩衝器密封板 *Bumper sealing plates*

密封板位於頂部與底部之橫向緩衝器及管式緩衝器上，其功用與底地板相同。保持煙氣路徑與熱回收鍋爐頂棚箱及地下室箱隔離。
*Sealing plates are located on the top and bottom transverse bumpers and pipe bumpers and fulfill the same purpose as the floor plates. Keeping the flue gas path and HRSG attic and basement boxes separated.*

在開始安裝緩衝器密封板之前，需提前準備一些工項。
*Before installation of bumper sealing plates can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance.*

##### 準備工作與先決條件 *Preparations and preconditions*
- 前一段落提及之文件與程序需備妥並由權責單位進行審查。
  *The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).*
- 下列準備工作/工項需已完成，若適用則需在 FQP 中簽署同意。
  *The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.*
    - 拆除臨時填隙片。
      *Removal of the temporary filler plates.*

##### 釋出後續工項 *Release subsequent activities*
- 順利完成本段落之工項後，即可釋出下列工項。
  *With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given:*
    - 安裝緩衝器端板。
      *Erection bumper end plates.*

##### 安裝 *Erection*
- 安裝、裝配並點銲緩衝器密封板。
  *Erect, fit and tack-weld the bumper sealing plates.*
    - 圖面上給定之自由空間係用於熱膨脹，檢查實際情況並調整（必要時）。正確公差請參見適用圖面。
      *The given free space on the drawings is required for thermal expansion, check the actual situation and adjust (if necessary). See the applicable drawings for the correct tolerances.*
    - 密封板之連接處可用作滑動點。安裝期間，妥善確認滑動點之位置，且僅銲接圖面指示之部件。
      *The sealing plate connection point is used as a sliding point. During installation properly verify where the sliding point is located and only weld the parts indicated on the drawing.*
    - 板上之長圓孔係用於板之熱膨脹。正確公差請參見圖面。
      *The slotted holes in the plates are required for thermal expansion of the plate. See drawings for the correct tolerances.*
    - 在長圓孔連接處，螺栓連接應以手部鎖緊之程度安裝並進行點銲，以確保在熱態下有適當之自由移動。然而，連接部件之間應有金屬接觸。
      *At the slotted hole connections the bolt connection shall be installed finger tight and tack welded, ensuring proper free movement during hot conditions. Metal contact between the connected parts however should exist.*
    - 在固定點處，所有螺帽應完全緊固且螺栓連接應點銲。
      *At the fixed points, all nuts shall be fully fastened and the bolt connection tack welded*
    - 安裝期間確認工件標記編號是否正確。
      *Verify the piece mark numbers for correctness during installation.*
    - 關於自由空間或自由間隙有任何偏差，請聯繫製造商。
      *In case of any deviation regarding free space or free gaps, contact the manufacturer.*

##### 銲接 *Welding*
- 銲接所有密封板與端部蓋板。
  *Weld all sealing plates and cover end plates.*
    - 依照圖面與 WPS 之銲接細節或型式進行。
      *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.*

##### 品質管制 *Quality control*
- 依據適用之 FQP 與/或程序執行品質管制工項。
  *Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).*
- 檢查滑動點與固定點處之螺栓連接。
  *Check the bolt connections at sliding and fix points.*
- 檢查長圓孔之正確公差。
  *Check the slotted holes for correct tolerances.*
- 釋出並隨帶未完成事項清單。
  *Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).*

##### 緩衝器端部板之安裝 *Erection bumper end plates*
- 安裝、裝配並點銲緩衝器端板。
  *Erect, fit and tack-weld the bumper end plates.*
    - 將型鋼正確安裝至側壁內襯板，無間隙。
      *Fit the profile correctly to the sidewall liner sheeting without gap.*
    - 安裝型鋼期間，保持圖面上提及之給定自由間隙非常重要。
      *During installation of the profile it is important to keep the given free gap as mentioned on the drawings.*
    - 僅依照圖面所示點銲蓋板，並確保在滑動點處能自由移動。
      *Tack weld the cover plates only as stated on the drawing and ensure free movement at the sliding point.*
    - 關於自由間隙有任何偏差，請聯繫製造商。
      *In case of any deviation regarding free gaps, contact the manufacturer.*

##### 銲接 *Welding*
- 銲接所有密封板與端部蓋板。
  *Weld all sealing plates and cover end plates.*
    - 依照圖面與 WPS 之銲接細節或型式進行。
      *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.*

##### 品質管制 *Quality control*
- 依據適用之 FQP 與/或程序執行品質管制工項。
  *Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).*
- 銲接前檢查所有自由間隙。
  *Check all free gaps before welding.*
- 釋出並隨帶未完成事項清單。
  *Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).*

#### 8.9.4. 頂棚(Attic)與地下室(basement)導流板 *Attic and basement baffles*

頂棚與地下室導流板位於熱回收鍋爐之頂棚與地下室擋風箱中，用於減少這些腔室中之旁通煙氣，其為將頂棚箱與地下室擋風箱劃分為數個封閉腔室的垂直密封板。
*The attic and basement baffles are located in the HRSG attic and basement boxes and serve the purpose of reducing bypass flow in these compartments. They are vertical sealing plates dividing the attic and basement boxes in several closed of compartments.*

在安裝頂棚與地下室導流板之前，需提前準備一些工項。
*Before erection of the attic and basement baffles, some activities need to be prepared in advance.*

##### 準備工作與先決條件 *Preparations and preconditions*
- 前一段落提及之文件與程序需備妥並由權責單位進行審查。
  *The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).*
- 下列準備工作/工項需已完成，若適用則需在 FQP 中簽署同意。
  *The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.*
    - 熱回收鍋爐內部管道已安裝。
      *HRSG internal piping installed.*
    - 熱回收鍋爐頂棚箱與地下室箱之內部保溫材已安裝。
      *Internal insulation HRSG attic and basement boxes installed*
    - 緩衝器密封板已安裝。
      *Bumper sealing plates installed*
- 所有大型頂棚與地下室導流板材料在先前的安裝步驟中已存放，且地下室導流板已定位於地下室框中，頂棚導流板已定位於頂棚框中。
  *All large attic and basement baffle materials were already stored in previous erection steps and are positioned in the basement boxes for the basement baffles and in the attic boxes for the attic baffles.*
- 導流板組件之識別。
  *Identification of the baffle components.*
    - 所有現場安裝之導流板組件其上皆有單獨之工件標記編號以利識別。
      *All field installed baffle components have individual piece mark numbers for identification.*
    - 這些應在安裝前進行檢查。
      *These shall be checked prior to installation.*
    - 若有任何偏差，請聯繫製造商。
      *In case of any deviation contact the manufacturer.*
- 測量「箱體」以確認其尺寸。
  *Measurements of the “boxes” for verification of sizes.*
    - 在開始安裝前，仔細測量「箱體」尺寸。在此測量確認期間，確切確定管道穿透件之位置非常重要。
      *Before start erection carefully measure the “boxes” for sizing. During this measurement verification, it is important to exactly determine the location of the piping penetrations.*
    - 若有任何偏差，請聯繫製造商。
      *In case of any deviations contact the manufacturer.*

##### 安裝 *Erection*
- 安裝、裝配並點銲導流板。
  *Erect, fit and tack-weld the baffles.*
    - 導流板可在垂直與水平方向進行調整，但保持圖面提及之自由間隙與空間。將實際尺寸與圖面進行比較。若有重大偏差，請聯繫製造商。
      *The baffles can be adjusted in the vertical and horizontal direction, but keep the free gaps and spaces as mentioned on the drawings. Compare the actual dimensions with the drawings.In case of major deviations, contact the manufacturer.*
    - 關於頂棚導流板之安裝，從頂部緩衝器上之底部開始，對齊導流板並確認自由間隙與空間是否存在。
      *For erection of the attic baffles, start with the bottom part on the top bumpers, align the baffles plates and verify presence of the free gaps and spaces.*
    - 其次，安裝頂部。同樣地，在此對齊鋼板並確認可用之自由間隙與空間。
      *Secondly, erect the top part. Also, align the plates here and verify the free gaps and spaces available.*
    - 關於地下室導流板之安裝，從底部緩衝器上之頂部開始，對齊鋼板並檢查自由間隙與空間。
      *For erection of the basement baffles, start with the top part on the bottom bumpers, align the plates and check the free gaps and spaces.*
    - 其次，安裝底部。同樣地，在此對齊鋼板並確認可用之自由間隙與空間。
      *Secondly, erect the bottom part. Also, align the plates here and verify the free gaps and spaces available.*
    - 仔細確認組裝期間在導流板壁板上所作之割孔。必要時進行調整。
      *Carefully verify the cut-outs made on the baffle profiles during the assembly. Adjust when necessary*
    - 依據公差圖面檢查所有尺寸。
      *Check all dimensions according the tolerances drawings.*

##### 銲接 *Welding*
- 銲接所有導流板。
  *Weld all the baffles.*
    - 依照圖面與 WPS 之銲接細節或型式進行。
      *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.*
    - 銲接前，檢查頂棚與地下室導流板與內部內襯板之間的自由間隙。
      *Check the free gap between the attic and basement baffles and the internal liner sheeting before welding.*
    - 在銲接作業期間，仔細控制熱輸入量，確保鋼板材料不發生變形。
      *Carefully control heat input during welding works, assuring no deformation of the plate material.*

##### 頂棚與地下室導流板現場組件之安裝 *Field components erection attic and basement baffles*
- 在每個導流板管道穿透孔處安裝、裝配並點銲密封板。
  *Erect, fit and tack weld the sealing plates at each baffle pipe penetration.*
    - 管道密封板之安裝應以使管道在熱態下能自由移動之方式進行。
      *Pipe sealing plates shall be installed in such a way that the pipe can move freely during hot conditions.*
    - 關於自由間隙若有任何偏差，請聯繫製造商。
      *In case of any deviations regarding free gaps, contact the manufacturer.*
- 安裝、裝配並點銲密封角鋼及相應之連接板。
  *Erect, fit and tack weld the sealing angles and respective connection plates.*
    - 密封角鋼位於右側與左側側壁之側壁內襯板上，並固定頂棚與地下室導流板，減少煙氣旁通流量。
      *Sealing angles are located on the sidewall liner sheeting on the right and left side wall and fixate the attic and basement baffles and reduce flue gas bypass flow.*
    - 將密封角鋼無間隙地安裝至側壁內襯板，並符合圖面。密封角鋼應與頂棚導流板接觸。
      *Fit the sealing angles to the sidewall liner sheeting without gap and as per drawing.The sealing angle shall touch the attic baffle.*
    - 安裝期間，確認密封角鋼與固定塊之實際位置並保持所需之自由間隙至關重要。
      *It is important during the installation to verify the actual position of the sealing angles and maintain the required free gap to the casing.*
    - 仔細確認預先組裝期間在密封角鋼上所作之割孔。必要時進行調整。
      *Carefully verify the cut-outs made on the sealing angles during the pre-assembly.Adjust when necessary*
    - 連接板應僅點銲且用作滑動點，如圖面所示。
      *The connection plates shall only be tack welded and used as a sliding point, as per drawing,*
    - 關於自由間隙有任何偏差，請聯繫製造商。
      *In case of any deviation regarding free gaps contact the manufacturer.*

##### 現場組件之銲接 *Welding of the field components*
- 銲接所有已安裝之現場零件。
  *Weld all installed field components.*
    - 依照圖面與 WPS 之銲接細節或型式進行。
      *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.*

##### 品質管制 *Quality control*
- 依據適用之 FQP 與/或程序執行品質管制工項。
  *Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).*
- 釋出並隨帶未完成事項清單。
  *Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).*
- 製造商組應目視檢查並審查頂棚與地下室導流板與內部內襯板之間尺寸的量測實際報告，以符合適用之公差圖面 60031-730-06-系列。
  *Manufacturer shall visually check and review the actual survey report for the measurements from the attic and basement baffles with internal liner sheeting.to be in accordance with the applicable tolerance drawings 60031-730-06-series.*

#### 8.9.5. 模組側壁煙氣導流板 *Module sidewall gas baffles*

本段落描述模組側壁煙氣導流板之安裝。
*This paragraph describes the erection of the module sidewall gas baffles.*

模組側壁煙氣導流板位於鍋爐煙道內部，沿著側壁之整個高度配置。導流板定位於配有模組之各箱體之前端與後端、以及左側與右側。
*Module sidewall gas baffles are located on the inside of the boiler duct along the complete height of the sidewalls. The baffles are positioned on the front and rear side and left and right side of each box that contains modules.*

存在不同類型之側壁煙氣導流板。關於不同類型，請參見適用之模組側壁煙氣導流板圖面與本章中之段落。
*Different kinds of sidewall gas baffles exist. For the different types, see the applicable module sidewall gas baffle drawings and the paragraphs in this chapter.*

施工方法說明書 / 風險評估以及模組側壁煙氣導流板安裝之吊裝計畫應由安裝承包商準備。
*Work method statements / risk assessments with lifting plans for the erection of the module sidewall gas baffles shall be prepared by the erection contractor.*

模組側壁煙氣導流板之安裝順序示于文件 60031-730-05-001。
*The erection sequence for the module sidewall gas baffles is shown in document 60031-730-05-001.*

在安裝模組側壁煙氣導流板之前，需提前準備一些工項。
*Before erection of the module side wall gas baffles, some activities need to be prepared in advance.*

##### 準備工作與先決條件 *Preparations and preconditions*
- 前一段落提及之文件與程序需備妥並由權責單位進行審查。
  *The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).*
- 下列準備工作/工項需已完成，若適用則需在 FQP 中簽署同意。
  *The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.*
    - 拆除所有臨時安裝之填隙片(木板)（在頂部 / 底部集管、環繞固定件、管式緩衝器與內部護肩處）。
      *Removal of all temporary erected filler plates and profiles (at top / bottom headers, wraparounds, pipe bumpers and internal shoulders).*
    - 各箱體之內部管道已吊裝。
      *Internal piping (per box) erected.*
    - 模組無任何障礙物。
      *Modules free from any obstacles.*
    - 材料已接收並檢測其數量與品質 (OSD 報告)。
      *Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report)*

##### 型式一 導流板與蓋板之安裝 *Erection of type one (1) baffles and cover plates*
- 裝配並點銲位於側壁內襯板上之導流板型鋼（帶有加強件），並將型鋼裝配在模組側。此外，將蓋板裝配在相應之導流板型鋼上。
  *Fit and tack weld the baffle profiles (with stiffeners) located on the sidewall liner sheeting and fit the profile on the module side. Also, fit the cover plates on respective baffle profiles.*
    - 遵循適用圖面之附註。
      *Follow the notes on the applicable drawings.*
    - 正確將型鋼安裝至側壁內襯板，無間隙。導流板一旦安裝，應符合圖面與模組接觸。
      *Fit the profiles correctly and without gap to the sidewall liner sheeting. The baffles once fitted, shall touch the modules as per drawing.*
    - 安裝期間，保持至頂部集管、中間緩衝器與底部緩衝器所需之自由間隙非常重要。這係為了允許運轉期間之熱膨脹。
      *During erection it is important to keep the required free gap to the top headers, the intermediate bumpers and the bottom bumpers. This to allow for thermal expansion during operation.*
    - 蓋板為滑動點，在熱態下需可自由移動。密切遵循圖面上的銲接細節。
      *The cover plates are sliding points and need to move freely during hot conditions.Closely follow the details for welding on the drawings.*
    - 關於外部空間或自由間隙有任何偏差，請聯繫製造商。
      *In case of any deviation regarding free spaces or free gaps contact the manufacturer.*

##### 型式一 導流板型鋼（帶有加強件）與蓋板之銲接 *Welding of type one (1) baffle profiles (with stiffener) and the cover plates*
- 銲接所有安裝之型鋼與蓋板。
  *Weld all erected profiles and cover plates.*
    - U 型鋼為間斷銲。
      *U-profiles are stitch welded.*
    - 帶有加強件之型鋼為塞銲，在兩個塞銲之間進行間斷銲，並在導流板端部進行間斷銲。
      *The profiles with stiffeners are plug welded, stitch welded in between two plug welds and stich welded at the baffle ends.*
    - 銲接期間，遵循圖面以確定哪一側要銲接蓋板。
      *During welding follow the drawings to determine which side to weld the cover plates.*
    - 依照圖面與 WPS 之銲接細節或型式進行。
      *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.*

##### 型式二 導流板與蓋板之安裝 *Erection of type two (2) baffles and cover plates*
此類型之側壁煙氣導流板構造由位於模組上之 U 型鋼、位於側壁內襯板上之型鋼（帶有加強件）以及位於 U 型鋼「內部」之型鋼組成。
*This type of side wall gas baffle construction consists of a U-profile located on the modules, a profile (with stiffeners) located on the sidewall liner sheeting and a profile “inside” the U-profile.*

導流板之間的間隙使用蓋板予以封閉。蓋板使用在兩個導流板上。
*Gaps between baffles are closed using cover plates. Cover plates are used on both baffles*
- 裝配並點銲位於模組側之 U 型鋼導流板。
  *Fit and tack-weld the U-profile baffles, located on the module side.*
- 裝配並點銲位於 U 型鋼上之蓋板。
  *Fit and tack-weld the cover plates, located on the U-profiles.*
    - 遵循適用圖面之附註。
      *Follow the notes on the applicable drawings.*
    - 在 U 型鋼安裝期間，監測至側壁之自由空間、至頂部集管之自由間隙、至中間緩衝器之自由間隙以及至底部緩衝器之自由間隙非常重要。這係為了允許運轉期間之熱膨脹。
      *During erection of the U-profiles it is important to monitor the free space to the sidewalls, the free gap to the top headers, the free gap to the intermediate bumpers and the free gap to the bottom bumpers.This to allow for thermal expansion during operation.*
    - 自 U 型鋼至內襯板之自由空間在整個側壁高度上需保持一致。
      *The free space from the U-profile to the liner sheeting needs to be maintained over the complete sidewall height.*
    - 蓋板為滑動點，在熱態下需可自由移動。密切遵循圖面上的銲接細節。
      *The cover plates are sliding points and need to move freely during hot conditions.Closely follow the details for welding on the drawings.*
    - 關於自由空間、間隙或尺寸有任何偏差，請聯繫製造商。
      *In case of any deviation regarding free spaces, gaps or dimensions contact manufacturer.*
- 裝配並點銲位於側壁內襯板與 U 型鋼上之加強型鋼（帶有加強件）。
  *Fit and tack-weld the profiles with stiffeners, located on the side wall liner sheeting and the U-profile.*
- 裝配並點銲位於型鋼上之蓋板。
  *Fit and tack-weld the cover plates, located on the profiles.*
    - 將型鋼正確且無間隙地安裝至側壁內襯板。
      *Fit the profiles correctly to the sidewall liner sheeting and without gap.*
    - 切勿將型鋼過緊地裝配至 U 型鋼內部。
      *Do not fit the profiles too tight into the U-profile.*
    - 安裝型鋼期間，保持給定之至頂部集管自由間隙、至中間緩衝器自由間隙以及至底部緩衝器自由間隙。這係為了允許運轉期間之熱膨脹。
      *During erection of the profile keep the given free gap to the top headers, free gap to the intermediate bumpers and free gap to the bottom bumpers. This to allow for thermal expansion during operation.*
    - 蓋板為滑動點，在熱態下需可自由移動。密切遵循圖面上的銲接細節。
      *The cover plates are sliding points and need to move freely during hot conditions.Closely follow the details for welding on the drawings.*
    - 關於自由間隙、公差或其他尺寸若有任何偏差，請聯繫製造商。
      *In case of any deviations regarding free gaps, tolerances or other dimensions, contact the manufacturer*

##### 型式二 導流板 U 型鋼（帶有加強件）與蓋板之銲接 *Welding of type two (2) baffle U-profiles (with stiffener) and the cover plates*
- 銲接所有安裝之型鋼與蓋板。
  *Weld all erected profiles and cover plates.*
    - U 型鋼間斷銲接至模組。
      *The U-profile is stitch welded to the module.*
    - 帶有加強件之型鋼為塞銲，兩塞銲之間進行間斷銲，並在導流板端部進行間斷銲。
      *The profiles with stiffeners are plug welded, stitch welded in between 2 plug welds and stich welded at the baffle ends.*
    - 密切遵循蓋板要銲接哪一側，以確保能自由移動。
      *Closely follow which side to weld for the cover plates in order to ensure free movement.*
    - 依照圖面與 WPS 之銲接細節或型式進行。
      *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.*

##### 型式三 導流板與蓋板之安裝 *Erection of type three (3) baffles and cover plates*
此類型之側壁煙氣導流板構造由位於模組上預先組裝之「門」形構件以及兩片型鋼（角鋼）組成。第一片型鋼（側壁角鋼）位於側壁內襯板上，第二片型鋼（固定角鋼）位於第一片型鋼上。在吊裝後，兩片型鋼將「預先組裝之門形導流板」鎖定在適當位置。
*This type of side wall gas baffle construction consists of a pre-assembled “door” located on the modules and two profiles (angles). The first profile (sidewall angle) is located on the sidewall liner sheeting and the second profile (fixation angle) is located on the first profile. After erection, the two profiles lock the “pre-assembled door baffle” in position).*
- 在模組上定位「門」。
  *Positioning the “doors” on the modules.*
    - 將「門」定位至正確位置，高程 90 度，公差為 0.5 度。
      *Position the “doors” to the correct position, 90 degrees with a tolerance of 0.5 degree.*
    - 安裝期間，檢查朝向內襯板之外部空間是否符合圖面說明。
      *During erection check the free space to the liner sheeting to be as mentioned on the drawing.*
    - 關於外部空間有任何偏差，請聯繫製造商。
      *In case of any deviation regarding free space, contact the manufacturer.*
- 裝配並點銲位於側壁內襯板上之側壁角鋼，並裝配及點銲蓋板。
  *Fit and tack weld the sidewall angle located on the sidewall liner sheeting and fit and tack weld the coverplates.*
    - 將側壁角鋼無間隙地安裝至側壁內襯板。
      *Fit the side wall angle profiles correctly and without gap to the sidewall liner sheeting.*
    - 安裝期間，保持給定之至頂部集管自由間隙距離、至中間緩衝器自由間隙、至底部緩衝器自由間隙以及「門」與「門」之間自由間隙非常重要。
      *During erection it is important to keep the given free gap distance to the top headers, the free gap to the intermediate bumpers, the free gap to the bottom bumpers and the free gap between the “doors”.*
    - 蓋板為滑動點，在熱態下需可自由移動。密切遵循圖面上的銲接細節。
      *The cover plates are sliding points and need to move freely during hot conditions.Closely follow the details for welding on the drawings.*
    - 關於自由間隙有任何偏差，請聯繫製造商。
      *In case of any deviation regarding free gaps contact the manufacturer.*
- 在側壁角鋼上裝配並點銲固定角鋼。
  *Fit and tack weld the fixation angle profiles on the sidewall angle profiles.*
    - 將固定角鋼無間隙地安裝至側壁角鋼。
      *Fit the fixation angle profile correctly to the sidewall angle profile and without gap.*
    - 安裝固定角鋼期間，保持給定之「門」與「門」之間自由間隙。
      *During erection of the fixation angle profile maintain the given free gap between the “doors”.*
    - 關於自由間隙有任何偏差，請聯繫製造商。
      *In case of any deviation regarding free gaps contact the manufacturer.*

##### 型式三 導流板型鋼與蓋板之銲接 *Welding of type three (3) baffle profiles and cover plates*
- 銲接所有安裝之側壁與固定角鋼型鋼。
  *Weld all erected sidewall and fixation angle profiles.*
    - 與內襯板連接之側壁角鋼為塞銲與間斷銲。
      *Sidewall angles profiles connected to the liner sheeting are plug and stich welded.*
    - 固定角鋼為塞銲，且在兩個孔之間進行間斷銲。
      *Fixation angles are plug welded and stitch welded between 2 holes.*
    - 密切遵循蓋板要銲接哪一側，以確保能自由移動。
      *Closely follow which side to weld for the cover plates in order to ensure free movement.*
    - 依照圖面與 WPS 之銲接細節或型式進行。
      *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.*

##### 品質管制 *Quality control*
- 依據適用之 FQP 與/或程序執行品質管制工項。
  *Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).*
    - 銲接前檢查所有自由間隙與公差。
      *Check all free gaps and tolerances before welding.*
    - 製造商阻應目視檢查並審查模組側壁煙氣導流板之量測實際報告，以符合適用之公差圖面 60031-730-06-系列。
      *Manufacturer shall visually check and review the actual survey report for the measurements from the module side wall gas baffles to be in accordance with the applicable tolerance drawings 60031-730-06-series.*
    - 釋出並隨帶未完成事項清單。
      *Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).*

#### 8.9.6. 導流板(Flow baffle) *Flow baffle*

本段落描述導流板(Flow baffle)之安裝。
*This paragraph describes the erection of the flow baffles.*

此導流板經由覆蓋進口煙道底部保溫與 E 軸底部緩衝器之間的開口，防止煙氣進入箱體 1 前方的熱箱區域。
*This baffle prevents flue gasses from entering the hot box area in front of box 1, by covering the opening between the inlet duct bottom insulation and the bottom bumper in axis E.*

施工方法說明書 / 風險評估以及導流板(Flow baffle)安裝之吊裝計畫應由安裝承包商準備。
*Work method statements / risk assessments with lifting plans for the erection of the flow baffle shall be prepared by the erection contractor.*

導流板(Flow baffle)之安裝順序示于文件 60031-730-05-001。
*The erection sequence for the flow baffle is shown in document 60031-730-05-001.*

在安裝導流板(Flow baffle)之前，需提前準備一些工項。
*Before erection of the flow baffle, some activities need to be prepared in advance.*

##### 準備工作與先決條件 *Preparations and preconditions*
- 前一段落提及之文件與程序需備妥並由權責單位進行審查。
  *The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).*
- 下列準備工作/工項需已完成，若適用則需在 FQP 中簽署同意。
  *The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.*
    - 進口煙道已吊裝，包括 E 軸前方之垂直板。
      *Inlet duct erected, including vertical panel in front of axis E.*
    - 進口煙道熱箱管道已吊裝。
      *Inlet duct hot box piping erected.*
    - 材料已接收並檢測其數量與品質 (OSD 報告)。
      *Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report)*

##### 導流板(Flow baffle)之安裝 *Erection of flow baffle*
- 將滑動支撐安裝在垂直爐殼皮組件之管式緩衝器上，並將導流板(Flow baffle)放置在滑動支撐與 E 軸底部緩衝器頂部。
  *Fit the sliding supports over the pipe bumpers of the vertical casing panels and place the flow baffles on top of the sliding support and bottom bumper of axis E.*
    - 遵循適用圖面之附註。
      *Follow the notes on the applicable drawings.*
    - 將型鋼正確且無間隙地安裝至橫向緩衝器。導流板一旦安裝，應符合圖面與緩衝器接觸。
      *Fit the profiles correctly and without gap to the transverse bumper. The baffles once fitted, shall touch the bumpers as per drawing.*
    - 安裝期間，保持至垂直板保溫材所需之自由間隙非常重要。這係為了允許運轉期間之熱膨脹。
      *During erection it is important to keep the required free gap to the insulation sheeting of the vertical panel. This to allow for thermal expansion during operation.*
    - 滑動點在熱態下需可自由移動（切勿銲接至管式緩衝器！）。
      *The sliding points need to move freely during hot conditions (no welding to the pipe bumpers!).*
    - 關於外部空間或自由間隙有任何偏差，請聯繫製造商。
      *In case of any deviation regarding free spaces or free gaps contact the manufacturer.*

##### 導流板(Flow baffle)之銲接 *Welding of the flow baffles*
- 銲接所有導流板(Flow baffle)。
  *Weld all flow baffles.*
    - 依照圖面與 WPS 之銲接細節或型式進行。
      *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.*
    - 銲接前檢查所有自由間隙。
      *Check all free gaps before welding.*

##### 導流板(Flow baffle)密封角鋼 *Sealing angles flow baffles*
- 在垂直外殼板（箱體 1 前方）處安裝、裝配並點銲密封角鋼。
  *Erect, fit and tack weld the sealing angles at vertical casing panel (in front of box 1).*
    - 密封板應以使導流板(Flow baffle)在熱態下能自由移動之方式安裝。
      *Sealing plates shall be erected in such a way that the flow baffle can move freely during hot conditions.*
    - 關於自由間隙若有任何偏差，請聯繫製造商。
      *In case of any deviations regarding free gaps, contact the manufacturer.*
- 安裝、裝配並點銲密封角鋼及相應之連接板。
  *Erect, fit and tack weld the sealing angles and respective connection plates.*
    - 密封角鋼位於箱體 1 前方之垂直外殼板內襯板上，將氣流自進口煙道底部板引導至導流板(Flow baffle)，以減少煙氣旁通流量。
      *Sealing angles are located on the vertical casing panel liner sheeting in front of box 1, guiding gas flow from inlet duct bottom panel onto the flow baffle, to reduce flue gas bypass flow.*
    - 將密封角鋼無間隙地安裝至內襯板，並符合圖面。密封角鋼應與導流板(Flow baffle)接觸。
      *Fit the sealing angles to the liner sheeting without gap and as per drawing. The sealing angle shall touch the flow baffle.*
    - 安裝期間，確認密封角鋼與固定夾之實際位置並保持所需之自由間隙至關重要。
      *It is important during the erection to verify the actual position of the sealing angles and the fixation clips and maintain the required free gaps.*
    - 關於自由間隙有任何偏差，請聯繫製造商。
      *In case of any deviation regarding free gaps contact the manufacturer.*

##### 密封角鋼之銲接 *Welding of the sealing angles*
- 銲接所有已安裝之現場零件。
  *Weld all installed field components.*
    - 依照圖面與 WPS 之銲接細節 or 型式進行。
      *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.*
    - 確保組裝件之自由間隙與膨脹可能性。
      *Ensure free gap and expansion possibilities of the assembly.*

##### 品質管制 *Quality control*
- 依據適用之 FQP 與/或程序執行品質管制工項。
  *Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).*
- 釋出並隨帶未完成事項清單。
  *Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).*
- 製造商組應目視檢查並審查頂棚與地下室導流板與內部內襯板之間尺寸的量測實際報告，以符合適用之公差圖面 60031-730-06-系列。
  *Manufacturer shall visually check and review the actual survey report for the measurements from the attic and basement baffles with internal liner sheeting.to be in accordance with the applicable tolerance drawings 60031-730-06-series.*

#### 8.9.7. 熱回收鍋爐導流板與密封板之最終檢查 *Final inspection of the HRSG baffles and sealing plates*

當特定系統 or 一組特定組件之機械安裝完成後，應進行檢查。未完成項目應彙整於未完成項目清單中，並附於最終檢查合格證上。
*When the mechanical erection of a certain system, or group of specific components is finalized these shall be inspected. Outstanding items shall be collected in an outstanding items list and attached to the Final inspection Certificate.*

熱回收鍋爐導流板與密封板之最終檢查合格書描述了所檢查之系統或組件。
*The Final inspection Certificate of the HRSG baffles and sealing plates describes the systems or components inspected.*

##### 檢查 *Inspection*
- 最終檢查合格書上提及之所有系統或特定組件組應進行正確安裝、完整性與損壞之最終檢查。
  *All systems or group of specific components referred to on the Final inspection Certificate shall have a final inspection for correct erection, completeness and damages.*
- 在步行檢視後應立即建立未完成項目紀錄（如有）。
  *A record of outstanding items (if any) shall be set-up directly after the walk-down.*
- 若有未完成項目清單適用，其應分類為：
  *In case a list of outstanding items is applicable it shall be categorized in :*
    - 於水壓試驗前需解決之項目（A 級項目）
      *Items to be solved before hydro testing (A-items)*
    - 於熱試運轉前需解決之項目（B 級項目）
      *Items to be solved before hot-commissioning (B-items)*
    - 於初期驗收前需解決之項目（C 級項目）
      *Items to be solved before provisional acceptance (PAC) (C-items)*
- 確認所涉及系統之適用現場 FQP 已由所有涉入方簽署同意。未完成項目應納入未決點清單。
  *Verify that the applicable site FQPs for the systems involved are signed off by all parties involved. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list*
- 確認所有不符合事項報告已關閉。未完成項目應納入未決點清單。
  *Verify that all Non-Conformity Reports are closed. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list*

## 9. SCR 系統 *SCR SYSTEMS*

本章包含以下段落：
*This chapter contains the following paragraphs:*

1. SCR 煙道底部與側壁爐殼：第 9.1 節
   *Bottom and side wall casing SCR duct : paragraph 9.1*
2. AIG / SCR 系統：第 9.2 節
   *AIG / SCR system : paragraph 9.2*
3. SCR 煙道頂部爐殼：第 9.3 節
   *Top wall casing SCR duct : paragraph 9.3*

### 9.1. SCR 煙道底部與側壁爐殼 *Bottom and side wall casing SCR duct*

#### 9.1.1. 一般 *General*

AIG / SCR 爐殼（底部與側壁爐殼）安裝之施工方法說明書 / 風險評估以及吊裝計畫應由安裝承包商準備。
*Work method statements / risk assessments with lifting plans for the erection of the AIG / SCR casing (bottom and side wall casing) shall be prepared by the Erection contractor.*

外殼板之安裝順序示于文件 60028-730-05-001。
*The erection sequence for casing panels is shown in document 60028-730-05-001.*

#### 9.1.2. 燃燒器與煙道爐殼安裝之文件與程序 *Documents and procedures for Burner and duct casing erection*

需由下列單位核准、審查、接受與釋出：
*To be approved, reviewed, accepted and released by*

業主 *Client*
- 安裝承包商已核准與審查之項目：
  *Approved and reviewed from erection contractor:*
    - 施工方法說明書：安裝鍋爐外殼板。
      *Work method statement  : Erection boiler casing panels*
    - 施工方法說明書：安裝高空作業平台（鍋爐內部）。
      *Work method statement : Erection elevated work platform (inside boiler)*
    - 施工方法說明書：安裝鍋爐爐殼施工施工架。
      *Work method statement : Erection scaffolding boiler casing*
    - 銲接作業程序書 / 銲接程序資格檢定紀錄 / 銲工資格檢定：非受壓組件。
      *WPS / PQR / WPQ : Non-pressure parts*
    - 銲接地圖 / 紀錄：非受壓組件。
      *Weld typical / record : Non-pressure parts*
    - 銲接耗材處理程序書：非受壓組件。
      *Welding consumable handling procedure : Non-pressure parts*
    - 非破壞檢測程序書 / 人員資格認證：非受壓組件。
      *NDE procedures / personnel qualifications : Non-pressure parts*
- 接受：*Acceptance:*
    - 外殼板安裝之準備：鍋爐爐殼現場組裝施工旅程表。
      *Preparation for erection of casing panels : Site assembly traveller boiler casing*
- 釋出：*Release:*
    - 外殼板之安裝：鍋爐爐殼現場組裝施工旅程表。
      *Erection of casing panels : Site assembly traveller boiler casing*

製造商 *Manufacturer*
- 不適用。
  *N.A.*

#### 9.1.3. 外殼板安裝之前置準備工作 *Preparation casing panels erection*

在外殼板安裝之前與期間，需提前準備一些工項。
*Before and during erection of the casing panels, some activities need to be prepared in advance.*

在外殼板安裝之同時，亦可進行其他工項。
*Parallel to the erection of casing panels other activities can be carried out.*

##### 準備工作 *Preparation*
- 進入鍋爐「底部內部」之施工施工架。
  *Scaffolding for access to the boiler “bottom inside”.*
    - 在開始安裝底部外殼板之前，準備用於進入鍋爐「底部內部」之施工施工架。
      *Before erection of the bottom casing panels can start, prepare scaffolding for access to the boiler “bottom inside”.*
    - 將施工施工架搭建在主鋼構鋼柱之外側。施工施工架需自地面層搭建至底部橫梁之頂部。
      *Place the scaffolding on the outside of the main steel columns. Scaffolding to be built-up from ground level to the top of the bottom girder.*
    - 提供自鍋爐左側與右側之通道。
      *Provide access from both the left and right side of the boiler.*
- 在底部外殼板上使用並鋪設保護夾板。
  *Use and apply plywood on the bottom casing panels.*
    - 在主鋼構鋼柱預組裝期間，準備（用於保護底部外殼板之）夾板。
      *Prepare the plywood panels (for protection of the bottom panels) during the pre-assembly of the main steel columns for the boiler main steel.*
    - 為避免損壞鍋爐底部外殼板之內襯板，請使用夾板進行保護。在安裝底部板期間搭設夾板。
      *To avoid damaging of the boiler casing panels liner sheeting use plywood panels. Erect the plywood panels during erection of the bottom panels.*
    - 在對齊與銲接工項期間打開夾板，但保持各板之間儘可能密合。
      *Open the plywood panels during the fit-up and weld activities, but keep the panels as far as closed to each other as possible.*
    - 底部板上之夾板需保持在原位（在內襯板上），直至施工階段結束。
      *Plywood on the bottom panels needs to be in place (on the liner sheeting) until the end of the construction phase.*
    - 在完成內部底部爐殼後，修改夾板，使其在後續安裝期間能「保護地面」。
      *After finalizing the inside bottom casing, modify the plywood in such a way that the “floor is protected” during further erection.*
    - 在夾板上切割供管道施工作業之孔洞，並在相關管道安裝完成前將孔洞封閉。
      *Cut holes in the plywood for piping activities and close the holes until the relevant piping is erected.*
- 高空作業平台（在安裝底部外殼之後，以及在安裝側壁爐殼期間或之後）。
  *Elevated platform (after erection of the bottom casing and during or after the erection of the sidewall casing).*
    - 鍋爐內部之高空作業平台（吊籠）對於在爐殼側壁保溫現場銜接縫處安裝內部保溫非常有用。
      *An elevated working platform (man basket) on the inside of the boiler is useful for erection of internal insulation at the casing sidewall insulation field splices.*
    - 高空工作平台之安裝可在側壁外殼板安裝期間開始。
      *Erection of the elevated platforms can commence during sidewall casing panel erection.*
    - 高空工作平台需安裝在鍋爐兩側（右側 / 左側），以提供沿鍋爐側壁整個長度與高度之妥善通道。
      *Elevated platforms to be erected on both sides (right / left side) of the boiler in such a way that proper access along the complete length and height of the boiler sidewalls can be provided.*

#### 9.1.4. SCR 煙道底部外殼板之安裝 *Erection bottom casing panels SCR duct*

安裝 AIG / SCR 煙道之剩餘橫梁與 HRSG 底部外殼板，藉此完成 HRSG 底部地板結構。
*Erect the remaining HRSG bottom casing panels for the AIG / SCR duct, therewith completing the HRSG bottom floor structure.*

底部外殼板安裝前提：
*Bottom panels erection after*
- 文件與程序：*Documents and procedures:*
    - 已核准與審查。
      *Approved and reviewed*
- 接受：*Acceptance:*
    - 底部外殼板安裝準備工作就緒。
      *Preparation for erection bottom casing panels ready*
    - 模組已安裝完成。
      *Modules erected*
- 釋出：*Release:*
    - AIG / SCR 煙道底部外殼板之安裝。
      *Erection bottom casing panels SCR duct*

##### 安裝 *Erection*
- 安裝、裝配並點銲底部外殼板。
  *Erect, fit and tack-weld the bottom wall casing panels.*
    - 安裝前，拆除爐殼穿透孔處之保護塑料與保溫保護棉。使用刀具妥善切割塑料與保溫棉。切勿用力拉扯。
      *Before erection, remove the plastic and insulation wool from the casing penetrations. Properly cut the plastic and wool using a knife. Do not pull it out using force.*
    - 將鋼板對齊至正確位置，並用螺栓將 U 型槽鋼鎖緊至主鋼構大梁上。若為銲接連接，則在對齊後將鋼板點銲至主鋼構架上。
      *Align the panel to the correct position and bolt the U-channels to the main steel girders. In case of welded connections tack-weld the panel to main steel structure after alignment.*
    - 切除底部鋼板上之內部保溫防護塑料。
      *Cut away the internal insulation protection plastic from the bottom panels.*
    - 裝配並點銲各鋼板，確保無間隙。依圖面要求於適當處使用填隙片（加強襯墊板）。
      *Fit and tack-weld the panels without gap. Use filler plates where required as per drawing.*
    - 在點銲期間，使用銲接護毯覆蓋保溫棉以進行火花防護。
      *During tack-welding, cover the insulation wool using weld blankets for spark protection.*
    - 安裝剩餘部位之螺栓與螺帽。若發現螺栓孔對位不良，需與製造商諮商後始可進行調整。
      *Erect the remaining bolts and nuts. When a misalignment of bolt holes is detected, adjustment can be made only after consultation with the manufacturer.*
    - 使用斜度墊圈將 U 型槽鋼連接至底部大梁。
      *Use taper washers for the connection of the U-channels to the bottom girder.*

##### 底部外殼板銜接縫之銲接 *Welding splices bottom casing panels*
- 銲接底部外殼板現場銜接縫。
  *Weld the bottom casing panel field splices*
    - 所有外部銲接應為連續銲，外部不允許進行間斷銲（跳銲）。
      *All external welds shall be continuous, no stitch welds on the outside allowed.*
    - 僅在內部接頭上允許進行間斷銲（若適用），尺寸請參見圖面細節。
      *Stitch welds are only allowed on the inside joints if applicable, for dimensions see the details on drawings.*
    - 所有槽鋼端部之銲接應為連續銲。
      *For all channel ends the welds shall be continuous.*
    - 依照圖面與 WPS 之銲接細節或型式進行。
      *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.*
    - 在銲接期間，使用銲接護毯覆蓋保溫棉以進行火花防護。
      *During welding, cover the insulation wool using weld blankets for spark protection.*

##### 底部外殼板之現場組件 *Field parts bottom casing panels*
- 安裝、裝配並點銲所有必要之現場組件。
  *Erect, fit and tack-weld all necessary field parts.*
    - 底部外殼板之現場組件可為填隙片、導向板與加強板。依據圖面指示識別所有需要之現場組件。
      *Field parts for the bottom casing panels can be filler, guide and stiffener plates. Identify all required field parts as indicated on the drawings.*
    - 遵循現場零件圖面上之型式銲接要求。
      *Follow the requirements of the weld typical on the field part drawings.*
    - 角隅處與現場銜接處之所有間隙均需使用填隙片（厚度 6 mm）予以密合（密封銲）。
      *All gaps at corners and field splices have to be closed (seal welded) using filler plates (6 mm thickness).*

##### 底部外殼板現場組件之銲接 *Welding field parts bottom casing panels*
- 銲接所有已安裝之現場組件。
  *Weld all erected field parts.*
    - 所有外部銲接應為連續銲，外部不允許進行間斷銲。
      *All external welds shall be continuous, no stitch welding on the outside allowed.*
    - 依照圖面之銲接細節或型式進行。
      *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings.*

##### 底部外殼板角隅連接 *Corner connections bottom casing panels*
- 使用角鋼或扁鋼連接安裝、裝配並點銲所有角隅連接。經由查閱安裝圖面以確定使用何種類型。
  *Erect, fit and tack-weld all corner connections using angle or flat bar connections. Verify the erection drawings to determine which type to use.*
    - 將角鋼連接對齊至外殼板，且無間隙。
      *Align the angle bar connections to the casing panels without gap.*
    - 角鋼交叉部位與連接點之安裝需採用正確之銲接坡口準備，細節參見圖面。
      *Angle bar cross sections and connection points need to be erected using the correct weld preparation, for details see the drawings.*

##### 底部外殼板角隅連接之銲接 *Welding corner connections bottom panels*
- 銲接所有角鋼或扁鋼連接。
  *Weld all angle or flat bar connections.*
    - 所有外部銲接應為連續銲，外部不允許進行間斷銲。
      *All external welds shall be continuous, no stitch welds on the outside allowed.*
    - 在銲接期間，使用銲接護毯覆蓋保溫棉以進行火花防護。
      *During welding, cover the insulation wool using weld blankets for spark protection.*
    - 依照圖面與 WPS 之銲接細節或型式進行。
      *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.*
    - 在銲接期間，使用銲接護毯覆蓋保溫棉以進行火花防護。
      *During welding, cover the insulation wool using weld blankets for spark protection.*

##### 業主品質管制 *Quality control client*
- 底部外殼板之品質管制依據：
  *Quality control for the bottom casing panels is based on:*
    - 鍋爐爐殼現場組裝品質計畫書。
      *Site assembly FQP boiler casing*
- 接受：*Acceptance:*
    - SCR 煙道底部外殼板之安裝。
      *Erection bottom casing panels SCR duct*
- 釋出：*Release:*
    - 底部現場銜接縫之內部保溫與內襯板安裝。
      *Internal insulation and liner sheeting bottom field splices*
    - 燃燒器與 SCR 煙道側壁外殼板之安裝。
      *Erection sidewall casing panels Burner and SCR duct*
    - 銲接前檢查底部外殼板之裝配情況。
      *Check fit-up of the bottom panels before welding.*
    - 釋出內部保溫之安裝（無任何未完成項目清單為原則，如有則需列出）。
      *Erection of the internal insulation after release without a list of outstanding items (if any).*

#### 9.1.5. SCR 煙道側壁外殼板之安裝 *Erection side wall casing panels SCR duct.*

安裝 SCR 煙道之側壁外殼板，藉此完成 HRSG 側壁結構。
*Erect the sidewall casing panels for the SCR duct, therewith completing the HRSG sidewall structure.*

側壁外殼板安裝前提：
*Side wall casing panels erection after*
- 文件與程序：*Documents and procedures:*
    - 已核准與審查。
      *Approved and reviewed*
- 接受：*Acceptance:*
    - SCR 煙道底部外殼板之安裝就緒。
      *Erection bottom casing panels SCR duct*
- 釋出：*Release:*
    - SCR 煙道側壁外殼板之安裝。
      *Erection side wall casing panels SCR duct*

##### 安裝側壁外殼板 *Erection side wall casing panels*
- 安裝、裝配並點銲側壁外殼板。
  *Erect, fit and tack-weld the side wall casing panels.*
    - 安裝前，拆除爐殼穿透孔處之塑料防護套與保溫保護棉。使用刀具妥善切割塑料與保溫棉。切勿用力拉扯。
      *Before erection, remove the plastic and insulation wool from the casing penetrations. Properly cut the plastic and wool using a knife and do not pull it out using force.*
    - 將側壁外殼板定位至正確位置並對齊。
      *Position and align the side wall casing panels to the correct position.*
    - 確認圖面上指示之裝配高程與公差。
      *Verify fit-up elevations and tolerances as indicated on the drawings.*
    - 切除側壁外殼板上之內部保溫防護塑料。
      *Cut away the internal insulation protection plastic from the side wall casing panels.*
    - 將鋼板裝配並點銲至對齊位置。
      *Fit and tack-weld the panels to the aligned position.*
    - 在點銲期間，使用銲接護毯覆蓋保溫棉以進行火花防護。
      *During tack welding, cover the insulation wool using weld blankets for spark protection.*

##### 側壁外殼板之銲接 *Welding of the side wall casing panels*
- 銲接側壁外殼板。
  *Weld the sidewall panels.*
    - 切除側壁板之內部保溫防護塑料。
      *Cut away the internal insulation protection plastic from the sidewall panels.*
    - 所有外部銲接應為連續銲，外部不允許進行間斷銲。
      *All external welds shall be continuous, no stitch welding on the outside allowed.*
    - 僅在圖面指示之內部接頭處允許進行間斷銲，其尺寸詳見圖面細節。
      *Stitch welding is only allowed on the inside joints where indicated on the drawings, for dimensions see the details on the drawings.*
    - 依照圖面與 WPS 之銲接細節或型式進行。
      *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.*
    - 在銲接期間，使用銲接護毯覆蓋保溫棉以進行火花防護。
      *During welding, cover the insulation wool using weld blankets for spark protection.*

##### 側壁外殼板之現場組件 *Field parts side wall casing panels*
- 安裝、裝配並點銲側壁外殼板所有必要之現場組件。
  *Erect, fit and tack-weld all necessary field parts for the side wall casing panels.*
    - 側壁外殼板之現場組件可為填隙片、導向板、加強支撐板與 U 型槽鋼。識別所有在圖面上指示之必要現場組件。
      *Field parts for the side wall casing panels can be filler, guide, stiffener plates and U-channels, identify all required field parts as indicated on the drawings.*
    - 導向板 / 加強板 / U 型槽鋼之交叉點與連接點，需採用正確之銲接坡口準備進行安裝。
      *Cross- and connection points of guide plates / stiffeners / U-channels need to be erected using the correct weld preparation.*
    - 角隅處與現場銜接縫處之所有間隙，均應使用填隙片（厚度 6 mm）進行密合（密封銲）。
      *All gaps at corners and field splices have to be closed (seal welded) using filler plates (6 mm thickness).*

##### 側壁外殼板現場組件之銲接 *Welding of the field parts for the side wall casing panels*
- 銲接所有側壁外殼板已安裝之現場組件。
  *Weld all erected field parts for the side wall casing panels.*
    - 依照圖面與 WPS 之銲接細節或型式進行。
      *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.*
    - 所有外部銲接應為連續銲，外部不允許進行間斷銲。
      *All external welds shall be continuous, no stitch welds on the outside allowed.*

##### 側壁外殼板之角隅連接 *Corner connections side wall casing panels*
- 使用角鋼或扁鋼連接安裝、裝配並點銲所有角隅連接。經由查閱安裝圖面以確定使用何種類型。
  *Erect, fit and tack-weld all corner connections using angle or flat bar connections. Verify the erection drawings to determine which type to use.*
    - 將角鋼或扁鋼連接件緊貼至外殼板，且無間隙。
      *Align the angle bar or flat bar connections to the casing panels without gap.*
    - 角鋼之交叉部位與連接點，需採用正確之銲接坡口準備進行安裝，細節詳見圖面。
      *Angle bar cross sections and connection points need to be erected using the correct weld preparation, for details see the drawings.*

##### 底部與側壁外殼板之間角隅連接之銲接 *Welding corner connections between bottom and side wall casing panels*
- 銲接所有角鋼或扁鋼連接。
  *Weld all angle or flat bar connections.*
    - 所有外部銲接應為連續銲，外部不允許進行間斷銲。
      *All external welds shall be continuous, no stitch welds on the outside allowed.*
    - 在銲接期間，使用銲接護毯覆蓋保溫棉以進行火花防護。
      *During welding, cover the insulation wool using weld blankets for spark protection.*
    - 依照圖面與 WPS 之銲接細節或型式進行。
      *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.*
    - 在銲接期間，使用銲接護毯覆蓋保溫棉以進行火花防護。
      *During welding, cover the insulation wool using weld blankets for spark protection.*

##### 業主品質管制 *Quality control client*
- 側壁外殼板安裝之品質管制依據：
  *Quality control for erection of the side wall casing panels is based on:*
    - 鍋爐爐殼現場組裝品質計畫書。
      * Site assembly FQP boiler casing*
- 接受：*Acceptance:*
    - SCR 煙道側壁外殼板之安裝。
      *Erection side wall casing panels SCR duct*
- 釋出：*Release:*
    - SCR 煙道側壁外殼板之保溫與內襯板工程。
      *Insulation and liner sheeting side wall casing panels SCR duct*
    - 銲接前，經常檢查外殼板與現場零組件之對齊與裝配情況。
      *Frequently check the fit-up for the casing panels and field part before welding.*
    - 釋出內部保溫之施工（以無任何未完成項目清單為原則）。
      *Release for internal insulation without a list of outstanding items.*

#### 9.1.6. 底部與側壁爐殼之內部保溫與內襯板 *Internal insulation and liner sheeting bottom and side wall casing*

    - 釋出內部保溫之安裝（以無任何未完成項目清單為原則，如有則需列出）。

### 9.2. AIG / SCR 系統 *AIG / SCR System*

#### 9.2.1. 一般 *General*

氨噴射系統 (AIG) 由以下組件構成：
*The AIG (Ammonia Injection Grid) system consists of:*
- AIG 支撐框架，含支撐件（鍋爐內部部件）
  *AIG supporting frame including supports (internal)*
- AIG 噴嘴管（鍋爐內部部件）
  *AIG injection lances (internal)*
- AIG 外部管道
  *AIG external piping*
- AIG 設備鞍座架板 (AIG Skid)
  *AIG Skid*

選擇性觸媒還原 (SCR) 系統由以下組件構成：
*The SCR (Selective Catalyst Reduction) system consists of:*
- SCR 支撐框架，含支撐件（內部部件）
  *SCR supporting frame including supports (internal)*
- SCR 觸媒積木塊（內部部件）（於初次點火運轉後安裝）
  *SCR catalyst blocks (internal) (erection after first fire)*
- 旁通煙氣導流板（內部部件）
  *By-pass flow baffling (internal)*

安裝 AIG / SCR 系統之施工方法說明書 / 風險評估以及吊裝計畫應由安裝承包商準備。
*Work method statements / risk assessments with lifting plans for the erection of the AIG / SCR systems shall be prepared by the Erection contractor.*

#### 9.2.2. 安裝順序 *Erection sequence*

AIG / SCR 系統之安裝順序示于文件 60028-730-05-001。
*The erection sequence for the AIG / SCR systems is shown in document 60028-730-05-001.*

#### 9.2.3. AIG / SCR 系統安裝之文件與程序 *Documents and procedures for erection of the AIG / SCR system*

需由下列單位核准、審查、接受與釋出：
*To be approved, reviewed, accepted and released by*

業主*Client*
- 安裝承包商已核准與審查之項目：
  *Approved and reviewed from the erection contractor:*
    - 施工方法說明書：安裝 AIG 系統。
      *Work method statement : Erection AIG system*
    - 施工方法說明書：安裝 SCR 系統。
      *Work method statement : Erection SCR system*
    - 施工方法說明書：現場搭建鍋爐內部施工施工架。
      *Work method statement  : Erection scaffolding HRSG inside*
    - 銲接作業程序書 / 銲接程序資格檢定紀錄 / 銲工資格檢定：非受壓組件。
      *WPS / PQR / WPQ : Non-pressure parts*
    - 銲接地圖 / 紀錄：非受壓組件。
      *Weld typical / record : Non-pressure parts*
    - 銲接耗材處理程序書：非受壓組件。
      *Welding consumable handling procedure : Non-pressure parts*
    - 非破壞檢測程序書 / 人員資格認證：非受壓組件。
      *NDE procedures / personnel qualifications : Non-pressure parts*
- 接受：*Acceptance:*
    - AIG 或 SCR 爐殼箱體（底部與側壁）。：爐殼現場組裝檢驗計畫書 (ITP)。
      *Side and bottom wall casing SCR box. : Site assembly ITP casing*
- 釋出：*Release:*
    - AIG 系統之安裝：SCR 系統現場組裝施工品質計畫書 (FQP)。
      *Erection AIG system : Site assembly FQP SCR system*
    - SCR 系統之安裝：SCR 系統現場組裝施工品質計畫書 (FQP)。
      *Erection SCR system : Site assembly FQP SCR system*

#### 9.2.4. AIG 系統 *AIG system*

在開始安裝內部之 AIG 系統之前，需提前準備一些工項。
*Before erection of the AIG system inside can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance.*

##### 前置準備工作 *Preparation*
- 確認 AIG 穿透孔與支撐件在爐殼上之正確定位與高程。
  *Verification of the correct positioning of the AIG piping casing penetrations and supports.*
- 用於安裝 AIG 及其支撐鋼架零件之吊裝設備與機具。
  *Lifting equipment for the erection of the AIG and supporting frame parts.*
    - 在安裝 AIG 支撐框架之前，進行爐殼穿透管件之尺寸與高程測量。
      *Before erection of the AIG supporting frame, take measurements (elevation) of the casing penetrations.*
    - 若有任何偏差且需要進行調整，請在這種情況下諮商製造商。
      *In case of deviations and adjustments are required, consult the manufacturer in this case.*

##### AIG 系統之安裝前提 *AIG system erection after*
- 文件與程序：*Documents and procedures:*
    - 已核准與審查。
      *Approved and reviewed*
- 接受：*Acceptance:*
    - SCR 煙道側壁外殼板之保溫與內襯板工程已接受。
      *Insulation and liner sheeting side wall casing panels SCR duct*
- 釋出：*Release:*
    - AIG 外部管道之施工。
      *AIG piping (external)*

##### 內部安裝 *Erection (inside)*
- 安裝 AIG 支撐框與 AIG 內部管道。
  *Erect the AIG supporting frame and AIG piping.*
    - 密切遵循 AIG 供應商提供之安裝說明，此說明由安裝手冊與製造商安裝圖面組成。
      *Follow the AIG supplier erection instructions, which consist out of an erection manual and manufacturer erection drawings.*

##### 銲接 *Welding*
- 遵循供應商相關之銲接說明。
  *Follow the relevant supplier instructions for welding.*
    - 依照圖面與 WPS 之銲接細節或型式進行。
      *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.*

##### 業主品質管制 *Quality control client*
- 內部 AIG 系統安裝之品質管制依據：
  *Quality control for erection of the AIG system inside is based on:*
    - 鍋爐 SCR 系統現場組裝施工品質計畫書。
      *Site assembly FQP SCR system boiler*
- 接受：*Acceptance:*
    - AIG 系統內部安裝。
      *Erection AIG system (inside)*
- 釋出：*Release:*
    - AIG 外部管道。
      *AIG piping (external)*
    - 安裝期間檢查所需之公差。
      *During erection check the required tolerances.*
    - 釋出並隨帶未完成事項清單。
      *Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).*
    - AIG 系統管道之安裝應依據「管道系統」章節進行。遵循該章節中提及之安裝與品質步驟。
      *AIG system piping to be erected based on Chapter “Piping”. Follow the erection and quality steps mentioned in this chapter.*

#### 9.2.5. SCR 系統 *SCR system*

在開始內部 SCR 系統安裝之前，需提前準備一些工項。
*Before erection of the SCR system inside can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance.*

##### 前置準備工作 *Preparation*
- 確認觸媒單元支撐座之正確定位與安裝完工。
  *Verification of the correct positioning and erection of the element supports.*
- 用於安裝 SCR 支撐框架零件之吊裝設備物料。
  *Lifting equipment for the erection of the SCR supporting frame parts.*
    - 在安裝 SCR 系統之前，測量兩側（右側和左側）之支撐高程。
      *Before erection of the SCR system, take measurements (elevation) of the supports on the right – and left side.*
    - 若有任何偏差且需要進行調整，請在這種情況下諮商製造商。
      *In case of deviations and adjustments are required, consult the manufacturer in this case.*

##### SCR 系統之安裝前提 *SCR system erection after*
- 文件與程序：
  *Documents and procedures:*
    - 已核准與審查。
      *Approved and reviewed*
- 接受：*Acceptance:*
    - SCR 煙道側壁板之保溫與內襯板。
      *Insulation and liner sheeting sidewall casing panels SCR duct*
- 釋出：*Release:*
    - SCR 系統（內部）之安裝。
      *Erection SCR system (inside)*

##### 內部安裝 *Erection (inside)*
- 安裝內部支撐、SCR 支撐鋼架以及煙氣導流板組件。
  *Erect the supports, SCR supporting frame and gas baffle parts.*
    - 密切遵循相關供應商之安裝說明，此說明由安裝手冊與製造商安裝圖面構成。
      *Follow the relevant supplier erection instructions, which consist out of an erection manual and manufacturer erection drawings.*
    - 僅在首次點火運轉後，始可進行 SCR 觸媒積木塊之安裝。參見製造商之試運轉說明書。
      *Erection off the SCR catalyst blocks only after first fire. See the manufacturer commissioning manual.*

##### 銲接 *Welding*
- 遵循供應商相關之銲接說明。
  *Follow the relevant supplier instructions for welding.*
    - 依照圖面與 WPS 之銲接細節或型式進行。
      *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.*

##### 業主品質管制 *Quality control client*
- 內部 SCR 系統安裝之品質管制依據：
  *Quality control for erection of the SCR system inside is based on:*
    - 鍋爐 SCR 系統現場組裝之檢驗及品質計畫 (ITP)。
      *Site assembly ITP SCR system boiler*
- 接受：*Acceptance:*
    - SCR 系統內部安裝完成。
      *Erection SCR system (inside)*
- 釋出：*Release:*
    - SCR 煙道頂部外殼板之安裝。
      *Erection top casing panels SCR duct*
    - 安裝期間檢查所需之公差。
      *During erection check the required tolerances.*
    - 釋出並隨帶未完成事項清單。
      *Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).*

### 9.3. SCR 煙道頂部外殼板 *Top casing panels SCR duct*

#### 9.3.1. 一般 *General*

頂棚外殼板安裝之施工方法說明書 / 風險評估以及吊裝計畫應由安裝承包商準備。
*Work method statements / risk assessments with lifting plans for the erection of casing panels shall be prepared by the Erection contractor.*

#### 9.3.2. 安裝順序 *Erection sequence*

燃燒器與 SCR 頂棚外殼板之安裝順序示于文件 60028-730-05-001。
*The erection sequence for the Burner and SCR top casing is shown in document 60028-730-05-001.*

#### 9.3.3. SCR 頂棚外殼板安裝之文件與程序 *Documents and procedures for erection of the SCR casing panels (top)*

需由下列單位核准、審查、接受與釋出：
*To be approved, reviewed, accepted and released by*

業主*Client*
- 安裝承包商已核准與審查之項目：
  *Approved and reviewed from erection contractor:*
    - 施工方法說明書：安裝鍋爐爐殼。
      *Work method statement  : Erection boiler casing*
    - 施工方法說明書：現場搭建鍋爐爐殼施工施工架。
      *Work method statement : Erection scaffolding boiler casing*
    - 銲接作業程序書 / 銲接程序資格檢定紀錄 / 銲工資格檢定：非受壓組件。
      *WPS / PQR / WPQ : Non-pressure parts*

#### 9.3.4. SCR 煙道頂部外殼板 *Top casing panels for the SCR duct*

安裝 SCR 煙道之水平頂部外殼板。
*Erect the horizontal top panels for the SCR duct.*

頂棚外殼板安裝前提：
*Top casing panels after*
- 文件與程序：*Documents and procedures:*
    - 已核准與審查。
      *Approved and reviewed*
- 接受：*Acceptance:*
    - 施工施工架搭設完成。
      *Scaffolding ready*
    - AIG 與 SCR 系統（內部）安裝完成。
      *Erection AIG and SCR systems (inside) completed*
- 釋出：*Release:*
    - 燃燒器與 SCR 煙道頂部外殼板之安裝。
      *Erection top panels Burner and SCR duct*

##### 安裝 *Erection*
- 安裝、裝配並點銲上半部外殼板。
  *Erect, fit and tack-weld the top casing panels.*
    - 安裝前，拆除爐殼穿透孔處之皮組件保護塑料與保溫保護棉（若適用）。使用刀具妥善切割塑料與保溫棉。切勿用力拉扯。
      *Before erection, remove the plastic and insulation wool from the casing penetrations if applicable. Properly cut the plastic and wool using a knife. Do not pull it out using force.*
    - 將外殼鋼板對齊至正確位置，並在對齊後將鋼板點銲至主鋼構架上。
      *Align the panel to the correct position and tack-weld the panel to the main steel structure after alignment.*
    - 切除頂部外殼板上之內部保溫防護塑料。
      *Cut away the internal insulation protection plastic from the top casing panels.*
    - 裝配並點銲各鋼板，確保無間隙。依圖面要求於適當處使用填隙片（加強板）。
      *Fit and tack-weld the panels without gap. Use filler plates where required as per drawing.*
    - 在點銲期間，使用銲接護毯覆蓋保溫棉以進行火花防護。
      *During tack-welding, cover the insulation wool using weld blankets for spark protection.*

##### 銲接 *Welding*
- 銲接上半部外殼板之工地現場銜接縫。
  *Weld the top casing panel field splices*
    - 所有外部銲接應為連續銲，外部不允許進行間斷銲。
      *All external welds shall be continuous, no stitch welds on the outside allowed.*
    - 僅在內部接頭上隨適用圖面指示允許進行間斷銲，其高寬尺寸詳見細節。
      *Stitch welds are only allowed on the inside joints, for dimensions see the details on drawings.*
    - 所有槽鋼端部之銲接應為連續銲。
      *For all channel ends the welds shall be continuous.*
    - 依照圖面與 WPS 之銲接細節或型式進行。
      *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.*
    - 在銲接期間，使用銲接護毯覆蓋保溫棉以進行火花防護。
      *During welding, cover the insulation wool using weld blankets for spark protection.*

##### 頂部外殼板之現場組件 *Field parts top casing panels*
- 安裝、裝配並點銲所有必要之現場組件。
  *Erect, fit and tack-weld all necessary field parts.*
    - 上半部外殼板之現場零件可為填隙片、導向板與加強鋼板。識別所有在裝配圖上指示之必要現場組件。
      *Field parts for the top casing panels can be filler, guide and stiffener plates. Identify all required field parts as indicated on the drawings.*
    - 遵循現場零件圖面上之型式銲接細節。
      *Follow the requirements of the weld typical on the field part drawings.*
    - 角隅處與現場銜接處之所有間隙，均應使用填隙片（厚度 6 mm）進行密合（密封銲）。
      *All gaps at corners and field splices have to be closed (seal welded) using filler plates (6 mm thickness).*

##### 現場組件之銲接 *Welding field parts*
- 銲接所有已鎖固裝配之現場組件。
  *Weld all fitted field parts.*
    - 所有外部銲接應為連續銲，外部不允許進行間斷銲。
      *All external welds shall be continuous, no stitch welding on the outside allowed.*
    - 依照圖面之銲接細節或型式進行。
      *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings.*

##### 頂部外殼板角隅連接 *Corner connections top panels*
- 使用角鋼或扁鋼連接安裝、裝配並點銲所有角隅連接。檢視安裝圖確定使用何種型式。
  *Erect, fit and tack-weld all corner connections using angle or flat bar connections. Verify the erection drawings to determine which type to use.*
    - 將角鋼 / 扁鋼連接件緊貼對齊至外殼板，且無間隙。
      *Align the angle / flat bar connections to the casing panels without gap.*
    - 角鋼 / 扁鋼交叉部與連接點，需採用正確之銲接坡口準備進行安裝，細節參見細部圖。
      *Angle / flat bar cross sections and connection points need to be erected using the correct weld preparation, for details see the drawings.*

##### 頂部外殼板角隅連接之銲接 *Welding corner connections top panels*
- 銲接所有角鋼或扁鋼連接。
  *Weld all angle or flat bar connections.*
    - 所有外部銲接應為連續銲，外部不允許進行間斷銲。
      *All external welds shall be continuous, no stitch welds on the outside allowed.*
    - 在銲接期間，使用銲接護毯覆蓋保溫棉以進行火花防護。
      *During welding, cover the insulation wool using weld blankets for spark protection.*
    - 依照圖面與 WPS 之銲接細節或型式進行。
      *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.*
    - 在銲接期間，使用銲接護毯覆蓋保溫棉以進行火花防護。
      *During welding, cover the insulation wool using weld blankets for spark protection.*

##### 業主品質管制 *Quality control client*
- 頂部外殼板之品質管制依據：
  *Quality control for the bottom casing panels is based on:*
    - 鍋爐爐殼現場組裝品質計畫書。
      *Site assembly FQP boiler casing*
- 接受：*Acceptance:*
    - 燃燒器與 SCR 煙道頂部外殼板之安裝。
      *Top panels Burner and SCR duct*
- 釋出：*Release:*
    - SCR 煙道頂棚板內部保溫與內襯板現場銜接工程。
      *Internal insulation and liner sheeting field splices for the top casing panels SCR duct.*
    - 釋出內部現場保溫施工（以無任何未完成項目清單為原則，如有則列出）。
      *Erection of the internal insulation after release without a list of outstanding items (if any).*

#### 9.3.5. 內部現場保溫與內襯板安裝 *Internal field insulation and liner sheeting for the top casing panels SCR duct.*

頂部橫面側現場保溫及內襯板之安裝與品質管制依據「內部保溫及內襯板」章節。
*Erection and quality control for the internal insulation and liner sheeting is based on chapter “Internal Insulation and liner sheeting”*

頂棚外殼板之內部現場保溫安裝前提：
*Boiler casing internal field insulation top panels after*
- 文件與程序：*Documents and procedures:*
    - 已核准與審查。
      *Approved and reviewed*
- 接受：*Acceptance:*
    - 適用之外殼皮組件區域已準備好進行內部保溫與內襯板安裝。
      *Applicable casing area ready for internal insulation and liner sheeting*
- 釋出：*Release:*
    - 內部現場保溫與內襯板之安裝。
      *Erection internal field insulation and liner sheeting.*

##### 安裝 *Erection*
- 執行「內部保溫與內襯板」章節中提及之所有安裝步驟。
  *Execute all erection steps as mentioned in chapter “Internal Insulation and liner sheeting”*

##### 業主品質管制 *Quality control client*
- 頂部外殼之現場內部保溫與內襯板品質管制依據：
  *Quality control for internal insulation and liner sheeting for the top side casing is based on:*
    - 鍋爐外殼現場組裝品質計畫書。
      *Site assembly FQP boiler casing*
- 接受：*Acceptance:*
    - 內部現場保溫與內襯板。
      *Internal insulation and liner sheeting*
- 釋出：*Release:*
    - 不適用。
      *N.A.*
    - 釋出（如有未完成項目則列出清單）。
      *Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).*

#### 9.3.6. AIG 與 SCR 系統之機械完工 *Mechanical completion AIG and SCR systems*

當特定系統或一組特定組件之機械安裝完成後，應進行檢查。未完成項目應彙整於未完成項目清單中。未完成項目清單可檢附在機械完工合格證書上。
*When the mechanical erection of a certain system, or group of specific components is finalized these shall be inspected. Outstanding items shall be collected in an outstanding items list. The outstanding items list can be attached to a Mechanical Completion Certificate.*

此合格證書作為安裝工項正確完工之紀錄。
*Such certificate serves as a record for proper completion of the erection activities.*

SCR / AIG 系統之機械安裝完工合格證書上描述了所檢查之系統或組件。
*The Mechanical Completion Certificate for the SCR / AIG system describes the systems or components inspected.*

藉由在機械完工合格證書上簽字，涉入各方確認所提及之系統或組件已達到足夠之安裝進度，可確定該系統移交給試運轉前之未決點，或者在無任何未決點之情況下直接將系統移交給試車組。
*By signing the Mechanical Completion Certificate the parties involved confirm that the system or components referred to are in a sufficiently advanced stage of erection to either identify the points remaining before the system can be handed over to Commissioning, or in absence of any of such points hand over the system to Commissioning directly.*

##### 現場步行檢查 *Walk-down*
- 機械安裝完工合格證書上所提及之所有系統或特定組件組，均應進行正確安裝、完整性與損壞之最終檢查。
  *All systems or group of specific components referred to on the Mechanical Completion Certificate shall have a final inspection for correct erection, completeness and damages.*
- 完成現場步行檢查後，應立即建立未決點/未完成項目紀錄（如有）。
  *A record of outstanding items (if any) will be set-up directly after the walk-down.*
- 若有未完成項目清單適用，其應分類為：
  *In case a list of outstanding items is applicable it shall be categorized:*
    - 水壓試驗前應解決之項目。
      *Items to be solved before hydro testing.*
    - 試運轉前應解決之項目。
      *Items to be solved before commissioning.*
    - 初期驗收 (PAC) 前應解決之項目。
      *Items to be solved before provisional acceptance.*
- 確認所涉入系統之適用現場安裝旅程表（隨店紀錄卡）已由所有涉入方簽署同意。
  *Verify that the applicable site assembly travellers for the systems involved are signed off by all involved parties.*
- 檢查是否有任何未處置之不符合事項報告 (NCR)（如有）。
  *Check for any outstanding NCRs (if any).*
- 檢查先前階段所建立之未完成項目清單。
  *Check for lists of outstanding items made in earlier stages.*

#### 9.3.7. SCR 觸媒積木塊之裝設 *Installation of scr blocks*

在基礎負載（滿載運轉）達 24 小時之後，依相關供應商文件安裝 SCR 觸媒模組（觸媒積木塊）。
*Install the SCR block according the relevant supplier documentation 24 hours after running on base load.*


## 10. 汽鼓與容器 *DRUMS AND VESSELS*

本章包含以下段落：
*This chapter contains the following paragraphs:*
1. 一般：第 10.1 節
   *General : paragraph 10.1*
2. 文件與程序：第 10.2 節
   *Documents and procedures : paragraph 10.2*
3. 汽鼓安裝：第 10.3 節
   *Drum erection : paragraph 10.3*
4. 汽鼓對正：第 10.4 節
   *Drum alignment : paragraph 10.4*
5. 汽鼓中心固定叉與導向板：第 10.5 節
   *Drum center fixation fork and guide plates : paragraph 10.5*
6. 汽鼓內部組件與設備：第 10.6 節
   *Drum internals and equipment : paragraph 10.6*
7. 高壓分離器容器安裝：第 10.7 節
   *HP separator vessel erection : paragraph 10.7*
8. 汽鼓與容器最終檢查：第 10.8 節
   *Final inspection Drums and vessels : paragraph 10.8*

### 10.1. 一般 *General*

熱回收鍋爐 (HRSG) 範圍內之汽鼓與容器安裝包括中壓 (IP) 汽鼓、低壓 (LP) 汽鼓與高壓 (HP) 分離器容器。
*Drum and vessel erection for the HRSG scope consists out of a IP and LP drum and a HP separator vessel.*
安裝承包商應針對汽鼓之吊裝準備施工方法說明書 / 風險評估以及吊裝計畫。
*Work method statements / risk assessments with lifting plans for the erection of drums shall be prepared by the erection contractor.*
汽鼓與容器之安裝順序示於文件 60031-730-05-001。
*The erection sequence for drums and vessels is shown in document 60031-730-05-001*

### 10.2. 文件與程序 *Documents and procedures*

- 安裝汽鼓與容器所需之文件與程序。
  *Documents and procedures required for installation of the drums and Vessels.*
	- 施工方法說明書：安裝汽鼓與桶槽槽。
	  *Work method statement : Erection drums and tanks*
	- 施工品質計畫書：熱回收鍋爐汽鼓與容器。
	  *FQP : HRSG drums and vessels*
	- 銲接作業程序書 / 銲接程序資格檢定紀錄 / 銲工資格檢定：非受壓組件。
	  *WPS / PQR / WPQ : Non-pressure parts.*
	- 螺栓緊固程序書：非受壓組件。
	  *Bolt torque procedure : Non pressure parts.*
	- 銲接地圖 / 紀錄：非受壓組件。
	  *Weld typical / record : Non-pressure parts.*
	- 銲接耗材處理程序書：非受壓組件。
	  *Welding consumable handling procedure : Non-pressure parts.*
	- 非破壞檢測程序書 / 人員資格認證：非受壓組件。
	  *NDE procedures / personnel qualifications : Non-pressure parts.*
	- 依據「管道系統」章節之文件：受壓組件。
	  *Documents according Chapter “piping” : Pressure parts.*

### 10.3. 汽鼓安裝 *Drum erection*

在開始安裝汽鼓之前，需提前準備一些工項。
*Before erection of the drums can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance.*

##### 準備工作與先決條件 *Preparations and preconditions*
- 前述段落中提到之文件與程序需已就緒，並由權責方審查完畢。
  *The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).*
- 下列準備工作 / 工項需已完成，且在對應之施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 中視適用情況進行簽認。
  *The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.*
	- 中壓與低壓降流管之臨時存放。
	  *Temporary storage of IP and LP down comers*
	- 汽鼓支撐樑安裝完成。
	  *Drum support beams erected*
	- 鋼結構主框架立柱底座無收縮水泥灌漿與錨定螺栓緊固。
	  *Grouting of main steel columns and torqueing of the anchors.*
	- 高程正確。
	  *Elevation correct*
- 在汽鼓懸吊樑上安裝滑動支承。
  *Install the sliding supports on the drum suspension beams.*
- 在汽鼓鞍座上安裝附調整墊片的滑動對接板。
  *Install the counter sliding plates with shims on the drum saddles.*
- 在汽鼓之固定耳板上安裝調整墊片。
  *Install shim plates on the fixation lug of the drum.*
	- 進行測量以確定汽鼓固定耳板支撐件與汽鼓中心固定叉之位置與尺寸（另參見鋼結構主框架圖面）。一旦汽鼓定位完成，中心固定叉與固定耳板支承件之間的自由空間應平均分配至兩側，並如汽鼓圖面所示。根據測量報告中之尺寸，可安裝並銲接正確之調整墊片厚度。
	  *Perform a survey to determine the location and dimensions of the drum fixation lug support and the drum centre fixation fork. (See also main steel structure) Once the drum is positioned the free space between the centre fixation fork and the fixation lug support shall be equally divided to each side and be as given on the drum drawings. Based on the dimensions from the survey report the correct shim thickness can be installed and welded.*
	- 進行測量以確定從汽鼓中心線到汽鼓鞍座最低點之尺寸。汽鼓支撐樑之高程亦應已知並可取得。根據可用之尺寸與高程，可確定並安裝需裝設於滑動對接板與汽鼓鞍座之間的調整墊片厚度。使用製造商之公差圖面。
	  *Perform a survey to determine the dimensions from the centreline of the drum to the lowest points of the drum saddles. Elevation of the drum support beams shall be known and available as well.Based on the available dimensions and elevations the required shim thickness for installation between the counter sliding plates and the drum saddles can be determined and installed.Use the tolerance drawings from the manufacturer.*
	- 安裝期間保持該位置清潔，並防止表面污染。
	  *Keep the location clean during erection and prevent pollution of surfaces.*
	- 在汽鼓支撐樑之正確位置安裝滑動支承板，不要進行點銲。
	  *Install the slide support plates on the drum support beams at the correct location, NO TACK WELDING.*

##### 釋出後續工項 *Release subsequent activities*
- 隨著本段落工項之成功完成，即可釋出以下工項：
  *With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given:*
	- 汽鼓吊裝對正。
	  *Alignment of the drums erection*
- 依據適用之施工方法說明書進行汽鼓之吊裝 / 運輸。
  *Lift / transport the drums as per the applicable Work Method Statement.*
	- 汽鼓吊裝 / 運輸前，檢查所有連接點。
	  *Check all connections before lifting / transport of the drums*
	- 在裝載與吊裝期間，應經常檢查設備狀態，確保其處於良好狀態。
	  *During loading and lifting, frequently check the status of the equipment to be in good shape.*
	- 依據吊裝及施工方法說明書中之指示進行運輸 / 吊裝。
	  *Transport / Lifting to take place according the instructions for lifting and the Work Method Statement.*
	- 如有任何偏差或失效，請與製造商聯繫。
	  *In case of any deviation or failure, contact the manufacturer.*
- 將汽鼓安裝至正確之高程。
  *Erect the drums on the correct elevation.*
	- 安裝期間，經常檢查附有聚四氟乙烯 (PTFE) 墊片之杯狀滑動支承底座（位於汽鼓支撐樑上）未受損損壞。
	  *Frequently check the cup shaped sliding support base with PTFE pad is not damaged during erection. (On the drum support beams)*
	- 確認高程是否符合汽鼓公差圖面。若需要調整汽鼓高程，切勿忘記將門型鋼結構列頂部之實際尺寸納入評估中。與製造商討論此項。
	  *Verify the elevation to be in accordance with the drum tolerance drawings. In case adjustment of the drum elevation is required, do not forget to incorporate the actual dimensions of the top of the steel goalpost rows in the evaluation. Discuss this with manufacturer.*
	- 針對汽鼓之最終高程製作測量報告。
	  *Make a survey report for the final elevation of the drums.*

##### 品質管制 *Quality control*
- 依據適用之施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 與/或程序書執行品質管制工項。
  *Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).*
- 確認汽鼓高程與滑動板上之放置正確無誤。
  *Verify the elevation of the drum and placement on sliding plates for correctness.*
- 製造商代表應目視檢查並審查汽鼓實際測量測繪報告，以確保其符合適用之 60031-730-06 系列公差圖面。
  *Manufacturer shall visually check and review the actual survey report for the drum measurement to be in accordance with the applicable tolerance drawings 60031-730-06-series.*

### 10.4. 汽鼓對正 *Drum alignment*

在開始汽鼓對正之前，需提前準備一些工項。
*Before alignment of the drums can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance.*

##### 準備工作與先決條件 *Preparations and preconditions*
- 前述段落中提到之文件與程序需已就緒，並由權責方審查完畢。
  *The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).*
- 下列準備工作 / 工項需已完成，且在對應之施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 中視適用情況進行簽認。
  *The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.*
	- 汽鼓安裝完成。
	  *Drums installed*

##### 釋出後續工項 *Release subsequent activities*
- 隨著本段落工項之成功完成，即可釋出以下工項：
  *With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given:*
	- 汽鼓中心固定叉與導向板之安裝。
	  *Installation drum centre fixation fork and guide plates*

##### 對正 *Alignment*
- 從蛇形管排聯箱管嘴到汽鼓管嘴安裝數根上升管。在左側與右側安裝兩根上升管，並有兩根上升管均勻分布在蛇形管排聯箱上。
  *Install several riser pipes from the harp header nozzles to the drum nozzles. Install two riser pipes on the left and right sides and two riser pipes divided over the harp headers.*
- 在上升管道裝配期間，於蛇形管排聯箱側使用管夾。使上升管道在汽鼓管嘴側保持無任何夾緊狀態。
  *During fit-up of the riser piping use pipe clamps on the harp header side. Keep the riser piping free from any clamping on the drum nozzles side.*
	- 若上升管道與汽鼓管嘴之間的連接處顯示有偏差（超出公差），需調整汽鼓之位置。
	  *In case (out of tolerance) offset is showing at the connection between the riser piping and the drum nozzles, the drum placement needs adjustment.*
	- 使用蛇形管排聯箱側作為汽鼓對正之「固定點」與起始點。
	  *Use the harp header side as the “fixed point” and starting point for the drum alignment.*
	- 在安裝上升管道期間，切勿忘記安裝金屬膨脹接頭。
	  *During erection of the riser piping DO NOT FORGET TO INSTALL THE METAL EXPANSION BELLOWS.*
	- 當偏差超出允許之公差時，請與製造商聯繫。
	  *When the offset is more than the allowable tolerances, contact the manufacturer.*

##### 品質管制 *Quality control*
- 依據適用之施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 與/或程序書執行品質管制工項。
  *Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).*
	- 點銲作業僅可在受壓組件（管道）之所有文件經業主核准與審查後始得開始。
	  *Tack-welding can only commence when all documents for the pressure parts (piping) are approved and reviewed by the client.*
	- 確認管道之裝配符合無應力狀態。
	  *Verify the fit-up of the piping to be stress-free.*
	- 確認金屬膨脹接頭已安裝（若適用）。
	  *Verify the metal expansion bellow is installed (if applicable).*
	- 製造商代表應目視檢查並審查汽鼓實際測量報告，以確保其符合適用之 60031-730-06 系列公差圖面。
	  *Manufacturer shall visually check and review the actual survey report for the drum measurements to be in accordance with the applicable tolerance drawings 60031-730-06-series.*

##### 上升管道之點銲 *Tack-welding of the riser piping*
- 在蛇形管排聯箱管嘴與汽鼓管嘴之間點銲上升管道。
  *Tack-weld the riser piping between the harp header nozzles and the drum nozzles.*
	- 密切遵循圖面與銲接作業程序書 (WPS) 上之銲接細節或型式。
	  *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.*

### 10.5. 汽鼓中心固定叉與導向板 *Drum centre fixation fork and guide plates*

在開始安裝汽鼓中心固定叉與導向板之前，需提前準備一些工項。
*Before erection of the drum centre fixation fork and guide plates can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance.*

##### 準備工作與先決條件 *Preparations and preconditions*
- 前述段落中提到之文件與程序需已就緒，並由權責方審查完畢。
  *The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).*
- 下列準備工作 / 工項需已完成，且在對應之施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 中視適用情況進行簽認。
  *The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.*
	- 汽鼓對正完成。
	  *Drums aligned*

##### 釋出後續工項 *Release subsequent activities*
- 隨著本段落工項之成功完成，即可釋出以下工項：
  *With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given:*
	- 外部管道安裝。
	  *erection external piping*

##### 安裝 *Erection*
- 經由點銲將汽鼓中心固定叉安裝在正確�### 14.5. 次鋼構與吊掛型鋼之最終檢查 (Final inspection of secondary steel and hoisting beams)

當特定系統或一組特定組件之機械安裝完成後，應進行檢查。未完成項目應彙整於未決點清單內，並檢附於最終檢查合格證書上。
*When the mechanical erection of a certain system, or group of specific components is finalized these shall be inspected. Outstanding items shall be collected in an outstanding items list. The outstanding items list can be attached to a Final Inspection Certificate.*
此證書作為妥善完成組裝工項之紀錄。
*Such certificate serves as a record for proper completion of the erection activities.*
次鋼構之最終檢查合格證書中描述了所檢查之系統或組件。
*The Final Inspection Certificate for secondary steel describes the systems or components inspected.*
藉由簽署最終檢查合格證書，所涉及之各方確認所指之系統或組件已達到足夠先進之安裝階段，得以識別出系統移交給試運轉前之剩餘要點；或在無此項目之情況下，直接將系統移交給試運轉。
*By signing the Final Inspection Certificate the parties involved confirm that the system or components referred to are in a sufficiently advanced stage of installation to either identify the points remaining before the system can be handed over to Commissioning, or in absence of any of such points hand over the system to Commissioning directly.*

##### 檢查 *Inspection*
- 最終檢查合格證書中所提及之所有系統或特定組件組，應針對正確安裝、完整性與損壞進行最終檢查。
  *All systems or group of specific components referred to on the Final inspection Certificate shall have a final inspection for correct installation, completeness and damages.*
- 完成現場步行檢查後，應立即建立未完成項目 / 未決點紀錄（如有）。
  *A record of outstanding items (if any) shall be set-up directly after the walk-down.*
- 若有施作未完成項目清單，其應分類為：
  *In case a list of outstanding items is applicable it shall be categorized in:*
	- 水壓試驗前應解決之項目（A 級項目）。
	  *Items to be solved before hydro testing. (A-items)*
	- 試運轉前應解決之項目（B 級項目）。
	  *Items to be solved before commissioning. (B-items)*
	- 初期驗收 (PAC) 前應解決之項目（C 級項目）。
	  *Items to be solved before provisional acceptance. (C-items)*

確認所涉及系統之適用施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 已由所有權責方簽字認可。未完成項目應納入未決點清單。
*Verify that the applicable site FQPs for the systems involved are signed off by all parties involved. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list.*
確認所有不符合事項報告 (NCR) 已關閉。未完成項目應納入未決點清單。
*Verify that all Non-Conformity Reports (NCR’s) are closed. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list.*

## 11. 桶槽與鞍座 *TANKS / SKIDS*

本章包含以下段落：
*This chapter contains the following paragraphs:*

1. 一般：第 11.1 節
   *General : paragraph 11.1*
2. 文件與程序：第 11.2 節
   *Documents and procedures : paragraph 11.2*
3. 桶槽 / 鞍座安裝：第 11.3 節
   *Tank / skid erection : paragraph 11.3*
4. 水泥灌漿：第 11.4 節
   *Grouting : paragraph 11.4*
5. 桶槽 / 鞍座最終檢查：第 11.5 節
   *Final inspection tanks / skids : paragraph 11.5*

### 11.1. 一般 *General*

熱回收鍋爐 (HRSG) 範圍內之桶槽安裝包括連續/間歇排污槽（洩壓槽）。熱回收鍋爐 (HRSG) 範圍內之鞍座安裝通常包括氨氣注入柵 (AIG) 鞍座。
*Tank erection for the HRSG scope consists out of a blowdown tank. Skid erection for the HRSG scope normally consists out of a AIG skid.*
安裝承包商應針對桶槽 / 鞍座之安裝準備施工方法說明書 / 風險評估以及吊裝計畫。
*Work method statements / risk assessments with lifting plans for the erection of tanks / skids shall be prepared by the erection contractor.*
連續/間歇排污槽與 AIG 鞍座之安裝順序示於文件 60031-730-05-001。
*The erection sequence for blowdown tank and AIG skid is shown in document 60031-730-05-001*

### 11.2. 文件與程序 *Documents and procedures*

- 安裝桶槽 / 鞍座所需之文件與程序。
  *Documents and procedures required for erection of the tanks / skids.*

	- 施工方法說明書：安裝汽鼓與桶槽槽。
	  *Work method statement : Erection drums and tanks*
	- 施工方法說明書：安裝選擇性觸媒還原 (SCR) 系統。
	  *Work method statement : Erection SCR system*
	- 施工品質計畫書：熱回收鍋爐汽鼓與壓力容器。
	  *FQP : HRSG drums and pressure vessels*
	- 施工品質計畫書：熱回收鍋爐選擇性觸媒還原 (SCR) 系統。
	  *FQP : HRSG SCR system*
	- 螺栓緊固程序書：非受壓組件。
	  *Bolt torque procedure : Non pressure parts.*
	- 銲接作業程序書 / 銲接程序資格檢定紀錄 / 銲工資格檢定：非受壓組件。
	  *WPS / PQR / WPQ : Non-pressure parts.*
	- 銲接地圖 / 紀錄：非受壓組件。
	  *Weld typical / record : Non-pressure parts.*
	- 銲接耗材處理程序書：非受壓組件。
	  *Welding consumable handling procedure : Non-pressure parts.*
	- 非破壞檢測程序書 / 人員資格認證：非受壓組件。
	  *NDE procedures / personnel qualifications : Non-pressure parts.*
	- 依據「管道系統」章節之文件：受壓組件。
	  *Documents according Chapter “piping” : Pressure parts.*

### 11.3. 桶槽 / 鞍座安裝 *Tank / skid erection*

在開始安裝連續/間歇排污槽或 AIG 鞍座之前，需提前準備一些工項。
*Before erection of the blowdown tank or AIG skid can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance.*

##### 準備工作與先決條件 *Preparations and preconditions*
- 前述段落中提到之文件與程序需已就緒，並由權責方審查完畢。
  *The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).*
- 下列準備工作 / 工項需已完成，且在對應之施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 中視適用情況進行簽認。
  *The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.*
	- 桶槽 / 鞍座基礎。
	  *Tank / skid foundation*
- 依據適用之施工方法說明書起吊並運輸桶槽 / 鞍座。
  *Lift and transport the tank / skid as per the applicable Work Method Statement.*
	- 桶槽 / 鞍座吊裝及運輸前，檢查所有連接點。
	  *Check all connections before lifting and transporting the tank / skid.*
	- 在裝載與吊裝期間，應經常檢查設備狀態，確保其處於良好狀態。
	  *During loading and lifting, frequently check the status of the equipment to be in good shape.*
	- 依據吊裝說明與施工方法說明書中之指示進行運輸與吊裝。
	  *Transport and lifting to take place according the instructions for lifting and the Work Method Statement.*
	- 針對鞍座，請確認供應商之搬運與安裝說明手冊。
	  *In case of skids verify the supplier handling and installation instructions.*
	- 如有任何偏差或失效，請與製造商聯繫。
	  *In case of any deviation or failure, contact the manufacturer.*

##### 釋出後續工項 *Release subsequent activities*
- 隨著本段落工項之成功完成，即可釋出以下工項：
  *With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given:*
	- 桶槽 / 鞍座無收縮水泥灌漿。
	  *Grouting of tanks / skids*
	- 管道連接。
	  *Piping connections*

##### 安裝 *Erection*
- 將桶槽 / 鞍座定位至其鋼結構支撐件上。
  *Position the tank / skid onto its steel structure supports.*
- 使用鋼製調整墊片調整高程與對正。
  *Adjust for elevation and alignment using steel shims.*
- 如圖面所示將桶槽 / 鞍座連接至鋼結構上。
  *Connect the tank/skid to the steel structure as indicated on the drawings.*
	- 定位期間密切監控桶槽 / 鞍座之座標。
	  *Closely monitor tank/skid coordinates during positioning.*
	- 當定位完成時，進行正確位置、對正與高程之測量測繪。
	  *Perform a survey for correct position, alignment and elevation of the tank/skid when in position.*
	- 任何裝設之調整墊片應與鋼結構銲接。
	  *Any shims placed shall be welded to the steel structure.*
	- 調整墊片之銲接僅在確認位置正確後始得進行。
	  *Welding of shims only after confirmation of correct position.*
	- 密切遵循圖面與銲接作業程序書 (WPS) 上之銲接細節或型式。
	  *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.*

##### 品質管制 *Quality control*
- 依據適用之施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 與/或程序書完成品質管制工項。
  *Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).*
- 釋出並隨帶未完成事項清單。
  *Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).*
- 檢查桶槽內部之清潔度，並清除槽容器內部之所有矽膠防潮包。
  *Inspect the inside of a tank for cleanliness and remove any silica gel bags from the inside of the vessel.*

### 11.4. 無收縮水泥灌漿 *Grouting*

桶槽 / 鞍座之灌漿作業應依據本手冊中之「無收縮水泥灌漿」章節進行。
*Grouting of the tanks / skids is based on the Chapter “Grouting” in this manual.*
執行期間遵循該章節中提到之安裝與品質步驟。
*Follow the installation and quality steps mentioned in this chapter during execution.*

### 11.5. 桶槽 / 鞍座最終檢查 *Final inspection tanks / skids*

當特定系統或一組特定組件之機械安裝完成後，應進行檢查。未完成項目應彙整於未決點清單內，並檢附於最終檢查合格證書上。
*When the mechanical erection of a certain system, or group of specific components is finalized these shall be inspected. Outstanding items shall be collected in an outstanding items list and attached to the Final inspection Certificate.*

桶槽 / 鞍座之最終檢查合格證書中描述了所檢查之系統或組件。
*The Final inspection Certificate of the tanks / skids describes the systems or components inspected.*

##### 檢查 *Inspection*
- 最終檢查合格證書中所提及之所有系統或特定組件組，應針對正確安裝、完整性與損壞進行最終檢查。
  *All systems or group of specific components referred to on the Final inspection Certificate shall have a final inspection for correct erection, completeness and damages.*
- 完成現場步行檢查後，應立即建立未完成項目 / 未決點紀錄（如有）。
  *A record of outstanding items (if any) shall be set-up directly after the walk-down.*
- 若有施作未完成項目清單，其應分類為：
  *In case a list of outstanding items is applicable it shall be categorized in :*
	- 水壓試驗前應解決之項目（A 級項目）。
	  *Items to be solved before hydro testing (A-items)*
	- 熱試運轉前應解決之項目（B 級項目）。
	  *Items to be solved before hot-commissioning (B-items)*
	- 初期驗收 (PAC) 前應解決之項目（C 級項目）。
	  *Items to be solved before provisional acceptance (PAC) (C-items)*

確認所涉及系統之適用現場安裝品質計畫書 (FQP) 已由所有權責方簽字認可。未完成項目應納入未決點清單。
*Verify that the applicable site FQPs for the systems involved are signed off by all parties involved. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list*
確認所有不符合事項報告 (NCR) 已關閉。未完成項目應納入未決點清單。
*Verify that all Non-Conformity Reports are closed. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list.*


## 12. 煙囪與出口煙道 *STACK AND OUTLET DUCT*

本章包含以下段落：
*This chapter contains the following paragraphs:*

1. 煙囪安裝：第 12.1 節
   *Stack erection : paragraph 12.1*
2. 出口煙道安裝：第 12.2 節
   *Outlet duct erection : paragraph 12.2*

### 12.1. 煙囪安裝 *Stack erection*

本段落描述主煙囪之安裝。
*This paragraph describes the erection of the main stack.*

#### 12.1.1. 一般 *General*

煙囪將分多個（預組合裝配之）段口進行安裝，惟煙囪鋼底環（基座環）除外，其直接放置於錨定螺栓上。
*The stack is to be erected in several (pre-assembled) sections, except for the stack base ring, which is directly placed on the anchor bolts.*
安裝承包商應針對煙囪之安裝準備施工方法說明書 / 風險評估以及吊裝計畫。
*Work method statements / risk assessments with lifting plans for the erection of the stack shall be prepared by the erection contractor.*
煙囪之安裝順序示於文件 60031-730-05-001。
*The erection sequence for the stack is shown in document 60031-730-05-001.*

#### 12.1.2. 文件與程序 *Documents and procedures*

- 安裝煙囪所需之文件與程序。
  *Documents and procedures required for erection of the stack.*

	- 施工方法說明書：安裝煙囪 / 出口煙道。
	  *Work method statement : Erection stack / outlet duct.*
	- 施工方法說明書：搭設煙囪 / 出口煙道施工架。
	  *Work method statement : Erection scaffolding stack / outlet duct.*
	- 施工品質計畫書：熱回收鍋爐煙囪。
	  *FQP : HRSG stack.*
	- 螺栓緊固程序書：非受壓組件。
	  *Bolt torque procedure : Non pressure parts.*
	- 銲接作業程序書 / 銲接程序資格檢定紀錄 / 銲工資格檢定：非受壓組件。
	  *WPS / PQR / WPQ : Non-pressure parts.*
	- 銲接地圖 / 紀錄：非受壓組件。
	  *Weld typical / record : Non-pressure parts.*
	- 銲接耗材處理程序書：非受壓組件。
	  *Welding consumable handling procedure : Non-pressure parts.*
	- 非破壞檢測程序書 / 人員資格認證：非受壓組件。
	  *NDE procedures / personnel qualifications : Non-pressure parts.*

#### 12.1.3. 煙囪鋼底環 *Stack base ring*

在開始安裝煙囪鋼底環分段段口之前，需提前準備一些工項。
*Before Erection of the segments of stack base ring, some activities need to be prepared in advance.*

##### 準備工作與先決條件 *Preparations and preconditions*
- 前述段落中提到之文件與程序需已就緒，並由權責方審查完畢。
  *The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).*
- 下列準備工作 / 工項需已完成，且在對應之施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 中視適用情況進行簽認。
  *The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.*
	- 基礎已就緒。
	  *Foundation ready*
	- 材料已收訖，並對數量與品質進行檢驗（填寫溢裝、短裝與損壞報告，即 OSD 報告）。
	  *Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report)*
- 裝設煙囪鋼底環之底座調整墊片。
  *Placement of the base plate shims for stack base ring.*
- 準備用於煙囪安裝之施工架及/或高空作業車。
  *Prepare the scaffolding and or sky climbers for erection of the stack*
- 準備安裝煙囪所需之工具。
  *Prepare the tools required for erection of the stack*
	- 施工架與高空作業車需基於適用之施工方法說明書。
