	  *Scaffolding and sky climbers based on applicable work method statements.*
	- 與煙囪安裝平行，亦可執行其他工項。
	  *Parallel to the erection of the stack other activities can be carried out.*

##### 釋出後續工項 *Release subsequent activities*
- 隨著本段落工項之成功完成，即可釋出以下工項：
  *With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given:*
	- 外部保溫（如有）。
	  *External insulation (if any)*
	- 接續煙囪段口之安裝。
	  *Erection subsequent stack sections.*
	- 煙囪鋼底環之水泥灌漿。
	  *Grouting of stack base ring.*

##### 安裝 *Erection*
- 安裝、對合並點銲煙囪鋼底環之段口。
  *Erect, fit and tack-weld the segments for stack base ring*
- 在開始安裝煙囪鋼底環段口之前，極為重要之步驟是在基礎上正確之高程與位置放置調整墊片。為使煙囪段口獲得均勻水平且高程正確之基礎，可能需要裝設調整墊片。
  *Before erection of stack base ring segments can commence, it is important to place shims with the correct elevation and on the correct location on the foundation. Shimming can be required to obtain an equally leveled and correctly elevated foundation for the stack segments.*
	- 為整平煙囪鋼底環而裝設之任何調整墊片，應安裝於法蘭下方，且不得突出。
	  *Any shims placed (for levelling of stack base ring) shall be installed under the flanges and shall not protrude.*
	- 在段口安裝前，清晰標記 0、90、180 與 270 度之基準參考線。
	  *Before erection of the segments, clearly mark the 0, 90, 180 and 270 degrees references.*
	- 在安裝期間，檢查段口縱向銲縫之位置。
	  *During erection check the position of the segments longitudinal seams.*
	- 在組立期間，經常確認煙囪部件之高程、尺寸與圓度。
	  *During assembly frequently verify the elevation, dimensions and roundness of the stack part.*
	- 應在多個位置使用牽索（拉線）固定，以確保煙囪段口之穩定性。
	  *Stack segments stability shall be ensured by having guy wires secured at several points.*

##### 銲接 *Welding*
- 銲接煙囪鋼底環段口之縱向銲縫。
  *Weld the longitudinal seams of the stack base ring sections.*
	- 密切遵循圖面與銲接作業程序書 (WPS) 上之銲接細節或型式。
	  *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.*

##### 品質管制 *Quality control*
- 依據施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 與/或程序書完成品質管制工項。
  *Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).*
- 銲接前檢查段口之對合與縱向銲縫之位置。
  *Check fit-up of segments and position of longitudinal seams before welding*
- 銲接前檢查第 1 段煙囪段口之高程與圓度。
  *Check elevation and roundness of the stack section 1 before welding.*
- 釋出並隨帶未完成事項清單。
  *Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).*

##### 安裝現場組件 *Erect field parts*
煙囪之現場組件可包括加強板、U 型鋼、二級鋼構支撐件與平台。識別圖面中指示之所有所需現場組件。
*Field parts for the stack can be stiffener plates, U-channels, secondary steel supporting and platforms. Identify all required field parts indicated on the drawings.*
- 安裝、對合並點銲現場組件。
  *Erect, fit and tack-weld the field parts*
	- 遵循圖面中適用於現場組件之型式示範。
	  *Follow the typical for the field parts on the drawings.*

##### 銲接 *Welding*
- 銲接現場組件。
  *Weld the field parts.*
	- 密切遵循圖面與銲接作業程序書 (WPS) 上之銲接細節或型式。
	  *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.*

##### 品質管制 *Quality control*
- 依據適用之施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 與/或程序書完成品質管制工項。
  *Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).*
- 釋出並隨帶未完成事項清單。
  *Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).*
- 製造商代表應目視檢查並審查煙囪鋼底環量測之實際測繪報告，以確保其符合適用之公差圖面（60031-730-06 系列）中所提之公差。
  *Manufacturer shall visually check and review the actual survey report for measurements of the stack base ring to be in accordance with the tolerances mentioned on the applicable tolerance drawings (60031-730-06-series).*

#### 12.1.4. 接續之煙囪段口（現場安裝） *Subsequent stack sections (field installed)*

介於煙囪鋼底環與煙囪擋風門之間的煙囪段口將在現場安裝就位。
*The stack sections between stack base ring and the stack damper will be erected in location.*
在開始安裝接續之煙囪段口之前，需提前準備一些工項。
*Before Erection of the segments of the subsequent stack sections, some activities need to be prepared in advance.*

##### 準備工作與先決條件 *Preparations and preconditions*
- 前述段落中提到之文件與程序需已就緒，並由權責方審查完畢。
  *The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).*
- 下列準備工作 / 工項需已完成，且在對應之施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 中視適用情況進行簽認。
  *The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.*
	- 煙囪鋼底環已完成就位。
	  *Stack base ring ready*
	- 材料已收訖，並對數量與品質進行檢驗（填寫溢裝、短裝與損壞報告，即 OSD 報告）。
	  *Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report)*
- 準備用於煙囪安裝之施工架及/或高空作業車。
  *Prepare the scaffolding and or sky climbers for installation of the stack*

##### 釋出後續工項 *Release subsequent activities*
- 隨著本段落工項之成功完成，即可釋出以下工項：
  *With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given:*
	- 外部保溫（如有）。
	  *External insulation (if any)*
	- 安裝煙囪擋風門。
	  *Erection stack damper.*

##### 安裝 *Erection*
- 安裝、對合並點銲接續之煙囪段口於煙囪鋼底環與先前已安裝之段口上。
  *Erect, fit and tack-weld the subsequent stack sections onto the stack base ring and previously erected sections.*
	- 安裝期間檢查煙囪段口之位置、高程與配對。
	  *During erection check position, elevation and alignment of stack sections.*
	- 依業主要求對壁厚進行「0 點（初期值）量測」。
	  *Perform “0-measurements” on wall thickness, as per client requirements.*
	- 安裝之煙囪部件應在多個位置使用牽索（拉線）固定。
	  *Erected stack part to be secured by use of guy wires at several locations.*

##### 品質管制 *Quality control*
- 依據適用之施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 與/或程序書執行品質管制工項。
  *Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).*
- 檢查接續煙囪段口之間的對合裝配。
  *Check the fit-up between subsequent stack sections*
- 定期檢查已安裝煙囪段口之尺寸、高程與圓度。
  *Regularly check dimension, elevation and roundness for erected stack sections.*

##### 銲接 *Welding*
- 將接續之煙囪段口銲接至煙囪鋼底環及先前已安裝之段口上。
  *Weld subsequent stack sections onto the stack base ring and previously erected sections.*
	- 密切遵循圖面與銲接作業程序書 (WPS) 上之銲接細節或型式。
	  *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.*

##### 品質管制 *Quality control*
- 依據適用之施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 與/或程序書完成品質管制工項。
  *Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).*
- 檢查已安裝煙囪段口之高程與圓度。
  *Check elevation and roundness of erected stack section*
- 釋出並隨帶未完成事項清單。
  *Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).*
- 製造商代表應目視檢查並審查實際測量測繪報告，以確保煙囪鋼底環測量符合適用之公差圖面（60031-730-06 系列）中提到之公差。
  *Manufacturer shall visually check and review the actual survey report for measurements of the stack base ring to be in accordance with the tolerances mentioned on the applicable tolerance drawings (60031-730-06-series).*

#### 12.1.5. 煙囪加強結構 *Stack reinforcement structure*

煙囪加強結構在連接出口煙道之煙囪位置提供剛性。
*The stack reinforcement structure gives rigidness to the stack at the stack location where the outlet duct is connected.*
在開始安裝加強結構之前，需提前準備一些工項。
*Before Erection of the reinforcement structure, some activities need to be prepared in advance.*

##### 準備工作與先決條件 *Preparations and preconditions*
- 前述段落中提到之文件與程序需已就緒，並由權責方審查完畢。
  *The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).*
- 下列準備工作 / 工項需已完成，且在對應之施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 中視適用情況進行簽認。
  *The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.*
	- 現場安裝之煙囪段口已完成就位。
	  *Field erected stack sections ready*
	- 材料已收訖，並對數量與品質進行檢驗（填寫溢裝、短裝與損壞報告，即 OSD 報告）。
	  *Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report)*
- 準備用於煙囪加強結構安裝之施工架及/或高空作業車。
  *Prepare the scaffolding and or sky climbers for erection of the stack reinforcement structure*

##### 釋出後續工項 *Release subsequent activities*
- 隨著本段落工項之成功完成，即可釋出以下工項：
  *With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given:*
	- 安裝煙囪底部。
	  *Erection bottom of the stack*
	- 安裝煙囪擋風門。
	  *Erection stack damper*

##### 安裝 *Erection*
- 安裝、對合並銲接該鋼結構。
  *Erect, fit and weld the steel structure.*
	- 在安裝後部線架（骨架）期間，切勿忘記安裝支撐板與封閉板。
	  *Do not forget to erect the support and closing plates during erection of the rear side wireframe.*
	- 安裝期間檢查鋼結構之正確位置。
	  *During erection check the correct position of the steel structure.*

##### 銲接 *Welding*
- 銲接結構體。
  *Weld the structure.*
	- 密切遵循圖面與銲接作業程序書 (WPS) 上之銲接細節或型式。
	  *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.*

##### 品質管制 *Quality control*
- 依據適用之施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 與/或程序書完成品質管制工項。
  *Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).*
- 檢查內部骨架之完整性。
  *Check the inside wireframe for completeness.*
- 釋出並隨帶未完成事項清單。
  *Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).*

#### 12.1.6. 煙囪底部 *Bottom of the stack*

在開始安裝煙囪底部之前，需提前準備一些工項。
*Before erection of the bottom of the stack, some activities need to be prepared in advance.*

##### 準備工作與先決條件 *Preparations and preconditions*
- 前述段落中提到之文件與程序需已就緒，並由權責方審查完畢。
  *The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).*
- 下列準備工作 / 工項需已完成，且在對應之施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 中視適用情況進行簽認。
  *The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.*
	- 現場安裝煙囪段口就位。
	  *Field erected stack sections ready*
	- 煙囪內部骨架安裝完成。
	  *Stack inside wireframe installed*
	- 材料已收訖，並對數量與品質進行檢驗（填寫溢裝、短裝與損壞報告，即 OSD 報告）。
	  *Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report)*

##### 安裝 *Erection*
- 安裝、對合並銲接底部護板。
  *Erect, fit and weld the bottom panels.*
	- 安裝期間檢查底部護板之正確位置（坡度 / 傾角）。
	  *During erection check the correct location (slope) of the bottom panel.*

##### 銲接 *Welding*
- 銲接底部護板。
  *Weld the bottom panels.*
	- 密切遵循圖面與銲接作業程序書 (WPS) 上之銲接細節或型式。
	  *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.*

##### 品質管制 *Quality control*
- 依據適用之施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 與/或程序書完成品質管制工項。
  *Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).*
- 釋出並隨帶未完成事項清單。
  *Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).*

#### 12.1.7. 煙囪擋風門 *Stack damper*

煙囪擋風門在出廠時已經預裝組立完成。參見章節：熱回收鍋爐預組裝。
*The stack damper has already been pre-assembled. See chapter: HRSG Pre-assembly.*
在開始安裝已預裝之煙囪擋風門之前，需提前準備一些工項。
*Before Erection of the pre-assembled stack damper, some activities need to be prepared in advance.*

##### 準備工作與先決條件 *Preparations and preconditions*
- 前述段落中提到之文件與程序需已就緒，並由權責方審查完畢。
  *The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).*
- 下列準備工作 / 工項需已完成，且在對應之施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 中視適用情況進行簽認。
  *The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.*
	- 現場安裝煙囪段口就位。
	  *Field erected stack sections ready*
	- 內部骨架就位。
	  *Inside wireframe ready*
	- 材料已收訖，並對數量與品質進行檢驗（填寫溢裝、短裝與損壞報告，即 OSD 報告）。
	  *Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report)*

##### 釋出後續工項 *Release subsequent activities*
- 隨著本段落工項之成功完成，即可釋出以下工項：
  *With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given:*
	- 剩餘（預組裝）煙囪段口之安裝。
	  *Erection remaining (pre-assembled) stack sections.*
	- 煙囪排水管線。
	  *Stack drain line*

##### 安裝 *Erection*
- 將預組裝之煙囪擋風門安裝至現場已組立之煙囪段口上，包括排水管道系統。
  *Erect the pre-assembled stack damper onto the field installed stack sections including the drain piping system.*
- 對合並點銲煙囪擋風門。
  *Fit and tack-weld the stack damper*
	- 起吊與安裝應依據相關圖面與搬運說明書進行。
	  *Lifting and erection to take place according the relevant drawing and handling instructions.*
	- 供應商文件可參閱文件 60031-730-01-006「供應商防銹保存、搬運與安裝程序書」。
	  *The supplier documentation can be found using document 60031-730-01-006 “Supplier conservation storage, handling and installation procedures”.*
	- 依據施工方法說明書，於點銲對合期間保持吊車連接之懸吊拉力狀態。
	  *Keep the crane connected during the fit-up, as per work method statement.*
	- 安裝期間，檢查煙囪擋風門之位置與對正。
	  *During erection check position and alignment of the stack damper*
	- 點銲固定完成後，拆除臨時運輸用之支撐斜撐。
	  *After tack-welding remove the temporary transport bracings*

##### 銲接 *Welding*
- 將煙囪擋風門銲接至現場已安裝之煙囪段口上。
  *Weld the stack damper to the field installed stack sections*
	- 密切遵循圖面與銲接作業程序書 (WPS) 上之銲接細節或型式。
	  *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.*

##### 品質管制 *Quality control*
- 依據適用之施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 與/或程序書執行品質管制工項。
  *Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).*
- 煙囪擋風門之排水管線應依據「管道系統」章節之要求裝設。
  *Stack damper drain line to be installed based on Chapter “Piping”*
- 擋風門通過驗收後，安裝驅動器、驅動器連接件與防護罩。
  *After acceptance of the damper install the driver, driver connection and protection.*
- 拆除煙囪內部之臨時施工架後，進行手動試運轉，以確認擋風門葉片能否自由無阻礙地動作。
  *After removal of the internal scaffolding stack perform a trial run (by hand) to verify free movement of the damper blades.*

#### 12.1.8. 剩餘之預組裝煙囪段口 *Remaining -pre-assembled- stack sections*

針對預組裝之煙囪段口，請遵循前文「接續之煙囪段口」段落中指示之步驟，進行剩餘預組裝煙囪段口之安裝 / 銲接與品質管制。
*For the pre-assembled stack sections, follow steps as indicated in the previous paragraph “Subsequent stack sections” for the erection/welding and quality control of the remaining pre-assembled stack sections.*

#### 12.1.9. 煙囪灌漿 *Grouting stack*

煙囪基座鋼底環（鋼底環）之灌漿應依據「無收縮水泥灌漿」章節進行。遵循該章中提到之執行與品質步驟。
*Grouting of the base ring of the stack is based on Chapter “Grouting”. Follow the execution and quality steps mentioned in this chapter.*

#### 12.1.10. 鍋爐煙囪最終檢查 *Final inspection of the boiler stack*

當特定系統或一組特定組件之機械安裝完成後，應進行檢查。未完成項目應彙整於未決點清單內，並檢附於最終檢查合格證書上。
*When the mechanical erection of a certain system, or group of specific components is finalized these shall be inspected. Outstanding items shall be collected in an outstanding items list and attached to the Final inspection Certificate.*

煙囪之最終檢查合格證書中描述了所檢查之系統或組件。
*The Final inspection Certificate of the stack describes the systems or components inspected.*

##### 檢查 *Inspection*
- 最終檢查合格證書中所提及之所有系統或特定組件組，應針對正確安裝、完整性與損壞進行最終檢查。
  *All systems or group of specific components referred to on the Final inspection Certificate shall have a final inspection for correct erection, completeness and damages.*
- 完成現場步行檢查後，應立即建立未完成項目 / 未決點紀錄（如有）。
  *A record of outstanding items (if any) shall be set-up directly after the walk-down.*
- 若有施作未完成項目清單，其應分類為：
  *In case a list of outstanding items is applicable it shall be categorized in :*
	- 水壓試驗前應解決之項目（A 級項目）。
	  *Items to be solved before hydro testing (A-items)*
	- 熱試運轉前應解決之項目（B 級項目）。
	  *Items to be solved before hot-commissioning (B-items)*
	- 初期驗收 (PAC) 前應解決之項目（C 級項目）。
	  *Items to be solved before provisional acceptance (PAC) (C-items)*

確認所涉及系統之適用現場安裝品質計畫書 (FQP) 已由所有權責方簽字認可。未完成項目應納入未決點清單。
*Verify that the applicable site FQPs for the systems involved are signed off by all parties involved. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list*
確認所有不符合事項報告 (NCR) 已關閉。未完成項目應納入未決點清單。
*Verify that all Non-Conformity Reports are closed. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list*

### 12.2. 出口煙道安裝 *Outlet duct erection*

本段落描述出口煙道之安裝。
*This paragraph describes the erection of the outlet duct.*

#### 12.2.1. 一般 *General*

安裝承包商應針對出口煙道之安裝準備施工方法說明書 / 風險評估以及吊裝計畫。
*Work method statements / risk assessments with lifting plans for the erection of the outlet duct shall be prepared by the erection contractor.*
出口煙道之安裝順序示於文件 60031-730-05-001。
*The erection sequence for the outlet duct is shown in document 60031-730-05-001.*

#### 12.2.2. 文件與程序 *Documents and procedures*

- 安裝出口煙道所需之文件與程序。
  *Documents and procedures required for erection of the outlet duct.*

	- 施工方法說明書：安裝煙囪 / 出口煙道。
	  *Work method statement : Erection stack / outlet duct.*
	- 施工方法說明書：搭設煙囪 / 出口煙道施工架。
	  *Work method statement : Erection scaffolding stack / outlet duct.*
	- 施工品質計畫書：熱回收鍋爐出口煙道。
	  *FQP : HRSG outlet duct.*
	- 螺栓緊固程序書：非受壓組件。
	  *Bolt torque procedure : Non pressure parts.*
	- 銲接作業程序書 / 銲接程序資格檢定紀錄 / 銲工資格檢定：非受壓組件。
	  *WPS / PQR / WPQ : Non-pressure parts.*
	- 銲接地圖 / 紀錄：非受壓組件。
	  *Weld typical / record : Non-pressure parts.*
	- 銲接耗材處理程序書：非受壓組件。
	  *Welding consumable handling procedure : Non-pressure parts.*
	- 非破壞檢測程序書 / 人員資格認證：非受壓組件。
	  *NDE procedures / personnel qualifications : Non-pressure parts.*

#### 12.2.3. 出口煙道底部護板安裝 *Erection of outlet duct bottom panel*

在開始安裝出口煙道之前，需提前準備一些工項。
*Before erection of the outlet duct can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance.*

##### 準備工作與先決條件 *Preparations and preconditions*
- 前述段落中提到之文件與程序需已就緒，並由權責方審查完畢。
  *The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).*
- 下列準備工作 / 工項需已完成，且在對應之施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 中視適用情況進行簽認。
  *The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.*
	- 煙囪。
	  *Stack*
	- 鍋爐本體之法蘭連接線。
	  *Flange connection boiler*
	- 材料已收訖，並對數量與品質進行檢驗（填寫溢裝、短裝與損壞報告，即 OSD 報告）。
	  *Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report)*

##### 釋出後續工項 *Release subsequent activities*
- 隨著本段落工項之成功完成，即可釋出以下工項：
  *With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given:*
	- 施工架搭建完畢後安裝右側 / 左側煙道壁板。
	  *erection right / left side ducting panels after scaffolding.*

##### 安裝 *Erection*
- 從鍋爐側至煙囪側，安裝、對合並點銲底部煙道壁板。
  *Erect, fit and tack-weld the bottom ducting panel from the boiler side to the stack side.*
	- 在鍋爐外殼法蘭與底部煙道壁板之間裝設間心定位塊（定位塊應代表膨脹接頭之安裝寬度）。調整法蘭配正，使得法蘭螺栓孔互相對合且朝向彼此。完成正確之對正後，將支撐件與煙囪鋼底環連接。
	  *Place distance holders between the boiler casing flange and the bottom duct (distance holder shall represent the width of the expansion joint). Align the flanges in such way that the flange bolt holes match and are opposite to each other.After correct alignment, connect the supports to the stack base ring.*
	- 當偵測到螺栓孔錯位不對正時，必須與製造商討論評估後始得進行調整。
	  *When a misalignment of the bolt holes is detected, adjustments can be made only after consultation with the manufacturer.*
	- 對齊底部壁板彼此以及煙囪側，必要時調整連接件，並將壁板點銲在一起且銲至煙囪側。
	  *Align the bottom panels to each other and to the stack side, adjust the connections where necessary and tack-weld the panels together and to the stack side.*
	- 必要時可設置臨時支撐件以確保底部壁板之穩定性。
	  *Where necessary place temporary supporting for stability of the bottom panels.*

##### 銲接 *Welding*
- 銲接底部壁板（接頭 / 銜接）與煙囪側之連接件。
  *Weld the bottom ducting (splices) and stack side connection.*
	- 密切遵循圖面與銲接作業程序書 (WPS) 上之銲接細節或型式。
	  *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.*

##### 品質管制 *Quality control*
- 依據適用之施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 與/或程序書執行品質管制工項。
  *Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).*
- 銲接前檢查對合裝配、高程與尺寸。
  *Check fit-up, elevation and dimensions before welding.*
- 釋出並隨帶未完成事項清單。
  *Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).*

#### 12.2.4. 出口煙道外部施工架搭設（右側或左側） *Scaffolding outlet duct (right or left) “outside”*

安裝承包商應針對施工架之搭設準備施工方法說明書 / 風險評估與吊裝吊運計畫。
*Work method statements / risk assessments with lifting plans for erection of scaffolding, shall be prepared by the erection contractor.*
在開始搭設出口煙道施工架之前，需提前準備一些工項。
*Before erection of the outlet duct scaffolding can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance.*

##### 準備工作與先決條件 *Preparations and preconditions*
- 前述段落中提到之文件與程序需已就緒，並由權責方審查完畢。
  *The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).*
- 下列準備工作 / 工項需已完成，且在對應之施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 中視適用情況進行簽認。
  *The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.*
	- 出口煙道底部壁板已完成安裝。
	  *Bottom outlet duct panel installed*

##### 釋出後續工項 *Release subsequent activities*
- 隨著本段落工項之成功完成，即可釋出以下工項：
  *With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given:*
	- 安裝右側 / 左側煙道壁板。
	  *Erection right / left side ducting panels.*

##### 安裝 *Erection*
- 施工架應沿著出口煙道右側或左側之「外部」搭設。
  *Scaffolding to be erected along the “outside” of the outlet duct right or left side.*
	- 施工架之搭設應確保所有待安裝之組件均可便利到達。
	  *Erect the scaffolding in such way that all components to be erected can be easily reached.*

##### 品質管制 *Quality control*
- 依據適用之施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 與/或程序書執行品質管制工項。
  *Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).*
- 確認施工架之進出動線及組立正確無誤。
  *Verify scaffolding for proper access and assembly.*

#### 12.2.5. 出口煙道右側或左側壁板 *Outlet duct right or left panel*

在先前步驟搭設施工架之那一側安裝出口煙道側壁板。
*Erect the outlet duct sidewall on the side where the scaffolding is erected during the previous step.*
在開始安裝出口煙道側壁板之前，需提前準備一些工項。
*Before erection of the outlet duct side panel can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance.*

##### 準備工作與先決條件 *Preparations and preconditions*
- 前述段落中提到之文件與程序需已就緒，並由權責方審查完畢。
  *The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).*
- 下列準備工作 / 工項需已完成，且在對應之施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 中視適用情況進行簽認。
  *The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.*
	- 出口煙道底部壁板安裝就位。
	  *Bottom outlet duct panel erected*
	- 出口煙道右側或左側之施工架搭設完成。
	  *Scaffolding outlet duct right or left side erected*

##### 釋出後續工項 *Release subsequent activities*
- 隨著本段落工項之成功完成，即可釋出以下工項：
  *With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given:*
	- 安裝出口煙道對側壁板。
	  *Erection outlet duct opposite side wall panels*

##### 安裝 *Erection*
- 從鍋爐至煙囪，安裝、對合並點銲右側或左側之出口側壁板。
  *Erect, fit and tack-weld the right or left outlet side wall panels between the boiler and stack*
	- 在鍋爐外殼法蘭與側壁銲合管道之間裝設間心定位塊（定位塊應代表膨脹接頭之安裝寬度）。調整法蘭配正，使得法蘭螺栓孔互相對合且朝向彼此。
	  *Place distance holders between the boiler casing flange and the sidewall ducting (distance holder shall represent the width of the expansion joint). Align the flanges in such way that the flange bolt holes match and are opposite to each other.*
	- 當偵測到螺栓孔不合錯位時，必須與製造商討論評估後始得進行調整。
	  *When a misalignment of the bolt holes is detected, adjustments can be made only after consultation with the manufacturer.*
	- 對齊側壁壁板彼此以及煙囪側，必要時調整連接件，並將壁板點銲在一起且銲至煙囪側。
	  *Align the sidewall panels to each other and to the stack side, adjust the connections where necessary and tack-weld the panels together and to the stack side.*
	- 必要時設置臨時支撐件。
	  *Where necessary place temporary supporting.*

##### 銲接 *Welding*
- 銲接側壁護牆（銜接組對）與煙囪側之連接件。
  *Weld the sidewall ducting (splices) and stack side connections.*
- 將側壁護牆銲接至底部壁板。
  *Weld the sidewall ducting to the bottom ducting.*

##### 品質管制 *Quality control*
- 依據適用之施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 與/或程序書執行品質管制工項。
  *Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).*
- 銲接前檢查對合裝配、高程與尺寸。
  *Check fit-up, elevation and dimensions before welding.*
- 釋出並隨帶未完成事項清單。
  *Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).*

#### 12.2.6. 對側出口煙道施工架搭設 *Scaffolding outlet duct opposite side*

在先前搭設之出口煙道側壁施工架之對側，搭建出口煙道施工架。
*Erect the outlet duct scaffolding on the opposite side of the previously erected outlet duct sidewall scaffolding.*
相關要求另見第 12.2.4 節。
*For requirements see also chapter 11.2.4.*

#### 12.2.7. 對側出口煙道側壁護牆 *Outlet duct opposite sidewall casing*

在開始安裝剩餘之側壁煙道壁板之前，需提前準備一些工項。
*Before erection of the remaining sidewall ducting panels can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance.*

##### 準備工作與先決條件 *Preparations and preconditions*
- 前述段落中提到之文件與程序需已就緒，並由權責方審查完畢。
  *The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).*
- 下列準備工作 / 工項需已完成，且在對應之施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 中視適用情況進行簽認。
  *The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.*
	- 出口煙道消音器（導流消音板）已完成安裝。
	  *Outlet duct baffles (silencers) installed*

##### 釋出後續工項 *Release subsequent activities*
- 隨著本段落工項之成功完成，即可釋出以下工項：
  *With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given:*
	- 安裝出口煙道頂部壁板。
	  *Installation outlet duct top panels.*

##### 安裝 *Erection*
- 在鍋爐與煙囪之間安裝、對合並點銲對側之出口側壁板，並於右側與左側出口煙道壁板之間安裝支撐框架（加強拉撐）。
  *Erect, fit and tack-weld the opposite outlet side wall panels between the boiler and stack and the bracing frame between the right and left outlet duct side walls*
	- 在鍋爐外殼法蘭與側壁壁板之間裝設定位墊塊（定位塊應代表膨脹接頭之安裝寬度）。調整法蘭配正，以使法蘭螺栓孔相互吻合且位置相對。
	  *Place distance holders between the boiler casing flange and the sidewall ducting (distance holder shall represent the width of the expansion joint). Align the flanges in such way that the flange bolt holes match and are opposite to each other.*
	- 當偵測到螺栓孔不合錯位時，必須與製造商討論評估後始得進行調整。
	  *When a misalignment of the bolt holes is detected, adjustments can be made only after consultation with the manufacturer.*
	- 將側壁壁板彼此以及對著煙囪側對齊，必要時調整連接件，並將壁板點銲在一起及銲接至煙囪側。
	  *Align the sidewall panels to each other and to the stack side, adjust the connections where necessary and tack-weld the panels together and to the stack side.*
	- 必要時設置臨時支撐件。
	  *Where necessary place temporary supporting.*

##### 銲接 *Welding*
- 銲接側壁壁板（銜接組對）與煙囪側之連接件。
  *Weld the sidewall ducting (splices) and stack side connections.*
- 將側壁壁板銲接至底部壁板。
  *Weld the sidewall ducting to the bottom ducting.*
	- 密切遵循圖面與銲接作業程序書 (WPS) 上之銲接細節或型式。
	  *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.*

##### 品質管制 *Quality control*
- 依據施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 與/或程序書執行品質管制工項。
  *Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).*
- 銲接前檢查對合裝配、高程與尺寸。
  *Check fit-up, elevation and dimensions before welding.*
- 釋出並隨帶未完成事項清單。
  *Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).*

#### 12.2.8. 出口煙道導流消音片 *Outlet duct baffles (silencers)*

在開始安裝出口煙道導流消音片之前，需提前準備一些工項。
*Before erection of the outlet duct baffles can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance.*

##### 準備工作與先決條件 *Preparations and preconditions*
- 前述段落中提到之文件與程序需已就緒，並由權責方審查完畢。
  *The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).*
- 下列準備工作 / 工項需已完成，且在對應之施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 中視適用情況進行簽認。
  *The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.*
	- 出口煙道底部壁板裝設就位。
	  *Bottom outlet duct panel installed*
	- 出口煙道右側或左側壁板一側裝設就位。
	  *Outlet duct right or left side panel installed*

##### 釋出後續工項 *Release subsequent activities*
- 隨著本段落工項之成功完成，即可釋出以下工項：
  *With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given:*
	- 安裝出口煙道剩餘之側壁壁板。
	  *Erection outlet duct remaining sidewall panels.*

##### 安裝 *Erection*
- 安裝、對合並點銲下方出口煙道導流消音板之底部支撐系統。
  *Install, fit and tack-weld the support system for the lower outlet duct baffles (silencers).*
	- 組對完成後對支撐件執行尺寸查核。
	  *Perform a dimensional check of the supports after fit-up.*
- 安裝下方消音片。自出口煙道壁板已安裝之那一側開始位置起吊裝。
  *Install the lower outlet baffles. Start the erection from the side where the outlet duct casing is already installed.*
	- 遵循相關消音器供應商之安裝指引與圖部細節。
	  *Follow the supplier erection instructions and drawing details for lifting and erection.*
	- 安裝期間檢查消音片之位置與高程。
	  *During erection check position and elevation of the baffles*
	- 確認消音片裝配於支撐系統內，且無受損傷。
	  *Verify the baffles are mounted in the support system without damaging the baffles.*
	- 安裝期間加設連接壓條（連接板條），並施加正確之螺栓緊固扭矩力。
	  *Install the connection strips during erection and apply the correct torque for bolting.*
	- 安裝完成後，拆除吊裝用之吊耳螺栓。
	  *Remove the lifting eye-bolts after erection.*
- 煙囪及煙道段搭建施工架。
  *Erection of scaffolding for the outlet sections*
	- 施工架應搭設至出口消音片之上游與下游。
	  *Scaffolding to be placed up and downstream of the outlet baffles.*

##### 銲接 *Welding*
- 銲接下方消音片之支撐系統。
  *Weld the lower baffle support system.*
	- 密切遵循圖面與型式，以及銲接作業程序書 (WPS) 上之銲接要求。
	  *Follow the details and typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.*
- 將上方消音片安裝於下方消音片之上方。自出口煙道壁板已安裝之那一側開始吊裝。
  *Install the upper outlet baffles on top of the lower outlet baffles. Start the erection from the side where the outlet duct casing is already installed.*
	- 起吊運輸，遵循供應商之安裝說明與圖式明細。
	  *Follow the supplier erection instructions and drawing details for lifting and erection.*
	- 安裝期間，檢查消音片之位置與高程。
	  *During erection check position and elevation of the baffles*
	- 安裝期間設置連接條，並施加正確之螺栓緊固扭矩力。
	  *Install the connection strips during erection and apply the correct torque for bolting.*
	- 安裝完成後，拆除吊裝用之吊座吊耳螺栓。
	  *Remove the lifting eye-bolts after erection.*

##### 品質管制 *Quality control*
- 依據施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 與/或程序書完成品質管制工項。
  *Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).*
- 釋出並隨帶未完成事項清單。
  *Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).*
- 在出口煙道頂部鋼殼蓋板驗收後，始得安裝上方消音片之頂支撐系統。
  *The upper baffle support system is installed after acceptance of the outlet duct top casing.*

#### 12.2.9. 出口煙道頂部蓋板 *Outlet duct top panel*

在開始安裝出口煙道頂部蓋板之前，需提前準備一些工項。
*Before erection of the outlet top panels can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance.*

##### 準備工作與先決條件 *Preparations and preconditions*
- 前述段落中提到之文件與程序需已就緒，並由權責方審查完畢。
  *The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).*
- 下列準備工作 / 工項需已完成，且在對應之施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 中視適用情況進行簽認。
  *The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.*
	- 出口煙道左側與右側壁板安裝就位。
	  *Outlet duct left and right sidewall panels erected*

##### 釋出後續工項 *Release subsequent activities*
- 隨著本段落工項之成功完成，即可釋出以下工項：
  *With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given:*
	- 安裝出口煙道與鍋爐本體之間的膨脹接頭（伸縮補償器）。
	  *Erection expansion joint between outlet duct and boiler.*
	- 出口煙道上方消音片頂部支撐系統。
	  *Upper stack baffle support system.*

##### 安裝 *Erection*
- 自鍋爐側至煙囪側，安裝、對合並點銲出口煙道頂部蓋板。
  *Erect, fit and tack-weld the outlet top panels from the boiler side to the stack side.*
	- 在鍋爐本體外殼法蘭與頂部煙道鋼蓋板之間設置定位間心塊（定位塊應代表膨脹接頭之安裝淨寬度）。調整法蘭，使法蘭螺栓孔兩兩對正且在對立位置。
	  *Place distance holders between the boiler casing flange and the top ducting (distance holder shall represent the width of the expansion joint). Align the flanges in such way that the flange bolt holes match and are opposite to each other.*
	- 當偵測到螺栓孔不合錯位時，必須與製造商討論評估後始得進行調整。
	  *When a misalignment of the bolt holes is detected, adjustments can be made only after consultation with the manufacturer.*
	- 對合頂部蓋板彼此以及對齊煙囪側，必要時調整連接件，並將壁板點銲在一起及銲接至煙囪側。
	  *Align the top panels to each other and to the stack side, adjust the connections where necessary and tack-weld the panels together and to the stack side.*

##### 銲接 *Welding*
- 銲接頂部蓋板（銜接銲道）與煙囪側之連接銲縫。
  *Weld the top ducting (splices) and the stack side connections.*
- 將頂部蓋板銲接至側壁護板。
  *Weld the top ducting to the sidewall ducting.*
	- 密切遵循圖面與銲接作業程序書 (WPS) 上之銲接細節或型式。
	  *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.*

##### 品質管制 *Quality control*
- 依據施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 與/或程序書完成品質管制工項。
  *Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).*
- 銲接前檢查組組對、高程與尺寸。
  *Check fit-up, elevation and dimensions before welding.*
- 依據本章「出口煙道導流消音板」段落所述，安裝出口煙道上方消音片之頂支撐系統。
  *Erection of outlet duct upper baffle support system as per paragraph “outlet duct baffles”, located in this chapter.*
- 釋出並隨帶未完成事項清單。
  *Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).*

#### 12.2.10. 出口煙道最終檢查 *Final inspection of the outlet duct*

當特定系統或一組特定組件之機械安裝完成後，應進行檢查。未完成項目應彙整於未決點清單內，並檢附於最終檢查合格證書上。
*When the mechanical erection of a certain system, or group of specific components is finalized these shall be inspected. Outstanding items shall be collected in an outstanding items list and attached to the Final inspection Certificate.*

出口煙道之最終檢查合格證書中描述了所檢查之系統或組件。
*The Final inspection Certificate of the outlet duct describes the systems or components inspected.*

##### 檢查 *Inspection*
- 最終檢查合格證書中所提及之所有系統或特定組件組，應針對正確安裝、完整性與損壞進行最終檢查。
  *All systems or group of specific components referred to on the Final inspection Certificate shall have a final inspection for correct erection, completeness and damages.*
- 完成現場步行檢查後，應立即建立未完成項目 / 未決點紀錄（如有）。
  *A record of outstanding items (if any) shall be set-up directly after the walk-down.*
- 若有施作未完成項目清單，其應分類為：
  *In case a list of outstanding items is applicable it shall be categorized in :*
	- 水壓試驗前應解決之項目（A 級項目）。
	  *Items to be solved before hydro testing (A-items)*
	- 熱試運轉前應解決之項目（B 級項目）。
	  *Items to be solved before hot-commissioning (B-items)*
	- 初期驗收 (PAC) 前應解決之項目（C 級項目）。
	  *Items to be solved before provisional acceptance (PAC) (C-items)*

確認所涉及系統之適用現場安裝品質計畫書 (FQP) 已由所有權責方簽字認可。未完成項目應納入未決點清單。
*Verify that the applicable site FQPs for the systems involved are signed off by all parties involved. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list*
確認所有不符合事項報告 (NCR) 已關閉。未完成項目應納入未決點清單。
*Verify that all Non-Conformity Reports are closed. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list.*


## 13. 進口煙道 *INLET DUCT*

本章包含以下段落：
*This chapter contains the following paragraphs:*

1. 進口煙道主鋼構：第 13.1 節
   *Inlet duct main steel structure : paragraph 13.1*
2. 進口煙道安裝：第 13.2 節
   *Inlet Duct erection : paragraph 13.2*
3. 進口煙道最終檢查：第 13.3 節
   *Final inspection of the inlet duct : paragraph 13.3*

### 13.1. 進口煙道主鋼構 *Inlet duct main steel structure*

本段落描述進口煙道主鋼構之安裝。
*This paragraph describes the erection of the inlet duct main steel structure.*

#### 13.1.1. 一般 *General*

進口煙道由包含底部、側部與頂部煙道之主鋼構組成。進口煙道直接連接至熱回收鍋爐 (HRSG) 煙道。為補償安裝與製造公差，連接至氣渦輪機 (GT) 煙道之膨脹接頭（伸縮補償器）法蘭連接線，設有可調式法蘭連接結構。
*The inlet duct consists out of a main steel structure containing the bottom, side and top ducting. The inlet duct is connected directly to the HRSG duct. In order to compensate for erection and fabrication tolerance the flange connection for the compensator to the GT duct contains an adjustable flange connection.*
進口煙道之安裝係從熱回收鍋爐煙道側往進口煙道側方向進行。
*Erection of the inlet duct takes place from the HRSG duct towards to inlet duct.*
安裝承包商應針對進口煙道主鋼構之安裝準備施工方法說明書 / 風險評估以及吊裝計畫。
*Work method statements / risk assessments with lifting plans for the erection of the inlet duct main steel structure shall be prepared by the erection contractor.*
進口煙道主鋼構之安裝順序示於文件 60031-730-05-001。
*The erection sequence for the inlet duct main steel structure is shown in document 60031-730-05-001.*

#### 13.1.2. 文件與程序 *Documents and procedures*

- 安裝進口煙道主鋼構所需之文件與程序。
  *Documents and procedures required for erection of the inlet duct main steel structure.*
	- 施工方法說明書：安裝進口煙道。
	  *Work method statement : Erection inlet duct.*
	- 施工品質計畫書：熱回收鍋爐進口煙道。
	  *FQP : HRSG inlet duct.*
	- 螺栓緊固程序書：非受壓組件。
	  *Bolt torque procedure : Non pressure parts.*
	- 銲接作業程序書 / 銲接程序資格檢定紀錄 / 銲工資格檢定：非受壓組件。
	  *WPS / PQR / WPQ : Non-pressure parts.*
	- 銲接地圖 / 紀錄：非受壓組件。
	  *Weld typical / record : Non-pressure parts.*
	- 銲接耗材處理程序書：非受壓組件。
	  *Welding consumable handling procedure : Non-pressure parts.*
	- 非破壞檢測程序書 / 人員資格認證：非受壓組件。
	  *NDE procedures / personnel qualifications : Non-pressure parts.*

#### 13.1.3. 鋼結構 *Steel structure*

在開始安裝鋼結構排架（門架）之前，需提前準備一些工項。
*Before erection of the steel structure rows can start, some activities need to be prepared in advance.*

##### 準備工作與先決條件 *Preparations and preconditions*
- 前述段落中提到之文件與程序需已就緒，並由權責方審查完畢。
  *The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).*
- 下列準備工作 / 工項需已完成，且在對應之施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 中視適用情況進行簽認。
  *The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.*
	- 基礎已就緒。
	  *Foundation ready*
	- 材料已收訖，並對數量與品質進行檢驗（填寫溢裝、短裝與損壞報告，即 OSD 報告）。
	  *Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report)*
- 在放置排架門柱之前，先在底座鋼板下方安裝調整墊片，並調整至正確之高程。
  *Erect the shims underneath the base plates before placement of the goalpost and level to the correct elevation.*
	- 極為重要之步驟是，（用於整平進口煙道鋼結構門架之）調整墊片必須位於底座鋼板下方，且不得突出。
	  *It is important that the shims (for levelling of the inlet duct steel structure portals) are underneath the base plates and do not protrude.*

##### 釋出後續工項 *Release subsequent activities*
- 隨著本段落工項之成功完成，即可釋出以下工項：
  *With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given:*
	- 安裝進口煙道底部壁板。
	  *Erection Inlet duct bottom panels.*

##### 安裝 *Erection*
- 安裝進口煙道之主鋼構排架排數。
  *Erect the main steel goalpost rows for the inlet duct.*
- 視適用情況，安裝帶有承壓板與 2 mm PTFE 滑動板之門架結構。
  *Erect the goalpost with the bearing plate and the 2 mm PTFE sliding plate, where applicable.*
在裝設於 PTFE 滑動板上之前，確認承壓板之清潔度。
*Verify cleanliness of the bearing plate before installation onto the PFTE sliding plate.*
- 安裝期間，檢查進口煙道主鋼構之位置、對正與高程。
  *During erection check for position, alignment and elevation of the inlet duct main steel structure.*
必要時使用牽索（拉線）及/或整平螺帽調整位置。
*Adjust position using the guy-wires and/or leveling nuts where required.*
- 一旦鋼結構調整定位後，將錨定螺栓緊固至其最終扭矩值。
  *Tighten the anchors bolts to their final torque value, once the steel structure is adjusted.*
	- 安裝期間密切監控鋼結構之位置坐標。
	  *Closely monitor the steel structure coordinates during installation.*
	- 鋼結構定位後，對正確位置、對正與高程進行精密測繪。
	  *Perform a survey for correct position, alignment and elevation of the steel structure when in position.*
	- 使用適用之扭矩值緊固錨定螺栓。
	  *Use the applicable torque value for tightening of the anchor bolts.*
	- 當偵測到螺栓孔錯位不對準時，必須與製造商討論評估後始得進行調整。
	  *When a misalignment of the bolt holes is detected, adjustments can be made only after consultation with the manufacturer.*

##### 品質管制 *Quality control*
- 依據施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 與/或程序書完成品質管制工項。
  *Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).*
- 将測繪尺寸報告與製造商之公差圖面進行比對。
  *Compare the dimensional reports of the survey with the manufacturer tolerance drawings.*
- 釋出並隨帶未完成事項清單。
  *Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).*

### 13.2. 進口煙道安裝 *Inlet Duct erection*

本段落描述進口煙道壁板之安裝。
*This paragraph describes the erection of the ducting panels for the inlet duct.*

#### 13.2.1. 一般 *General*

安裝承包商應針對進口煙道壁板之安裝準備施工方法說明書 / 風險評估以及吊裝計畫。
*Work method statements / risk assessments with lifting plans for the erection of the inlet duct panels shall be prepared by the erection contractor.*
進口煙道之安裝順序示於文件 60031-730-05-001。
*The erection sequence for the inlet duct is shown in document 60031-730-05-001.*

#### 13.2.2. 文件與程序 *Documents and procedures*

- 安裝進口煙道壁板所需之文件與程序。
  *Documents and procedures required for installation of the inlet duct panels.*
	- 施工方法說明書：安裝進口煙道。
	  *Work method statement : Erection inlet duct.*
	- 施工方法說明書：搭設進口煙道施工架。
	  *Work method statement : Erection scaffolding inlet duct.*
	- 施工品質計畫書：熱回收鍋爐進口煙道。
	  *FQP : HRSG inlet duct.*
	- 螺栓緊固程序書：非受壓組件。
	  *Bolt torque procedure : Non pressure parts.*
	- 銲接作業程序書 / 銲接程序資格檢定紀錄 / 銲工資格檢定：非受壓組件。
	  *WPS / PQR / WPQ : Non-pressure parts.*
	- 銲接地圖 / 紀錄：非受壓組件。
	  *Weld typical / record : Non-pressure parts.*
	- 銲接耗材處理程序書：非受壓組件。
	  *Welding consumable handling procedure : Non-pressure parts.*
	- 非破壞檢測程序書 / 人員資格認證：非受壓組件。
	  *NDE procedures / personnel qualifications : Non-pressure parts.*

#### 13.2.3. 進口煙道底部壁板 *Inlet duct bottom panels*

在開始安裝進口煙道底部壁板之前，需提前準備一些工項。
*Before Erection of the inlet duct bottom panels can start, some activities need to be prepared in advance.*

##### 準備工作與先決條件 *Preparations and preconditions*
- 前述段落中提到之文件與程序需已就緒，並由權責方審查完畢。
  *The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).*
- 下列準備工作 / 工項需已完成，且在對應之施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 中視適用情況進行簽認。
  *The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.*
	- 進口煙道鋼結構。
	  *Steel structure inlet duct*
	- 材料已收訖，並對數量與品質進行檢驗（填寫溢裝、短裝與損壞報告，即 OSD 報告）。
	  *Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report)*
- 準備用於進口煙道外殼壁板安裝之施工架及/或高空作業車。
  *Prepare the scaffolding and or sky climbers for installation of the inlet duct casing panels.*
- 準備安裝進口煙道所需之工具。
  *Prepare the tools required for erection of the inlet duct.*

##### 釋出後續工項 *Release subsequent activities*
- 隨著本段落工項之成功完成，即可釋出以下工項：
  *With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given:*
	- 進口煙道側壁壁板。
	  *Sidewall panels inlet duct.*
	- 底部現場銜接縫之內部保溫。
	  *Internal insulation of bottom splices.*

##### 安裝 *Erection*
- 安裝、對合並點銲底部煙道壁板至進口煙道鋼結構與鍋爐外殼。
  *Erect, fit and tack-weld the bottom duct panels to the inlet duct steel structure and the boiler casing.*
	- 進口煙道底部壁板之安裝係從鍋爐側朝向氣渦輪機側進行，因為用於補償安裝與製造公差之可調式法蘭連接結構，位於與氣渦輪機連接之部位。
	  *The inlet duct bottom panel erection is done from the boiler side to the gas turbine side, as the adjustable flange connection (In order to compensate for erection and fabrication tolerances) is located at the connection with the gas turbine.*
	- 安裝底部壁板期間，將支撐件安裝至鋼結構底樑上並進行點銲。
	  *During erection of the bottom duct, erect the supports on the steel structure bottom girders and tack weld.*
	- 將底部壁板對齊至正確之位置與高程。
	  *Align the bottom duct panels to the correct position and elevation.*
	- 無縫對合所有底部壁板。
	  *Fit all bottom duct panels without gaps.*
	- 當偵測到螺栓孔錯位不對正時，必須與製造商討論評估後始得進行調整。
	  *When a misalignment of the bolt holes is detected, adjustments can be made only after consultation with the manufacturer.*

##### 銲接 *Welding*
- 銲接所有底部銜接縫與所有支撐件。
  *Weld all bottom splices and all supports.*
	- 進口煙道外殼之銲接為連續銲，不得使用間斷銲（跳銲）。依圖面要求進行外部及/或內部銲接。
	  *Inlet duct casing welding is continuous, no stitch welding. Weld outside and/or inside as per drawings.*
	- 槽鐵端部必須進行密封銲。在安裝端板（封頭板）之前，準備（研磨平整）用以安裝端板之表面。
	  *Channel ends need to be seal welded. Before erecting the head plates prepare (grind smooth) the surface for erection of the head plates.*
	- 遵循圖面上銲接地圖與銲接作業程序書 (WPS) 之要求。
	  *Follow the requirements of the weld typical on the drawings and WPS.*

##### 品質管制 *Quality control*
- 依據施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 與/或程序書完成品質管制工項。
  *Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).*
- 銲接前檢查底部煙道支撐與連接板之組對、高程與中心線。
  *Check fit-up, elevations and centerline of the bottom ducting supports and connection plate before welding.*
- 釋出並隨帶未完成事項清單。
  *Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).*

#### 13.2.4. 進口煙道側壁壁板 *Inlet duct sidewall panels*

在開始安裝側壁壁板之前，需提前準備一些工項。
*Before erection of the side wall panels can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance.*

##### 準備工作與先決條件 *Preparations and preconditions*
- 前述段落中提到之文件與程序需已就緒，並由權責方審查完畢。
  *The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).*
- 下列準備工作 / 工項需已完成，且在對應之施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 中視適用情況進行簽認。
  *The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.*
	- 進口煙道底部壁板裝設就位。
	  *Bottom panels inlet duct erected*
	- 材料已收訖，並對數量與品質進行檢驗（填寫溢裝、短裝與損壞報告，即 OSD 報告）。
	  *Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report)*

##### 釋出後續工項 *Release subsequent activities*
- 隨著本段落工項之成功完成，即可釋出以下工項：
  *With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given:*
	- 進口煙道頂部壁板。
	  *Top wall panels inlet duct.*
	- 現場銜接縫之內部保溫。
	  *Internal insulation of field splices.*

##### 安裝 *Erection*
- 安裝、組對並點銲側壁板。安裝期間，在適用之處，將支撐件與進口煙道主鋼構進行連接。
  *Erect, fit and tack-weld side wall duct panels. During erection make the support connections to the inlet duct main steel structure where applicable.*
	- 側壁板之安裝係從鍋爐側朝向氣渦輪機側進行，因為用於補償安裝與製造公差之可調式法蘭連接結構，位於與氣渦輪機連接之部位。
	  *Side wall ducting to be erected from the boiler side to the gas turbine side, as the adjustable flange connection (In order to compensate for erection and fabrication tolerances) is located at the connection with the gas turbine.*
	- 在側壁煙道安裝期間，將各排架之支撐件安裝至鋼結構支柱。
	  *During erection of the side duct, install the supports to the steel structure columns for each row.*
	- 無縫將側壁板與底部壁板對齊組對。
	  *Fit the duct sidewalls to the bottom panels without gaps.*
	- 煙道必須具備氣密性，角隅部與現場銜接縫處之所有縫隙均應使用鋼板（6 mm 厚度）進行封閉（密封銲）。
	  *Ducting has to be gastight, all gaps in corners and at field splices shall be closed (seal welded) with plate (6 mm thickness).*
	- 當偵測到螺栓孔錯位不對正時，必須與製造商討論評估後始得進行調整。
	  *When a misalignment of the bolt holes is detected, adjustments can be made only after consultation with the manufacturer.*

##### 側壁煙道銲接 *Welding side ducting*
- 銲接所有側壁壁板之銜接縫。
  *Weld all side wall panel splices.*
- 銲接側壁壁板與底部壁板之間的角隅部連接線。
  *Weld the corner connections between the sidewall panels and the bottom panels.*
- 將進口煙道側壁與鍋爐側進行銲接。
  *Weld the inlet duct side wall to the boiler side.*
- 銲接所有支撐件。
  *Weld all supports.*
	- 進口煙道外殼之銲接為連續銲，不得使用間斷銲（跳銲）。依圖面進行外部及/或內部銲接。
	  *Inlet duct casing welding is continuous, no stitch welding.Welding outside and/or inside as per drawings.*
	- 遵循圖面上銲接地圖與銲接作業程序書 (WPS) 之要求。
	  *Follow the requirements of the weld typical on the drawings and WPS.*

##### 品質管制 *Quality control*
- 依據施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 與/或程序書完成品質管制工項。
  *Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).*
- 銲接前檢查側壁壁板與底部煙道壁板之組對、高程與連接處。
  *Check fit-up, elevations and side wall connection to the bottom ducting before welding*
- 釋出並隨帶未完成事項清單。
  *Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).*

#### 13.2.5. 進口煙道頂部壁板 *Inlet duct top panels*

在開始安裝頂部壁板之前，需提前準備一些工項。
*Before Erection of the top wall panels can start, some activities need to be prepared in advance.*

##### 準備工作與先決條件 *Preparations and preconditions*
- 前述段落中提到之文件與程序需已就緒，並由權責方審查完畢。
  *The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).*
- 下列準備工作 / 工項需已完成，且在對應之施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 中視適用情況進行簽認。
  *The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.*
	- 進口煙道側壁壁板完成安裝。
	  *Sidewall panels inlet duct erected*
	- 材料已收訖，並對數量與品質進行檢驗（填寫溢裝、短裝與損壞報告，即 OSD 報告）。
	  *Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report)*

##### 釋出後續工項 *Release subsequent activities*
- 隨著本段落工項之成功完成，即可釋出以下工項：
  *With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given:*
	- 現場銜接縫之內部保溫。
	  *Internal insulation field splices.*
	- 現場安裝組件。
	  *Erection field parts.*
	- 鋼結構排架基座之水泥灌漿。
	  *Grouting steel structure rows.*

##### 安裝 *Erection*
- 安裝、組對並點銲頂部煙道壁板，包含其與鋼結構之支撐連接。
  *Erect, fit and tack-weld the top duct, incl. supports to the steel structure.*
	- 頂部煙道壁板之安裝係從鍋爐側朝向氣渦輪機側進行，因為用於補償安裝與製造公差之可調式法蘭連接結構，位於與氣渦輪機連接之部位。
	  *Top duct to be erected from the boiler side to the gas turbine side, as the adjustable flange connection (In order to compensate for erection and fabrication tolerances) is located at the connection with the gas turbine.*
	- 安裝頂部煙道壁板期間，將各排排架之支撐件安裝至鋼結構。
	  *During erection of the top duct, erect the supports to the steel structure for each row*
	- 無縫將頂部煙道與側壁壁板外殼組對。
	  *Fit the top duct to the sidewall casing without gaps.*
	- 煙道必須具備氣密性，角隅部與現場銜接縫處之所有縫隙均應使用鋼板（6 mm 厚度）封閉（密封銲）。
	  *Ducting has to be gastight, all gaps in corners and at field splices have to be closed (seal welded) with plate (6 mm thickness).*
	- 當偵測到螺栓孔錯位不對正時，必須與製造商討論評估後始得進行調整。
	  *When a misalignment of the bolt holes is detected, adjustments can be made only after consultation with the manufacturer.*

##### 銲接 *Welding*
- 銲接所有頂部煙道壁板之銜接縫。
  *Weld all top duct panel splices.*
- 銲接側壁壁板與頂部壁板之間的角隅部連接線。
  *Weld the corner connections between the sidewall panels and the top panels.*
- 將進口煙道頂部與鍋爐外殼進行銲接。
  *Weld the inlet duct top to the boiler casing.*
- 銲接所有支撐件。
  *Weld all supports.*
	- 進口煙道外殼之銲接為連續銲，不得使用間斷銲（跳銲）。依圖面進行外部及/或內部銲接。
	  *Inlet duct casing welding is continuous, no stitch welding. Weld outside and/or inside as per drawings.*
	- 槽鐵端部必須密封銲。在安裝端板之前，準備（研磨平整）用以安裝端板之承面。
	  *Channel ends need to be seal welded. Before installing the head plates prepare (grind smooth) the surface for installation of the head plates.*
	- 遵循圖面銲接地圖與銲接作業程序書 (WPS) 之要求。
	  *Follow the requirements of the weld typical on the drawings and WPS.*

##### 品質管制 *Quality control*
- 依據施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 與/或程序書完成品質管制工項。
  *Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).*
- 銲接前檢查頂部煙道壁板與側壁煙道壁板之組對、高程與連接處。
  *Check fit-up, elevations and top wall connection to the side ducting before welding*
- 釋出並隨帶未完成事項清單。
  *Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).*

#### 13.2.6. 鋼結構灌漿 *Grouting of the steel structure*

進口煙道支撐鋼結構之灌漿應依據本手冊之「無收縮水泥灌漿」章節進行。施工期間遵循該章節提到之安裝與品質步驟。
*Grouting of the inlet duct steel structure is based on the Chapter “Grouting” in this manual. Follow the erection and quality steps mentioned in this chapter during execution.*

#### 13.2.7. 現場安裝組件 *Field parts*

在開始安裝現場安裝組件之前，需提前準備一些工項。
*Before erection of the field parts can start, some activities need to be prepared in advance.*

##### 準備工作與先決條件 *Preparations and preconditions*
- 前述段落中提到之文件與程序需已就緒，並由權責方審查完畢。
  *The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).*
- 下列準備工作 / 工項需已完成，且在對應之施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 中視適用情況進行簽認。
  *The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.*
	- 進口煙道頂部壁板完成安裝。
	  *Top wall panels inlet duct erected*
	- 材料已收訖，並對數量與品質進行檢驗（填寫溢裝、短裝與損壞報告，即 OSD 報告）。
	  *Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report)*

##### 釋出後續工項 *Release subsequent activities*
- 隨著本段落工項之成功完成，即可釋出以下工項：
  *With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given:*
	- 進口煙道可調式法蘭連接結構。
	  *Inlet duct adjustable flange connection.*

##### 安裝 *Erection*
- 安裝、組對並點銲端板以及與側壁外殼連接之連接板。
  *Erect, fit and tack-weld the head plates, connection plates for connection to the side wall casing.*
	- 安裝端板期間，確認槽鐵端部之銲接已完成並研磨平整。
	  *During erection of the head plates verify the weld on the channel ends is in place and grind smooth.*
	- 依據適用圖面上之型式示範，安裝所有現場安裝組件。
	  *Erect all field parts according the typical on the applicable drawings.*

##### 銲接 *Welding*
- 銲接所有現場安裝組件。
  *Weld all field parts.*
	- 密切遵循圖面與銲接作業程序書 (WPS) 上之銲接細節或型式。
	  *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.*
	- 所有外部銲縫應為連續銲，外部不允許使用間斷銲（跳銲）。
	  *All external welds shall be continuous, no stitch welds on the outside allowed.*
	- 依據適用圖面上之型式範例，安裝所有現場安裝組件。
	  *Install all field parts according the typical on the applicable drawings.*

##### 品質管制 *Quality control*
- 依據施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 與/或程序書完成品質管制工項。
  *Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).*
- 銲接前檢查現場安裝組件之對合組對。
  *Check the fit-up of field parts before welding.*
- 釋出並隨帶未完成事項清單。
  *Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).*

#### 13.2.8. 可調式法蘭連接結構 *Adjustable flange connection*

熱回收鍋爐 (HRSG) 進口煙道使用膨脹接頭與氣渦輪機煙道相連。熱回收鍋爐側之此膨脹接頭法蘭連接結構設計為可調節式，以補償安裝與製造之公差。
*The HRSG inlet duct is connected to the gas turbine duct using a compensator. The flange connection for this compensator on the HRSG side is made adjustable in order to compensate for erection and fabrication tolerances.*
在開始安裝可調式法蘭連接結構之前，需提前準備一些工項。
*Before erection of the adjustable flange connection can start, some activities need to be prepared in advance.*

##### 準備工作與先決條件 *Preparations and preconditions*
- 前述段落中提到之文件與程序需已就緒，並由權責方審查完畢。
  *The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).*
- 下列準備工作 / 工項需已完成，且在對應之施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 中視適用情況進行簽認。
  *The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.*
	- 進口煙道壁板與現場安裝組件完成安裝。
	  *Inlet duct panels and field parts erected.*
	- 材料已收訖，並對數量與品質進行檢驗（填寫溢裝、短裝與損壞報告，即 OSD 報告）。
	  *Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report)*

##### 釋出後續工項 *Release subsequent activities*
- 隨著本段落工項之成功完成，即可釋出以下工項：
  *With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given:*
	- 內部保溫施作。
	  *Internal insulation.*

##### 一般說明 *General*
- 該法蘭連接結構之設計允許在縱向與垂直方向上進行修正 / 調整。
  *The flange connection is designed for correction/adjustment in the longitudinal and vertical direction.*
- 該法蘭由以下物件組合而成：
  *The flange is built-up from :*
	- 連接於底部、側部與頂部煙道壁板之「內端板（縱向風道端板）」。
	  *An “In head plate” connected to the bottom, side and top ducting.*
	- 外部護罩板。
	  *An outside shell plate*
	- 一個外部用之扁鐵環。
	  *A ring for the outside*
- 有關可調式法蘭連接結構之架構，請參照相關圖面。
  *For an overview of the adjustable flange connection, see the applicable drawings.*

##### 安裝 *Erection*
- 安裝端板（垂直煙道板）。
  *Erect the head plate (vertical ducting plate).*
- 在端板與外部護罩板上安裝外圈扁鐵。
  *Erect the outside ring on the head plate and outside shell.*
- 組對並點銲已裝設之法蘭。
  *Fit and tack-weld the installed flange.*
	- 在氣渦輪機可調法蘭與熱回收鍋爐側之連接法蘭之間，裝設定位間心塊（定位墊塊代表膨脹接頭之安裝淨寬度）。
	  *Use distance holders between the adjustable flange of the gas turbine and connection flange on the HRSG side. (Distance holder to represent the width of the expansion joint).*
	- 安裝定位間心墊塊期間，保持連接法蘭與可調法蘭之「法蘭」螺栓孔互相比對一致。
	  *During erection of the distance holders keep the bolt holes for the “flange” on the connection and adjustable flange equal to each other.*

##### 銲接 *Welding*
- 銲接可調式法蘭連接結構。
  *Weld the adjustable flange connection.*
	- 切勿拆除定位間心墊塊，此些定位墊塊應於後續裝設膨脹接頭連接時拆除。
	  *DO NOT REMOVE the distance holders.These will be removed during installation of the expansion joint connection.*
	- 遵循圖面上的銲接地圖與銲接作業程序書 (WPS) 之要求。
	  *Follow the requirements of the weld typical on the drawings and WPS.*

##### 品質管制 *Quality control*
- 依據施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 與/或程序書完成品質管制工項。
  *Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).*
- 銲接前檢查組對裝配與尺寸。
  *Check the fit-up and dimensions before welding.*
- 釋出並隨帶未完成事項清單。
  *Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).*
- 製造商負責人應審查法蘭連接線之實際尺寸測繪報告，以確保其位置與高程符合適用之公差圖面（60031-730-06 系列）所規定之公差。
  *Manufacturer shall review the actual survey report of the flange connection for, location and elevations according the applicable tolerance drawings 60031-730-06-series.*

#### 13.2.9. 內部保溫 *Internal Insulation*

內部保溫與內襯護板之安裝應依據本手冊之「內部保溫」章節進行。施工期間應遵循該章節提到之安裝與品質步驟。
*Erection for the internal insulation and liner sheeting is based on the Chapter “Internal insulation”. Follow the installation and quality steps mentioned in this chapter during execution.*

### 13.3. 進口煙道最終檢查 *Final inspection of the inlet duct*

當特定系統或一組特定組件之機械安裝完成後，應進行檢查。未完成項目應彙整於未決點清單內，並檢附於最終檢查合格證書上。
*When the mechanical erection of a certain system, or group of specific components is finalized these shall be inspected. Outstanding items shall be collected in an outstanding items list and attached to the Final inspection Certificate.*

鍋爐本體分部之最終檢查主要涵蓋了鍋爐外殼，因為所有其他鍋爐部件皆有其獨立單獨之最終檢查。
*Final inspection for the boiler part is mainly covered by the boiler casing, because all other boiler parts have a separate final inspection round.*
進口煙道之最終檢查合格證書中描述了所檢查之系統或組件。
*The Final inspection Certificate of the inlet duct describes the systems or components inspected.*

##### 檢查 *Inspection*
- 最終檢查合格證書中所提及之所有系統或特定組件組，應針對正確安裝、完整性與損壞進行最終檢查。
  *All systems or group of specific components referred to on the Final inspection Certificate shall have a final inspection for correct erection, completeness and damages.*
- 完成現場步行檢查後，應立即建立未完成項目 / 未決點紀錄（如有）。
  *A record of outstanding items (if any) shall be set-up directly after the walk-down.*
- 若有施作未完成項目清單，其應分類為：
  *In case a list of outstanding items is applicable it shall be categorized in :*
	- 水壓試驗前應解決之項目（A 級項目）。
	  *Items to be solved before hydro testing (A-items)*
	- 熱試運轉前應解決之項目（B 級項目）。
	  *Items to be solved before hot-commissioning (B-items)*
	- 初期驗收 (PAC) 前應解決之項目（C 級項目）。
	  *Items to be solved before provisional acceptance (PAC) (C-items)*

確認所涉及系統之適用現場安裝品質計畫書 (FQP) 已由所有權責方簽字認可。未完成項目應納入未決點清單。
*Verify that the applicable site FQPs for the systems involved are signed off by all parties involved. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list.*
確認所有不符合事項報告 (NCR) 已關閉。未完成項目應納入未決點清單。
*Verify that all Non-Conformity Reports are closed. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list.*

## 14. 次鋼構 *SECONDARY STEEL*

本章包含以下段落：
*This chapter contains the following paragraphs:*

1. 一般說明：第 14.1 節
   *General : paragraph 14.1*
2. 文件與程序：第 14.2 節
   *Documents and procedures : paragraph 14.2*
3. 次鋼構與吊掛型鋼安裝：第 14.3 節
   *Secondary steel (and hoisting beam erection) : paragraph 14.3*
4. 次鋼構灌漿：第 14.4 節
   *Grouting secondary steel : paragraph 14.4*
5. 次鋼構與吊掛型鋼之最終檢查：第 14.5 節
   *Final inspection of secondary steel and hoisting beams : paragraph 14.5*

### 14.1. 一般說明 *General*

此處所述之次鋼構組件安裝係採一般性設定，適用於所有次鋼構安裝工作。
*The described erection for secondary steel components is set-up generally and applies for all secondary steel erection works.*
次鋼構安裝之特定要求，或有提及時，應參照相關章節或段落。
*Specific requirements as a part of the erection for secondary steel are mentioned in the relevant chapter or paragraph (if any).*
在熱回收鍋爐安裝期間，將次鋼構之安裝與管道（支架）系統以及施工架搭設相結合是極為重要的。
*During erection of the HRSG it is important to combine the installation of secondary steel with the piping (supports) systems and scaffolding erection.*
在專案早期階段，應與現場相關各方討論並協調次鋼構、管道及施工架之安裝，以形成並達成良好之安裝計畫。
*Discuss and coordinate the erection of secondary steel, piping and scaffolding with the relevant parties on site in order to form and achieve a good plan for erection, in an early stage of the project.*
製造商之建議是在可行之情況下，於安裝次鋼構之前先安裝管道（支架）系統。在某些情況下，管道支架為次鋼構之一部分。
*Manufactures advice is to erect the piping (supports) systems before erection of the secondary steel, where possible. In some cases piping supports are part of the secondary steel.*
次鋼構之安裝順序示於文件 60031-730-05-001。
*The erection sequence for secondary steel is shown in document 60031-730-05-001.*

### 14.2. 文件與程序 *Documents and procedures*

- 安裝次鋼構（與吊掛型鋼）所需之文件與程序。
  *Documents and procedures required for installation of the secondary steel (and hoisting beams.)*
	- 施工方法說明書：安裝次鋼構。
	  *Work method statement : Erection secondary steel*
	- 施工方法說明書：次鋼構施工架搭設。
	  *Work method statement : Scaffolding secondary steel*
	- 施工品質計畫書：熱回收鍋爐次鋼構。
	  *FQP : HRSG secondary steel*
	- 螺栓緊固程序書：非受壓組件。
	  *Bolt torque procedure : Non-pressure parts*
	- 銲接作業程序書 / 銲接程序資格檢定紀錄 / 銲工資格檢定：非受壓組件。
	  *WPS / PQR / WPQ : Non-pressure parts*
	- 銲接地圖 / 紀錄：非受壓組件。
	  *Weld typical / record : Non-pressure parts*
	- 銲接耗材處理程序書：非受壓組件。
	  *Welding consumable handling procedure : Non-pressure parts*
	- 非破壞檢測程序書 / 人員資格認證：非受壓組件。
	  *NDE procedures / personnel qualifications : Non-pressure parts*

### 14.3. 次鋼構（與吊掛型鋼）安裝 *Secondary steel and hoisting beam erection*

次鋼構與吊掛型鋼應作為預組裝組件或散件進行安裝。
*Erection of secondary steel and hoisting beams as pre-assembled or loose components.*
在次鋼構開始安裝前，一些工項必須提前準備。
*Before erection of the secondary steel can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance.*

##### 準備工作與先決條件 *Preparations and preconditions*
- 前述段落中提到之文件與程序需已就緒，並由權責方審查完畢。
  *The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).*
- 下列準備工作 / 工項需已完成，且在對應之施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 中視適用情況進行簽認。
  *The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.*
	- 材料已收訖，並對數量與品質進行檢驗（填寫溢裝、短裝與損壞報告，即 OSD 報告）。
	  *Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report)*

##### 釋出後續工項 *Release subsequent activities*
- 隨著本段落工項之成功完成，即可釋出以下工項：
  *With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given:*
	- 二次灌漿（適用之處）。
	  *Grouting (where applicable)*

##### 安裝 *Erection*
- 安裝預組裝組件或散件。
  *Erect the pre-assembled components or loose parts.*
- 依據件號圖安裝散件，如柱、樑、斜撐、鋼梯、扶手與格柵板。
  *Erect loose parts like, columns, beams, bracings, stairs, handrail and grating according the piece mark drawings.*
	- 在地表放置垂直鋼結構之前，先在底座鋼板下方安裝調整墊片，並調整至正確之高程。
	  *Erect the shims (under the base plates) before placement of the vertical steel structure at ground level and level to the correct elevation.*
	- 在起吊前，確認扶手與格柵板皆已緊固且無鬆動。
	  *Before lifting verify that hand railing and grating is not loose, but all tightened.*
	- 用於柱整平之調整墊片必須位於底座鋼板下方，且不得突出。
	  *Shims used for levelling of the columns shall be under the base plate and not protrude.*
	- 依據施工方法說明書進行次鋼構組件之緊固。
	  *Tightening of secondary steel parts to take place according the work method statement.*
	- 在預組裝期間，檢查次鋼構上之件號標記是否正確。
	  *During pre-assembly check the piece marks on the secondary steel for correctness.*
	- 在預組裝期間，檢查鋼柱與鋼樑之位置與對正。
	  *During pre-assembly check position and alignment of the columns and beams.*
	- 安裝應分成便於管理的組件進行，以便於在安裝期間仍易於操控。在適當且可行之情況下，應包含鋼梯、平台、扶手與格柵板。
	  *Erection to be executed in manageable components which are still easily manipulated during erection. Where required and possible, include stairs, platforms, hand railing and gratings.*
	- 對於螺栓緊固，施加正確之扭矩值。
	  *Apply the correct torque value for bolt tightening.*
	- 螺栓連接不允許有銜接，除非圖面另有標示。
	  *Splices in bolted connections are not permitted, except as shown on drawing.*
	- 依據適用之螺栓清單，使用正確之螺栓材質與長度。
	  *Use the correct bolt material and length, according the applicable bolt list.*
	- 當偵測到螺栓孔錯位不對準時，必須與製造商討論後始得進行調整。
	  *When a misalignment of bolt holes is detected, adjustment can be made only after consultation with the manufacturer.*
	- 將格柵板安裝至平台框架時，確認承載條之跨距方向。
	  *Verify span direction of bearing bars when installing grating into the platform frames.*
	- 依據適用之油漆程序進行面漆補漆。
	  *Touch up painting according applicable painting procedure.*
	- 嚴格遵循圖面上之一般註記與銲接細節（如有）。
	  *Strictly follow the general notes and welding details on the drawings (if any).*
	- 嚴禁使用割炬調整孔徑。
	  *Adjustment of holes with cutting torches is prohibited.*
	- 嚴禁銲接臨時裝置。
	  *Welding of temporary devices is prohibited.*
- 節點偏差調整（如有）
  *Deviations on branch points (if any)*
	- 連接鋼樑過短：
	  *Connection beam to short:*
		- 容許之最大偏差為 -5mm 以內，且必須使用調整墊片進行補償。
		  *Maximum deviations up to - 5mm and must be compensated with shims.*
		- 僅允許使用一片符合實際間隙之調整墊片。若偏差超過 5 mm，則兩側均須使用調整墊片。
		  *Only one shim fitting the actual gap is permitted. If a deviation is over 5 mm, shims must be used on both sides.*
	- 連接鋼樑過長：
	  *Connection beam too long:*
		- 若連接鋼樑過長，必須將法蘭板切割下來，移除後將鋼樑長度修正至所需長度，再重新將法蘭板銲接上去。
		  *In case the connection beam is too long the flange plate must be cut off, after removal the length of the beam can be corrected to the required length and the flange plate welded on again.*
	- 法蘭板變形：
	  *Flange plate is distorted:*
		- 若法蘭發生變形，必須將法蘭板切割下來，修正後再重新銲接上去。
		  *If the flange is distorted, the flange plate must be cut off, corrected and welded on again.*
	- 法蘭板之間隙與平面度：
	  *Gap and flatness of the flange plates:*
		- 若對應間隙大於 5 mm 或法蘭角度不正確，必須將法蘭板切割下來，修正後再重新銲接上去。
		  *If respective gap is bigger than 5 mm or the angle of the flange is incorrect, the flange must be cut off, corrected and welded on again.*
- 次鋼構組件之銲接。
  *Welding of secondary steel components.*
	- 銲接時遵循圖面與銲接作業程序書 (WPS) 上之細節或型式示範。
	  *For welding follow the details and typical on the drawings and WPS.*

##### 品質管制 *Quality control*
- 依據適用之施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 與/或程序書進行品質管制工項。
  *Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).*
- 銲接前檢查組對（如有）。
  *Check fit-up before welding (if any).*
- 檢查螺栓連接之螺栓扭矩。
  *Check torque of bolted connections*
- 釋出並隨帶未完成事項清單。
  *Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).*

### 14.4. 次鋼構二次灌漿 *Grouting secondary steel*

次鋼構組件之二次灌漿係依據本手冊第 7.2 節「無收縮水泥灌漿」進行。施工期間應遵循該章節提到之安裝與品質步驟。
*Grouting for secondary steel parts is based on the Chapter 7.2 “Grouting” in this manual. Follow the installation and quality steps mentioned in this chapter during execution.*

### 14.5. 次鋼構與吊掛型鋼之最終檢查 *Final inspection of secondary steel and hoisting beams*

當特定系統或一組特定組件之機械安裝完成後，應進行檢查。未完成項目應彙整於未決點清單內，並檢附於最終檢查合格證書上。
*When the mechanical erection of a certain system, or group of specific components is finalized these shall be inspected. Outstanding items shall be collected in an outstanding items list. The outstanding items list can be attached to a Final Inspection Certificate.*
此證書作為妥善完成組裝工項之紀錄。
*Such certificate serves as a record for proper completion of the erection activities.*
次鋼構之最終檢查合格證書中描述了所檢查之系統或組件。
*The Final Inspection Certificate for secondary steel describes the systems or components inspected.*
藉由簽署最終檢查合格證書，所涉及之各方確認所指之系統或組件已達到足夠先進之安裝階段，得以識別出系統移交給試運轉前之剩餘要點；或在無此項目之情況下，直接將系統移交給試運轉。
*By signing the Final Inspection Certificate the parties involved confirm that the system or components referred to are in a sufficiently advanced stage of installation to either identify the points remaining before the system can be handed over to Commissioning, or in absence of any of such points hand over the system to Commissioning directly.*

##### 檢查 *Inspection*
- 最終檢查合格證書中所提及之所有系統或特定組件組，應針對正確安裝、完整性與損壞進行最終檢查。
  *All systems or group of specific components referred to on the Final inspection Certificate shall have a final inspection for correct installation, completeness and damages.*
- 完成現場步行檢查後，應立即建立未完成項目 / 未決點紀錄（如有）。
  *A record of outstanding items (if any) shall be set-up directly after the walk-down.*
- 若有施作未完成項目清單，其應分類為：
  *In case a list of outstanding items is applicable it shall be categorized in:*
	- 水壓試驗前應解決之項目（A 級項目）。
	  *Items to be solved before hydro testing. (A-items)*
	- 試運轉前應解決之項目（B 級項目）。
	  *Items to be solved before commissioning. (B-items)*
	- 初期驗收 (PAC) 前應解決之項目（C 級項目）。
	  *Items to be solved before provisional acceptance. (C-items)*

確認所涉及系統之適用施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 已由所有權責方簽字認可。未完成項目應納入未決點清單。
*Verify that the applicable site FQPs for the systems involved are signed off by all parties involved. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list.*
確認所有不符合事項報告 (NCR) 已關閉。未完成項目應納入未決點清單。
*Verify that all Non-Conformity Reports (NCR’s) are closed. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list.*

## 15. 配管 *PIPING*

本章包含以下段落：
*This chapter contains the following paragraphs:*

1. 一般說明：第 15.1 節
   *General : paragraph 15.1*
2. 文件與程序：第 15.2 節
   *Documents and procedure : paragraph 15.2*
3. 大管徑管路：第 15.3 節
   *Large bore piping : paragraph 15.3*
4. 小管徑管路：第 15.4 節
   *Small bore piping : paragraph 15.4*
5. 配管支撐灌漿：第 15.5 節
   *Grouting pipe supports : paragraph 15.5*
6. 各系統配管之最終檢查：第 15.6 節
   *Final inspection of piping per system : paragraph 15.6*

### 15.1. 一般說明 *General*

管路（預製管段）之安裝係依據熱回收鍋爐（HRSG）受壓組件安裝之適用施工規範與專案規範之要求進行。
*Piping (spools) erection is based on the requirements by the applicable construction code and project specifications for the pressure parts erection of the HRSG.*
所有於現場執行之工作皆應具備一流之品質與良好之工藝。安裝承包商應遵守所有適用之要求與法規，並確保工作之執行符合當地法律與規章。
*All work executed on site shall be of first class and good workmanship. The erection contractor shall adhere to all requirements and regulations applicable and ensure that work execution complies with local law and regulations.*
91/92 級鋼材之銲接為品質敏感性工項。必須遵循以下製造商關於 91/92 級鋼材銲接之規範：「IKZ09-909-14 91 級材料之製造與供應說明書」，如文件 60031-409-10 所示。未遵循正確之程序與要求可能導致品質問題。
*Welding of grade 91/92 is a quality sensitive activity. The following Manufacturer specification for welding of grade 91/92 materials has to be followed: “IKZ09-909-14 Instruction for fabrication and supply of grade 91 materials”, as attached in document 60031-409-10. Not following the right procedures and requirements might lead to quality issues.*
對於管路安裝，遵循現場安裝標準規範中提到之要求至關重要。此規範之部分主題已於安裝註記或段落中進行強調。
*For the piping erection it is important to follow the requirements as mentioned in the standard specification site installation. Some topics of this specification are emphasized in the notes for installation or the paragraphs.*
強烈建議針對外部管路，按箱體（頂部與底部）及按水壓試驗系統安裝大管徑管路與小管徑管路。
*It is a strong recommendation to erect the large bore piping and small bore piping per box (top and bottom) and per hydro testing system for the external piping.*
為了能夠啟動箱體之其餘安裝工項，如擋板、密封板與機械完工步行巡檢，完成每個箱體之管路安裝十分重要。
*In order to enable initiation of the remaining erection activities for a box, like baffles, sealing plates and mechanical completion walk downs, it is important to finish the erection of the piping per box.*
註：對於受壓組件安裝之重要事項：
*Note: Important for the erection of the pressure parts:*
- 進場材料之管制應依據材料接收報告 (MRR) 及溢短損 (OSD) 報告進行記錄（如有）。
  *Control of incoming materials to be recorded according the MRR with OSD (if any).*
- 使用 HTT 等角圖圖例標準作為管路安裝之資訊。
  *Use the HTT isometric legend standard as information for piping erection.*
- 依據適用之規範與專案特定要求執行非破壞檢測 (NDE) 工作。
  *Execute NDE works as per applicable code and project specific requirements.*
- 對於配管對接接頭、支管及管嘴連接在使用記錄熱電偶之局部熱處理，應遵循適用施工規範與專案規範中給出之圖示。安裝承包商應編寫用於桶槽 / 鞍座安裝之包含吊裝計畫之施工方法說明書 / 風險評估。管路之安裝順序示於文件 60031-730-05-001。
  *For local heat treatment of piping butt joints, branch and nozzle connections with recording thermocouples, follow the figures as given in the applicable construction code and project specifications.Work method statements / risk assessments with lifting plans for the installation of tanks / skids shall be prepared by the erection contractor. The erection sequence for piping is shown in document 60031-730-05-001.*

### 15.2. 文件與程序 *Documents and procedures*

- 安裝管路所需之文件與程序。
  *Documents and procedures required for installation of piping.*

	- 施工方法說明書：管路安裝
	  *Work method statement : Erection piping*
	- 施工品質計畫書：熱回收鍋爐管路
	  *FQP : HRSG Piping*
	- 螺栓緊固程序書：受壓組件
	  *Bolt torque procedure : Pressure parts*
	- 銲接作業程序書 / 銲接程序資格檢定紀錄 / 銲工資格檢定：受壓組件
	  *WPS / PQR / WPQ : Pressure parts*
	- 材料現場標識移植檢驗程序清單：受壓組件
	  *LISL’s : Pressure parts*
	- 非破壞檢測程序書 / 人員資格認證：受壓組件
	  *NDE procedures / personnel qualifications : Pressure parts*
	- 銲後熱處理程序書：受壓組件
	  *PWHT procedure : Pressure parts*
	- 硬度檢測程序書：受壓組件
	  *Hardness testing procedure : Pressure parts*
	- 銲接耗材處理程序書：受壓組件
	  *Welding consumable handling procedure : Pressure parts*
	- 銲工資格確認程序書：受壓組件
	  *Welder qualification procedure : Pressure parts*
	- 材料重新鋼印移植程序書：受壓組件
	  *Re-stamping materials procedure : Pressure parts*
	- 材料清潔度程序書：受壓組件
	  *Material cleanness procedure : Pressure parts*
	- 銲接作業程序書 / 銲接程序資格檢定紀錄 / 銲工資格檢定：非受壓組件
	  *WPS / PQR / WPQ : Non-pressure parts*
	- 銲接地圖 / 紀錄：非受壓組件
	  *Weld typical / record : Non-pressure parts*
	- 銲接耗材處理程序書：非受壓組件
	  *Welding consumable handling procedure : Non-pressure parts*
	- 非破壞檢測程序書 / 人員資格認證：非受壓組件
	  *NDE procedures / personnel qualifications : Non-pressure parts*

### 15.3. 大管徑管路 *Large bore piping*

大管徑管路描述了所有尺寸大於 2 英吋且包含許多管路附件之熱回收鍋爐 (HRSG) 管路。
*Large bore piping describes all HRSG piping, which is over 2” in size and contains a lot of piping accessories.*
大管徑管路附件之一些範例如下：
*Some examples of large bore piping accessories are:*

- 管路支撐架
  *Pipe supports*
- 閥門
  *Valves*
- 測量儀置
  *Measurement devices*
- 蒸汽消音器
  *Steam Silencers*
- 其他等
  *etc.*

#### 15.3.1. 大管徑管路安裝 *Erection large bore piping*

在管路安裝開始之前，需提前做好一些準備工作。
*Before erection of the piping can commence some preparations need to be made in advance.*
##### 準備工作與先決條件 *Preparations and preconditions*
- 前述段落中提到之文件與程序需已就緒，並由權責方審查完畢。
  *The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).*
- 下列準備工作 / 工項需已完成，且在對應之施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 中視適用情況進行簽認。
  *The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.*
	- 材料已收訖，並對數量與品質進行檢驗（填寫 OSD 報告）。
	  *Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report)*
	- 管排 / 汽鼓已安裝完成。
	  *Harps / drums installed*
- 依據用於安裝之配管等角圖，準備好管路、附件、附屬件與管支撐架。
  *Prepare piping, accessories, appendages and pipe supports according the isometrics for the erection.*
- 準備金屬膨脹接頭以供安裝（於管路臨時安裝期間）。
  *Prepare metal expansion bellows for the erection (during temporary erection of piping).*
	- 於管路最終檢查後安裝非金屬（織物）膨脹接頭。
	  *Fabric expansion bellow erection after Final inspection of piping.*
- 安裝鞍座與旋轉設備（如有）。
  *Installation of skids and rotating equipment (if any).*
- 準備次鋼構或施工架以供安裝使用。
  *Prepare secondary steel or scaffolding for the erection.*
- 準備臨時支撐。
  *Prepare temporary supporting.*
- 準備正確之工具與設備。
  *Prepare correct tools and equipment.*
	- 準備安裝所需之所有必要設備與工具。
	  *Prepare all necessary equipment and tools for the erection.*
	- 確認管件（管段）、附件、附屬件與管道支撐之件號、標籤（銘牌）、流向與尺寸是否正確。
	  *Verify piping (spools), accessories, appendages and pipe supports for correct numbering, labelling(nameplates), flow direction and dimensions.*
	- 為了保護銲接區域免受天氣影響，如需要時應對該區域進行防護遮蓋。
	  *In order to protect the weld area from weather influences, cover the area in case required.*
	- 切勿忘記在與管路一同安裝之期間安裝膨脹接頭（僅適用於金屬膨脹接頭或預製之非金屬織物膨脹接頭）。
	  *Do not forget to erect the expansion joints during erection together with the piping(only applicable in case of metallic bellows, or prefabricated fabric bellows).*
	- 同樣地，在安裝管路之前，切勿忘記安裝保溫套（甜甜圈）與穿透部外罩，因為此些物料係以單件形式交付。
	  *Similarly, do not forget to erect the insulation donuts and penetration covers, before piping installation, as these are delivered as 1 piece.*
	- 若配管（管段）有任何偏差，請與製造商聯繫。
	  *In case of any deviation regarding piping (spools) contact the manufacturer.*
##### 釋出後續工項 *Release subsequent activities*
- 隨著本段落工項之成功完成，即可釋出以下工項：
  *With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given:*
	- 水壓試驗。
	  *Hydrotesting.*
	- 安裝織物面料（非金屬）膨脹接頭。
	  *Erection fabric expansion bellows.*
##### 安裝 *Erection*
- 按系統安裝與組對配管及附件。
  *Erect and fit piping with accessories per system.*
	- 外部大管徑管路安裝之起點為系統的「固定點」，如已安裝之主聯箱、管排或桶槽與容器。
	  *Starting points for erection of external large bore piping are system “fixed points”, like already installed main headers, harps or tanks and vessels.*
	- 所有管路附件皆應依據相關供應商之安裝說明進行安裝。
	  *All piping accessories to be installed as per the relevant supplier installation instructions.*
	- 在預組裝期間，管路與管路附件應保持清潔，且無髒污或雜物。在可能之情況下，保持組件接頭戴上保護蓋。
	  *Piping and piping accessories shall be kept clean and free from dirt or debris during pre-assembly. In case possible keep components capped.*
	- 在安裝管路附件（銲接與銲後熱處理）期間，應遵循相關供應商之安裝說明。特別注意安裝期間閥門所需的開啟 / 關閉位置。
	  *During erection (welding and PWHT) of piping accessories follow the relevant supplier installation instructions. Especially focus on the required open/close position of valves during installation.*
	- 任何時候皆應無應力對正法蘭。使用正確之墊片並施加適當之螺栓緊固值。
	  *Align flanges free of stress at all time. Use the correct gasket and apply the appropriate bolt tightening values.*
	- 螺栓連接應使用適當之潤滑劑，並施加如螺栓緊固規範「60031-400-20 法蘭連接螺栓扭矩程序」中所述之扭矩值。
	  *Use the appropriate lubricant for bolted connections and apply torque values as mentioned in the bolt tightening specification “60031-400-20 “Bolt torque procedure flanged connections”.*
	- 在安裝期間確認管路坡度。
	  *Verify piping slope during erection.*
	- 若偏差超出規定的容許公差，請與製造商聯繫。
	  *In case of tolerances deviating more than the allowable tolerances specified, contact the manufacturer.*
	- 將最終支撐架安裝至正確之位置與地點。
	  *Fit the final supports to the correct position and location.*
	- 在需要時，已完工管線之圖面應製作為竣工圖（As-built）。
	  *Drawings of completed lines shall be made as-built, where required.*
- 定位銲組對之品質管制：
  *Quality control on tack-welded fit-ups:*
	- 銲接時遵循圖面 / WPS 上之細節及/或型式示範。
	  *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings / WPS.*
	- 臨時銲接附屬件之化學成分應與永久性材料相容。
	  *Temporary welded attachments shall be of a compatible chemical composition as the permanent material.*
	- 銲接前應檢查組對狀態。
	  *Fit-ups to be checked, before welding.*
- 銲接：
  *Welding:*
	- 銲接時遵循圖面 / WPS 上之細節及/或型式示範。
	  *Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings / WPS.*
	- 在管路附件之銲接與銲後熱處理 (PWHT) 期間，應遵循相關供應商之安裝說明。特別注意安裝期間閥門所需的開啟 / 關閉位置。
	  *During welding and PWHT of piping accessories follow the relevant supplier installation instructions.Especially focus on the required open/close position of valves during installation.*
##### 品質管制 *Quality control*
- 依據適用之施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 與/或程序書進行品質管制工項。
  *Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).*
- 釋出並隨帶未完成事項清單。
  *Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).*
- 安裝承包商應在每個系統配管完工後，繪製竣工管路及儀表圖 (P&ID) 與等角圖 (Isometrics)。
  *Erection contractor to draw-up as-built P&ID’s and isometrics upon piping completion per system.*

### 15.4. 小管徑管路 *Small bore piping*

2 英吋及以下之配管屬於小管徑管路。小管徑管路係以散件形式供應。
*Piping 2 inch and smaller is covered by the categories small bore. Small bore piping is supplied as loose items.*
小管徑管路之路徑需於現場進行最終尺寸檢核。然而，由於熱膨脹要求，等角圖上所示之整體幾何形狀應予維持。現場之實際佈線路徑應與小管徑等角圖上之路徑進行對比確認；允許每個方向有 10% 之偏差（除非等角圖另有規定）。
*Routing of small bore piping is subject to final dimension check at site. However, overall geometry as shown on the isometric shall be maintained due to expansion requirements. Actual routing at site to be verified against the routing on the small bore isometrics; 10% deviation in each direction is allowed (unless otherwise specified on the isometric).*
小管徑管路專案組裝之可能性取決於施工現場之狀況，如預組裝空間、起重機（吊車）之可用性、潛在之重工及安裝位置之通道。如前所述，應與所有相關各方妥善協調哪些部分將進行預組裝。
*Possibilities for pre-assembly of small bore piping depend on the situation at the construction site, like space for pre-assembly, availability of cranes, potential rework and access at the installation location. As mentioned before, properly coordinate which parts will be pre-assembled with all involved parties.*
小管徑管支撐架在等角圖上顯示為型式示範，且除非另有說明，否則與型式小管徑管支撐架文件相關聯。
*Small bore pipe supports are show as typicals on the isometrics and related to typical small bore pipe support documents unless otherwise noted.*

#### 15.4.1. 小管徑管路安裝 *Small bore piping erection*

小管徑管路安裝步驟與要求與「大管徑管路」段落相同。在執行小管徑管路安裝時，遵循該段落所述之安裝與品質步驟。
*Small bore piping installation steps and requirements are equal to and based on the paragraph “Large bore piping” . Follow the installation and quality steps mentioned in that paragraph for installation of small bore piping.*
此外，還應考慮以下小管徑管路之特定要求。
*In addition the following small bore piping specific requirements are to be taken into account.*
##### 安裝 *Installation*
- 按系統安裝與組對配管（管段）及其附件。
  *Erect and fit piping (spools) with accessories per system.*
	- 現場配管之路徑應在現場進行實際確認，以確保有足夠之保溫空間、膨脹空間以及便於小管徑附屬件之操作與足夠之維護空間。手柄與手輪之方向應便於操作員操作。
	  *Routing of field run piping is to be actually verified on site in order to ensure sufficient space for insulation, expansion and convenient operation of small-bore appendages and sufficient space for maintenance. Handles and hand wheels shall be orientated for operator convenience.*
	- 套筒（承插）連接在管路末端與承插座底部之間應留有 2 mm 之間隙。
	  *Socket connections shall have a gap of 2mm between the pipe end and the bottom of the socket.*

### 15.5. 二次灌漿配管支架 *Grouting pipe supports*

配管支撐架之二次灌漿係依據本手冊第 7.2 節「無收縮水泥灌漿」進行。施工期間應遵循該章節提到之安裝與品質步驟。
*Grouting of pipe supports is based on the Chapter 7.2 “Grouting” in this manual. Follow the erection and quality steps mentioned in this chapter during execution.*

### 15.6. 各系統配管之最終檢查 *Final inspection of piping per system*

當特定系統或一組特定組件之機械安裝完成後，應進行檢查。未完成項目應彙整於未決點清單內，且可檢附於機械完工證書上。
*When the mechanical installation of a certain system, or group of specific components is finalized these shall be inspected. Outstanding items shall be collected in an outstanding items list. The outstanding items list can be attached to a Mechanical Completion Certificate.*
此證書作為妥善完成安裝工項之紀錄。
*Such certificate serves as a record for proper completion of the installation activities.*
各系統配管之機械完工證書中描述了所檢查之系統或組件。
*The Mechanical Completion Certificate for piping per system describes the systems or components inspected.*
藉由簽署機械完工證書，所涉及之各方確認所指之系統或組件已達到足夠先進之安裝階段，得以移交給試運轉。
*By signing the Mechanical Completion Certificate the parties involved confirm that the system or components referred to are in a sufficiently advanced stage of installation to hand-over to Commissioning.*
a. 現場步行檢查 (Walk-down)
- 機械完工證書中所提及之所有系統或特定組件組，應針對正確安裝、完整性與損壞進行最終檢查。
  *All systems or group of specific components referred to on the Mechanical Completion Certificate shall have a final inspection for correct installation, completeness and damages.*
- 完成現場步行檢查後，應立即建立未完成項目 / 未決點紀錄（如有）。
  *A record of outstanding items (if any) will be set-up directly after the walk-down.*
- 若有施作未完成項目清單，其應分類為：
  *In case a list of outstanding items is applicable it shall be categorized in:*

	- 水壓試驗前應解決之項目（A 級項目）。
	  *Items to be solved before hydro testing. (A-items)*
	- 試運轉前應解決之項目（B 級項目）。
	  *Items to be solved before commissioning. (B-items)*
	- 初期驗收 (PAC) 前應解決之項目（C 級項目）。
	  *Items to be solved before provisional acceptance. (C-items)*

確認所涉及系統之適用施工品質計畫書 (FQP) 已由所有權責方簽字認可。未完成項目應納入未決點清單。
*Verify that the applicable FQPs for the systems involved are signed off by all parties involved. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list.*
確認所有不符合事項報告 (NCR) 已關閉。未完成項目應納入未決點清單。
